 vedānteṣu vipratipadyante vipaścitaḥ kecid aprāmāṇyam manyante ātmanaḥ pramāṇa antara siddha tve teṣām anuvādaka tvam asiddha tve saṃbandha agrahaṇāt apadārtha tve vākyasya aviṣaya tvāt pravṛtti nivṛtti anupadeśe ca apuruṣa artha tvāt anye tu pratipatti kartavya tā prāmāṇya vyājena aprāmāṇyam eva āhuḥ anye tu karma vidhi virodhāt pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt ca śruta artha parigrahe upacarita arthān manyante tad nirāsa artham ucyate ānandam iti parām ca devatām guṇa abhidhāna lakṣaṇayā stutyā kāya vāc manaḥ prahvatā lakṣaṇayā ca praṇatyā pūjayati prakaraṇa artham ca upakṣipati vipratipatti nirākaraṇa mukhena vedāntānām evaṃbhūte arthe prāmāṇya pratipādanāt yatas bhavati eṣaḥ api prakaraṇa arthaḥ atra kecid ānanda ātmaka tve brahmaṇaḥ ānanda rāgāt mumukṣu pravṛttiḥ syāt rāga nibandhanā ca pravṛttiḥ saṃsāra bījam iti na muktaye syāt śāntasya dāntasya ca ātmani darśanam ucyate na ca ānanda anurāgāt pravartamānaḥ śāntaḥ bhavati tasmāt sakala duḥkha atige brahma tattve duḥkhebhyaḥ udvignaḥ sukhebhyaḥ ca vīta rāgaḥ pravartamānaḥ mucyate ānanda śrutayaḥ ca sakala duḥkha atikramam eva āhuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hi kṣudh duḥkha ādi nivṛttau sukha śabdaḥ sā eva ca sukham iti anye na ca āśma ādau prasaṅgaḥ pratyak vṛtteḥ upalabhyamānāyāḥ sukha tvāt tad viśiṣṭa ātma upalabdheḥ vā tān pratyāha ānandam iti na tāvat duḥkha nivṛttiḥ eva sukham yugapad sukha duḥkhayoḥ darśanāt saṃtāpavataḥ śīta hrade nimagna ardha kāyasya atha sati api animagna ardha kāya duḥkhe itarasya abhāvāt sukham iti kumbhīpāke pacyamānasya naraka antara duḥkha abhāvāt sukhitva prasaṅgaḥ eka indriya dvāra duḥkhasya ca indriya antar dvāra duḥkha abhāvāt itas ca aduḥkhasya api viṣaya viśeṣa saṃparkāt saṃvedya āhlāda utpatteḥ yatra api duḥkha vigamaḥ tatra api na tanmātram eva sukham anna pāna viśeṣa upādānāt duḥkha vigamaḥ hi yaiḥ taiḥ anna pānaiḥ sidhyati na ca sa viśeṣavān yena tad viśeṣāya tad sādhana viśeṣaḥ apekṣyeta sukhe tu atiśayavat tvādi uktā tad sādhana atiśaya apekṣāḥ yad api manyante yadā api na anyat duḥkham nivartyam tadā api kāmasya duḥkha ātmaka tvāt tad nibarhaṇa rūpam sukham tatra api akāmasya viṣaya viśeṣa upabhoge na sukhitā syāt bhavati ca madhya sthaḥ api ramaṇīya viṣaya saṃparke hlādavān syāt etad yatra eva kāmaḥ saḥ eva sukhayati viṣayaḥ na itaraḥ tasmāt kāma nivṛttya eva viṣayāḥ sukhayitāraḥ anyathā yaḥ ekasya sukhaḥ sa sarvasya syāt kāma nivṛttyā tu sukha tve yatra yasya kāmaḥ  abhiruciḥ saḥ eva tasya sukhaḥ iti yujyate tatra akāmasya api viṣaya viśeṣa upabhogāt kāma abhivyaktau tad nivṛttau tad sukhitvam iti tad api asāram yatas viṣaya upabhogāḥ na avaśyam kāma nibarhaṇāḥ uktam hi na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati iti tathā bhoga abhyāsam anu vivardhante rāgāḥ kauśalāni ca indriyāṇām iti viṣaya doṣa darśanāt api ca kāma nivṛttiḥ tatra upabhoga tulyaḥ āhlādaḥ syāt samāne ca prārthita artha lābhe pramoda bhedaḥ na syāt kāma nivṛtteḥ aviśeṣāt syāt etad kāma atireke tad nivṛttau sukha atiśaya abhimānaḥ itaratra anyathā iti tad ca na kāma atirekāt prayasyantam avāptaḥ arthaḥ na tathā prīṇayati yathā prārthitaḥ vinā prayāsāt upanataḥ tathā hi kleśāt avāptaḥ ayam iti na tena tathā prīyate yathānāśaṃsita upanatena kāma abhāva mātre ca sukhe akāmita viṣaya upabhoge na bhoga avasthāyāḥ pūrva apare avasthe bhidyeyātām kāma pradhvaṃse vā para avasthā na bhidyeta bhoga avasthāyām prabuddha adhvasta kāmaḥ eva iti ced pūrvā parayoḥ api dvayoḥ avasthayoḥ tarhi sukhī itaratra duḥkhī iti anubhava viruddham āpadyeta aprāptaḥ ca smaraṇa viparivartī viṣayaḥ kāmasya udbodhakaḥ prāptaḥ nivartakaḥ prāptasya udbodha tve na tatas nivṛttiḥ syāt na ca yatra kāmaḥ tatra sukham manoratha śata arthitasya api upabhogena kasyacid duḥkhi tva darśanāt sukha pūrvakaḥ tu kāmaḥ anubhūta tad bhāve tad darśanāt yā api kācid ananubhūte api jāti viśeṣa bhājām kāma pravṛttiḥ sā api prāc bhavīya anubhava nibandhanā yathā ca kasyacid kvacid kāmaḥ  jāti bheda ādi nimittaḥ tathā kiñcid kasyacid sukham iti na avyavasthāḥ api ca kāma nivṛttya api kecid dūyante tad abhāve viṣaya upabhoga sāmarthya abhāvāt na tarhi nivṛtti kāmāḥ nivṛtti kāmā viṣayam prati tasya kutaścid nimittāt anupabhogya tvāt kim iti tarhi dūyanteḷ anubhūta carasya tad janmanaḥ sukhasya aprāpteḥ yathā pitta ādi upahata indriyāḥ viśiṣṭebhyaḥ anna pānebhyaḥ nivṛtti kāmāḥ tathā eva kāma nivṛttyā tapyante tatra anubhūta cara tad janma āhlāda vicchedāt na anyaḥ hetuḥ tasmāt pratyātma vedanīya sukha pratyākhyānam ayuktam sukha saṅgi jana upacchandanāya tu tatrabhavadbhiḥ varṇitam iti paśyāmaḥ tad evam duḥkha nivṛtteḥ anyat sukham sa ca ānanda śabdasya mukhyaḥ  arthaḥ śabda pramāṇake ca yathāśabdam pratipattiḥ yuktā na ca rāga nibandhanā tatra pravṛttiḥ na hi icchā mātram rāgaḥ avidyā kṣiptam abhūta guṇa abhiniveśam rāgam ācakṣate tattva darśana vaimalyāt tu tattve cetasaḥ prasādaḥ abhiruciḥ abhīcchā na rāga pakṣe vyavasthāpyate yathā saṃsāra asāra tā tattva darśana niṣpannaḥ na udvegaḥ tatas dveṣa pakṣe anyathā sarva duḥkha atige api tattve tad dveṣa nibandhanā pravṛttiḥ iti saṃsāra anubandhaḥ syāt api ca dṛṣṭa para utkarṣa rāgibhyaḥ api indriya jayaḥ upadiśyate sādhana tvena kāma ādi tyāga ātmakaḥ tathā iha api bhaviṣyati katham ca tatra samīhita itara viṣaya abhiṣvaṅga niṣedhaḥḷ sarva niṣedhe apravṛtti darśanāt  tathā uttama sukha rāga āt itarasmāt upanatāt api nivṛttiḥ tathā ca uktam kāma ātma tā na praśastā na ca eva iha asti akāma tā iti syāt etad  ānandaḥ ced brahmaṇi saṃvedyaḥ kartuḥ anyat karma iti dvaita prasaṅgaḥ kartṛ karma bhāvaḥ ca na kriyām karaṇam ca antareṇa yatas tatas  ānandam brahma iti ca na syāt tadvat tayā vyapadeśe advitīyam iti na yujyate asaṃvedane san  api asat kalpaḥ iti vyartham tad saṃkīrtanam puruṣa artha tvāya hi tad saṃkīrtanam asaṃvedyaḥ ca katham puruṣa arthaḥḷ ucyate phalavat kartṛ vat ca idam draṣṭavyam tathā hi pramāṇasya phalam artha antaram anartha antaram vā sarva parīkṣakaiḥ pratijñāyate prajñāyate ca na ca tad asaṃvedyam tad asaṃvedya tve sarva asaṃvedya tva prasaṅgāt tad kṛta tvāt saṃvedya bhāvasya bhāvānām na ca saṃvedyam phala antara anupalabdheḥ anavasthā prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt saṃvedyam ātma prakāśa tvāt asaṃvedyam ca viṣaya vat karma bhāva abhāvāt yathā ca kartari ātmani asaṃvedye saṃvid eva na syāt na hi tadā evam bhavati mayā idam viditam iti na hi ātmā saṃvedyaḥ phale viṣaye ca anusaṃdhātum śakyaḥ ananusaṃdhāne ca sva para saṃvedyayoḥ kaḥ atiśayaḥḷ na ca saṃvedyaḥ karma tve kartuḥ vyatireka prasaṅgāt anātma tva prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt ātma prakāśa tā eva tasya saṃvedya tā tathā brahmaṇaḥ sva ātma prakāśasya ānanda svabhāvaḥ na saṃvedyaḥ karma tva abhāvāt na ca asaṃvedyaḥ sva prakāśa tvāt tad kena kam paśyet ḷ aiti api niṣedhaḥ karma viṣayaḥ tathā hi sarva karma pratyasta maya hetukaḥ eva saḥ ucyate yadā asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt iti anye manyante dvividhā dharmāḥ bhāva rūpāḥ abhāva rūpāḥ ca iti tatra abhāva rūpāḥ na advaitam vighnanti yathā ekam amṛtam ajam iti na hi bheda udaya vyayānām nivṛttiḥ kiñcid vastu yena dvaitam āvahet ānandaḥ ca yadi bhāvaḥ tasya dharmi tve vijñānam dharmaḥ syāt atha vijñānam dharmi rūpam ānandaḥ  dharmaḥ na hi ekasya dve rūpe yujyete virodhāt tatra vijñānam ānandam brahma iti bhāva rūpayoḥ ānanda brahmaṇoḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhedāt advaita vighātaḥ syāt etad dharmaḥ api dharmiṇaḥ na bhinnaḥ bhede gavāśva vat dharma dharmi bhāva anupapatteḥ tad asat abhede api dharmi rūpavat tad anupapatteḥ tasmāt kathañcid bhinnaḥ dharmaḥ tathā ca ātyantika bheda abhāva śrutiḥ ekam eva advitīyam iti na yujyate evam yaḥ api ekasya rūpa dvayam pratipadyate tasmāt vijñāna ātmanaḥ brahmaṇaḥ  duḥkha abhāva upādhiḥ eva ānanda śabdaḥ yathā sthūla abhāva ādi upādhayaḥ asthūlam anaṇva hrasvam aitya ādayaḥ śabdāḥ na ca vijñāna ānandayoḥ eka tvam eva śabda dvaya prayoga vaiyarthyāt katham ca aparyāya śabda abhidheyaḥ eka tvamḷ tasmāt duḥkha uparama eva ānanda śabdasya brahmaṇi arthaḥ iti atra ucyate viśiṣṭasya āhlāda ātmanaḥ prakāśasya cāndramasasya iva śabda dvayena pratipādanāt na doṣaḥ yathā ca prakṛṣṭaḥ prakāśaḥ savitā iti na ca prakṛṣṭa prakāśa śabdayoḥ paryāya tvam atha ca ekaḥ eva abhyām artha viśeṣaḥ pratipādyate prakāśa viśeṣaḥ na hi prakarṣaḥ anyaḥ prakāśa rūpāt savitari na prakāśa rūpaḥ vā prakarṣāt api tu prakāśa bhedaḥ śabda dvaya upāyaḥ pratīyate tathā vijñānam ānandam brahma iti ānanda bhedaḥ vijñāna bhedaḥ vā brahma rūpam iti śabda dvayena avagamyate parama tām api asya kecid sādhana pāratantrya lakṣaṇāyāḥ kṣayitā lakṣaṇāyāḥ ca duḥkha tāyāḥ abhāvāt manyante tad api yathāśabdam pratipatteḥ śabda pramāṇake arthe na anumanyante na hi svarūpataḥ para ma tā saṃbhave virodhi asaṃsargāt upacaritā sā yuktā bhavitum tasmāt ātma prakāśa prakṛṣṭa ātma svabhāvam eva brahma iti yuktam evam ca laukika ānandaḥ etasya mātrā iti yujyate avacchedāt duḥkha nivṛttau tu duryojam etad itas ca ānanda svabhāvaḥ ātmā para prema āspada tvāt śrūyate hi para prema āspada tvam tad etad preyaḥ putrāt iti pratīyate ca tathā hi sarvasya iyam ātma āśīḥ kṛmeḥ api mā na bhūvam bhūyāsam iti sā ca priye avakalpate premā ca sukha ātmani na duḥkhe na ubhaya rūpa rahite dveṣāt upekṣaṇāt ca anye tu suṣupte sukham aham asvāpsama iti parāmarśāt ātmani sukha anubhavam āhuḥ na hi ananubhave parāmarśaḥ evam syāt suṣupta abhyupagamaḥ ca na ca anyathā anubhave sukham iti parāmarśaḥ na ca tatra ātmanaḥ anyat anubhavanīyam asti tathā ca aharahar brahma loka avāptiḥ śrūyate tatra anyaḥ āhuḥ duḥkha uparamāt api tathā parāmarśa siddheḥ na ekāntataḥ sukhitva siddhiḥ tān pratyāhuḥ anyathā abhāve avagate duḥkha uparama nimittaḥ sukha śabdaḥ iti yujyate anyathā mukhya artha tā eva yuktā tatra āhuḥ ubhayathā vyapadeśasya darśanāt upapatteḥ ca na vyapadeśa mātrāt artha siddhiḥ iti alam ati vistareṇa atra kecid bhoga vyavasthānāt mukta saṃsāri vibhāga upapatteḥ ca dṛś śakteḥ ca arthavat tvāt sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt dṛśyena ca draṣṭuḥ anumānāt dṛśyasya ca sukha duḥkha moha bheda vat śabda ādi vibhāga upalabdheḥ ekatva śrutiḥ jāti deśa kāla vibhāga abhāva nimitta upacārāt manyante ātmā eva idam sarvam iti ca tādarthya nimitta upacārāt tān pratyucyate ekam iti indraḥ māyābhiḥ puru rūpaḥ īyate iti vyaktam eva nānā rūpa avagamaḥ  māyā nibandhanaḥ darśitaḥ tatra katham eka tvam upacaritam iti vaktum śakyamḷ tathā vyaktaḥ nānātva niṣedhaḥ na iha nānā asti kiñcana iti nānātva darśana nindā ca mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti iti bheda darśanasya ca abhāvaḥ bheda dṛṣṭiḥ iva bhramāt yaḥ iha nānā iva paśyati iti iva śabdena prakāśitaḥ na upacaritaḥ eka tve avakalpate kāmam upacāra ādaḥ tu eka tvam na tu bhāvikasya nānātvasya nivṛttiḥ sā api upacāreṇa eva ucyate iti ced na prayojana abhāvāt sati nimitte prayojane ca upacāraḥ na ca nānā tva nivṛtti upacāre prayojanam paśyāmaḥ viparyayāt ca abhyudayāya niḥśreyasāya vā nānā tva nivṛttiḥ upacaryeta sā hi sādhya sādhana ādi vibhāgam nivartayantī sarvatra ca ātmā abhimānam āvirbhāvayantī tad virodhinī syāt tathā hi sarvatas nivṛttasya niḥśreyasam iti avisaṃvādaḥ corret tet api saṃvādaḥ edition tathā ekam eva advitīyam aiti avadhāraṇa ādvitīya śabdābhyām tasya eva arthasya punar punar abhidhānāt sarva prakāra bheda nivṛtti para tā śruteḥ lakṣyate abhyāse hi bhūyas tvam arthasya bhavati yathā ahaḥ darśanīyāḥ ahaḥ darśanīyāa iti na nyūna tvam api dūrata eva upacarita tvam yad tu bhoga vyavasthānāt iti tatra ucyate kalpitāt api bhedāt bhoga vyavasthā siddheḥ asāram etad tathā hi ekasmin  api ātmani sarva gate śarīra parimāṇe aṇu parimāṇe vā kalpita bheda nibandhanā bhoga vyavasthā dṛśyate pāde me vedanā śirasi me vedanā iti na hi pādasya śirasaḥ vā vedanayā abhisaṃbandhaḥ ajña tvāt śarīra parimāṇa ātma vādinaḥ api na avayavāḥ eva vedanā bhājaḥ ātmanaḥ tad viraha prasaṅgāt syāt etad aikātmye tadvat eva deha antara bhoga anusandhānam syāt anyat idānīm etad asti tāvat bhoga vyavasthā api ca tatra api na pradeśaḥ pradeśa antara vedanām anusaṃdadhāti tathā iha api na jīvaḥ jīva antara vedanām anusaṃdadhāti iti samānam tathā maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa ādiṣu sukha ādīnām varṇa saṃsthāna bheda vyavasthānam upalabhyate bheda abhāve api evam ca mukta saṃsāri vibhāgaḥ  api upapannaḥ tathā hi ekaḥ api ātmā pradeśaiḥ sukha duḥkha ādibhiḥ yujyamānaḥ tatra baddhaḥ iva itaratra muktaḥ iva ca gamyate yathā malīmase darpaṇa tale malīmasam mukham viśuddhe viśuddham darpaṇa rahitam ca gamyamānam tad upādhi doṣa asaṃpṛktam syāt etad kalpanā pratipattuḥ pratyayasya dharmaḥ na vastu vyavasthāpayitum alam na khalu pratipattuḥ pratyayam anu viparivartante vastūni na ca upacaritāt kāryam upapadyate na hi upacarita agni bhāvaḥ māṇavakaḥ dahati udāhṛtā tu vyavasthā satyam vibhramaḥ hi saḥ atra api vibhrama tvam na daṇḍa vāritam kalpitaḥ api ca ahidaṃśaḥ maraṇa kāryāya kalpate pratisūryakaḥ ca prakāśa kāryāya yad api dṛśyena eva draṣṭuḥ anumānāt draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ bhedaḥ dṛśyasya ca sukha ādi bheda upalabdheḥ nānātvam iti tad api asat na draṣṭarya prakāśe yatas dṛśyasya siddhiḥ asti iti uktam dṛśya bheda upalabdhiḥ ca na asti pramāṇasya anavacchedaka tvāt iti vakṣyate dṛś chakteḥ ca arthavat tvam sva ātma upayogāt na ca sva ātmani vṛtti virodhaḥ pradīpa vat pramāṇa phala vat ca iti uktam api ca ekatvaḥ eva ayam draṣṭṛ dṛśya bhāvaḥ avakalpate draṣṭuḥ eva cit ātmanaḥ tathā tathā vipariṇāmāt vivartanāt vā nānātve tu vivitkasvabhāvayoḥ asaṃsṛṣṭa paraspara svarūpayoḥ asambaddhayoḥ kīdṛśaḥ  draṣṭṛ dṛśya bhāvaḥ na hi cityā saṃsṛṣṭam cetitam iti yujyate ekāntaḥkaraṇa saṃkrāntau  asti eva sambandhaḥ iti ced na citeḥ śuddha tvāt apariṇāmāda pratisaṃkramāt ca dṛśyā buddhiḥ citi sannidheḥ tad chāyayā vivartate iti ced atha kā iyam tad śāyatāḷ atada ātmanaḥ tad avabhāsaḥ na tarhi paramārthataḥ dṛśyam dṛśyate paramārthataḥ ca adṛśyamānam draṣṭṛ vī atiriktam asti iti durbhaṇam yaḥ api manyate dṛśya tayā eva dṛśyam vyavasthāpyate na sambandhena darśanam ca idam aiti parāgrūpa viṣayam sa vaktavyaḥ satyam parāgrūpa viṣayam tattu ekasya eva ātmanaḥ tathā tathā vipariṇāmāt vivartanāt vā darpaṇa talaḥ iva ātmanaḥ tathā hi darpaṇa tala stham ātmānam vibhaktam iva ātmanaḥ pratyeti citeḥ tu vibhaktam asaṃsṛṣṭam tayā ca iti atas iti duravagamam evam ca draṣṭuḥ avyatirekaḥ dṛśyasyāmnāyate ātmani vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti tasmāt suṣṭhu uktam ekam iti kṣaṇika jñāna ātma vādinaḥ tu sa vāsana kleśa samucchedāt jñāna uparama lakṣaṇām eva brahma prāptim āhuḥ tathā ca śrūyate na pretya saṃjñā astia iti anye tu samucchinna sakala vāsana tvāt vidhūta viṣaya ākāra upaplava viśuddha jñāna utpāda lakṣaṇām anādi nidhana tve hi na apaneyam na upaneyam vā kiñcid asti iti tad arthāni śāstrāṇi tad arthāḥ ca pravṛttayaḥ vyarthāḥ syuḥ tathā hi vidyā svabhāvam ced na kiñcid nivartavyam avāptavyam vā syāt avidyāyāḥ abhāvāt vidyāyāḥ ca bhāvāt avidyā svabhāvam ced tasya nitya tve pūrva svabhāva tyāgāt svabhāva antara anāpatteḥ ca evam ubhaya svabhāva tve api vidyāyāḥ prāpta tvāt avidyāyāḥ ca ucchettum aśakya tvāt tān pratyāha amṛtam ajam iti na ca śāstrāṇām mukti arthānām ca pravṛttīnām vaiyarthyam avidyāyāḥ nivartya tvāt sarva pravādeṣu ca anādiḥ api avidyā ucchedya abhyupagamyate na brūmaḥ  anādeḥ na ucchedaḥ iti kim tu nityasya brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvasya atha avidyā na brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ artha antaram brahmaṇaḥ āpadyeta na vā syāt tatra kim nivartyamḷ atha matam agrahaṇam avidyā sā katham artha antaram syātḷ na ca anivartyā sarva pramāṇa vyāpārāṇām agrahaṇa nivṛtti artha tvāt tad api ayuktam tattva agrahaṇa ātmikayā vidyayā nivartyate sā ca nityāḥ brahmaṇi na ca brahmaṇaḥ anyaḥ asti yasya tattva agrahaṇam brahmaṇi prayatnalabhyayā vidyayā nivartyeta brahmaṇi tu yugapad grahaṇa agrahaṇe vipratiṣiddhe avipratiṣedhe vā na kadācid avidyā nivartyeta yasya tu viparyaya grahaṇam avidyā tasya brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ ced sa nityaḥ katham nivartyetaḷ asvabhāvaḥ ced artha antaram āpadyeta kasya ca tad iti vācyam brahmaṇaḥ anyasya abhāvāt brahmaṇaḥ eva iti ced  vipratiṣedhaḥ tasya vidyā svarūpa tvāt avipratiṣedhe vā kena nivṛttiḥḷ atra ucyate na avidyā brahmaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ na artha antaram na atyantam asatī na api satī evam eva iyam avidyā māyā mithyā avabhāsaḥ iti ucyate svabhāvaḥ ced kasyacid anyaḥ ananyaḥ vā parama arthaḥ eva iti na avidyā atyanta asattve kha puṣpa sadṛśī na vyavahāra aṅgam tasmāt anirvacanīyā sarva pravādibhiḥ ca ittham iyam āstheyā tathā hi śūnya vādinā sattve yathārtha darśanam na avidyā kha puṣpa tulya tve na vyavahāra aṅgam vijñāna mātra vādinaḥ api yathāvabhāsam jñāna sadbhāve na artha apahnavaḥ nīla pīta ādeḥ jñeya ākārasya bahis avabhāsān apahnavāt atyanta asattve bahis avabhāsa ayogāt kha puṣpa vat  bāhya artha vādinām api anitya ādiṣu nitya ādi khyātayaḥ rajata ādi vibhrāntayaḥ ca avabhāsamāna rūpa sadbhāve na avidyā tvam aśnu vīran na atyanta asattve tad nibandhanaḥ kaścana vyavahāraḥ syāt syāt etad avabhāsamānam rūpam mā bhūt avabhāsaḥ tu san  ā iva sa ca avidyā iti gīyate na etad sāram avabhāsamāne asati tad avabhāsaḥ api satyataḥ durnirūpaḥ avabhāsa mātram tu syāt tad avabhāsaḥ iti api bhrāntiḥ eva tasmāt na avidyā satī na api asatī iti atas eva ca asyāḥ nivṛttiḥ adṛḍha svabhāvāyāḥ māyā mātra tvāt anyathā svabhāve dṛḍham vyavasthitāyāḥ katham anyathātvam ḷ svabhāva hānāt śūnya tve svayam nivṛtta tvāt evam ca na advaitahānam na nivartanīyasya abhāvaḥ vā yad tu kasya avidyā iti jīvānām iti brūmaḥ nanu na jīvāḥ brahmaṇaḥ bhidyante evam hi āha anena jīvena ātma anupraviśya iti satyam paramārthataḥ kalpanayā tu bhidyante kasya punar kalpanā bhedikāḷ na tāvat brahmaṇaḥ tasya vidyā ātmanaḥ kalpanā śūnyatvāt na api jīvānām kalpanāyāḥ prāk  tad abhāvāt itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt kalpanā adhīnaḥ hi jīva vibhāgaḥ jīva āśrayā kalpanā iti atra kecid āhuḥ vastu siddhau  eva doṣaḥ na asiddham vastu vastu antara niṣpattaye alam na māyā mātre na hi māyāyām kācid anupapattiḥ anupapadyamāna arthā eva hi māyā upapadyamāna artha tve yathārtha bhāvāt na māyā syāt anye tu anādi tvāt ubhayoḥ avidyā jīvayoḥ bīja aṅkura santānayoḥ iva na itaretara āśrayam aprakḷptim āvahati iti varṇayanti tathā ca uktam avidyā upādānava ādibhiḥ anādiḥ aprayojanā ca avidyāa iti tatra anādi tvā anna itaretara āśraya tva doṣaḥ aprayojana tvāt na bheda prapañca sarga prayojana paryanuyoga avakāśaḥ yad eke paryanuyuñjate prayojanam anuddiśya na mandaḥ api pravartate iti tatra parasya brahmaṇaḥ prapañca sarga prayojanam vācyam na tāvat para anugrahaḥ prāk sargāt anugrāhyāṇām abhāvāt duḥkha uttara tvāt ca sargasya na ātma artha krīḍā ādiḥ āpta kāma tvāt iti tasya avidyā nibandhana tve sarge na avakāśaḥ na hi avidyā prayojanam apekṣya pravartate na hi gandharvanagara ādi vibhramāḥ samuddiṣṭa prayojanāḥ bhavanti tathā puruṣasya viśuddhasya na aśuddhā vikṛtiḥ bhavet iti api prayuktam avidyā nibandhane sarga vibhāge api ca kṛtārthānām āpta kāmānām eva krīḍā ādi pravṛttiḥ ullāsāt prārthanā parikṛṣṭa cetasām tu rati virahiṇām anabhimatā eva krīḍā bhavati na ca vaiṣamyanaiḥ ghṛṇya doṣaḥ na hi māyākārasya vividham prapañcam darśayataḥ aṅga sākalya vaikalya vibhāgena rāga dveṣa vibhāgaḥ citrapusta ādi kṛtām vā vikala avikala ādi bhedena citrāṇi tāni tāni kurvatām bālānām ca mṛṇmaya ādibhiḥ pratikṛti bhedaiḥ vicitraiḥ krīḍatām na teṣu kiñcid vaiṣamyam nairghṛṇyam vā karma āśaya anurodhena ca vidadhataḥ vaicitryam na doṣaḥ iti ācāryāḥ na ca anīśvara tva doṣaḥ na hi sevā bheda anurodhena phala bheda pradaḥ prabhuḥ aprabhuḥ bhavati tathā śuddhasya api aśuddhaḥ vikāraḥ na hi prakṛti vikārayoḥ atyantam availakṣaṇyam prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ eva na syāt dravāṇām ca apām karaka ādiḥ kaṭhinaḥ vikāraḥ tathā acetanasya gomayasya cetanaḥ vṛścikaḥ ityādi bahuvidham prakṛti vikāra vailakṣaṇyam utprekṣitavyam iti alam ati prasaṅgena nanu jīvāḥ api brahma tattva avyatirekāt viśuddha svabhāvāḥ tad katham teṣu avidyā vakāśaḥḷ vārtam etad na ca tāvat bimbāt avadātāt pratibimbam kṛpāṇa ādiṣu bhinnam atha ca tatra śyāma tā ādiḥ aśuddhiḥ avakāśam labhate vibhramaḥ saḥ iti ced samānam etad jīvānām api aśuddhiḥ vibhramaḥ anyathā duravāpa eva viśuddhiḥ syāt iti uktam syāt etad kṛpāṇa ādayaḥ mukhe vibhrānti hetavaḥ tathā iha api vibhrama hetuḥ vācyaḥ anādau vibhrame hetu anveṣaṇam asāmpratam iva tathā ca svapna ādi vat avidyāyāḥ pravṛttiḥ tasya kiṅkṛtā iti pratyuktam nanu svābhāvikī ana ādiḥ avidyā nirhetuḥ sā katham ucchidyetaḷ sarva śāstrāṇi eva tāvat naisargikyāḥ avidyāyāḥ ucchedāya prasthitāni api ca pārthivānām aṇūnām śyāma tā anādiḥ pāka jena varṇena nivartyate nanu svābhāvikam api kiñcid vilakṣaṇa pratyaya upanipātāt nivartatām aikātmya vādinaḥ tu anāgantuka arthasya tad abhāvāt kutas nivṛttiḥḷ na khalu ātma svabhāvaḥ eva vidyāḥ avidyā nivartikāḥ avidyāyāḥ tayā saha vṛtteḥ avirodhāt virodhe vā nitya nivṛtteḥ nityam uktam jagat syāt na ca vidyā antaram āgantukam virodhi nivartakam aikātmya vāde vyatiriktasya tasya ayogāt āgantukasya brahma svabhāva tva anupapatteḥ ca tad uktam svābhāvikīm avidyām tu na ucchettum kaścid arhati vilakṣaṇa upapāte hi naśyet svābhāvikam kvacid na tu aikātmya abhyupāyānām hetuḥ asti vilakṣaṇaḥa iti atra ucyate uktam etad jīvānām avidyā kaluṣita tvam na brahmaṇaḥ tad hi sadā viśuddha nitya prakāśam anāgantuka artham anyathā brahma bhūyam gatasya api na avidyā nivarteta tatra anirmokṣaḥ atha brahma eva saṃsarati brahma eva mucyate eka m uktau sarva mukti prasaṅgaḥ yatas bheda darśanena brahma eva saṃsarati abheda darśanena ca mucyate teṣām ca nisarga ja avidyā kaluṣāṇām vilakṣaṇa pratyaya vidyā udayena upapadyate avidyā nivṛttiḥ na hi jīveṣu nisarga jā vidyā asti avidyā eva hi naisargikī tasyāḥ āgantukyā vidyayā pravilayaḥ avyatireke api ca brahmaṇaḥ jīvānām bimba pratibimba vat vidyā avidyā vyavasthā vyākhyātā kena punar upāyena avidyā nivartateḷ śravaṇa manana dhyāna abhyāsaiḥ brahmacarya ādibhiḥ ca sādhana bhedaiḥ śāstra uktaiḥ kathamḷ yaḥ ayam śravaṇa manana pūrvakaḥ dhyāna abhyāsaḥ pratiṣiddha akhila bheda prapañce saḥ eṣa na iti na iti aātmani sa vyaktam eva bheda darśana pratiyogī tad nivartayati sa ca sāmānyena bheda darśanam pravilāpayan  ātmanā api pravilīyate na ca śrotṛ śravaṇa śrotavya ādi vibhāga parihāṇyāḥ vibhāga antara nivṛtti viṣayāḥ śravaṇa ādayaḥ api tu sāmānyena tathā ca tasmin  api pravilīne svacchaḥ pariśuddhaḥ asya ātmā prakāśate yathā rajaḥ samparka kaluṣitam udakam dravya viśeṣa cūrṇa rajaḥ prakṣiptam rajaḥ ntarāṇi saṃharat su ayam api saṃhriyamāṇam su acchām svarūpa avasthām upanayati evam eva śravaṇa ādibhiḥ bheda darśane pravilīyamāne viśeṣa abhāvāt tad gate ca bhede svacche pariśuddhe svarūpe jīvaḥ avatiṣṭhate avidyayā eva tu brahmaṇaḥ jīvaḥ vibhaktaḥ tad nivṛttau brahma svarūpam eva bhavati yathā ghaṭa ādi bhede tad ākāśam pariśuddham parama ākāśam eva bhavati syāt etad katham bhedena eva bhedaḥ pratisaṃhriyateḷ bheda pratipakṣa tvāt yathā rajasā rajaḥ iti uktam vyaktam eva bheda atīta brahmaṇi śravaṇa manana dhyāna abhyāsānām bheda darśana pratipakṣa tvam avidyā anubandhe api yathā payaḥ payaḥ  jarayati svayam ca jīryati yathā ca viṣam viṣa antaram śamayati svayam ca śāmyati yathoktam vidyām ca avidyām ca yaḥ tad veda ubhayam saha avidyayā mṛtyum tīrtvā vidyayā amṛtam aśnute etad uktam bhavati vidyā avidye dve api upāya upeya bhāvāt sahite na avidyām antareṇa vidyā udayaḥ asti sādhyā tarhi tathā ca kṛtaka tvāt anitya tvam atas āha avidyayā mṛtyum iti eṣaḥ arthaḥ na avidyā vidyāyāḥ sādhanam kim tu avidyayā śravaṇa ādi lakṣaṇayā api avidyā eva nivartate mṛtyuḥ iti avidyā eva ucyate tasyām nivṛttāyām vidyā rūpa upalakṣitam amṛtam aśnute svarūpa avasthānam sphaṭika maṇiḥ iva upādhi āśraya nibandhana uparāga tyāgāt antareṇa prayatna antaram vidyā svarūpe avatiṣṭhate iti anyaḥ  arthaḥ na avidyā vidyā rahitā asti tathā hi bheda darśanam api na prakāśa śūnyam tad abhāve na bhedaḥ prakāśeta tasmāt paraḥ eva prakāśaḥ tathā tathā prakāśate yathoktam tam eva bhāntam anubhāti sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti kim tu avidyā anubaddhaḥ yathā uktam sarvam darśanam anyūnam avikalpam vikalpitam iva tu ayam āntaraḥ puruṣaḥ abhimanyate tathā na vidyā aikātmya śravaṇa ādi lakṣaṇā vinā avidyayā śrotṛ śravaṇa ādi vibhāga anubaddha tvāt tatra avidyayā eva vidyā pratyāsannayā vibhāga darśanam avidyām tīrtvā vidyā lakṣaṇe nitye svarūpe avatiṣṭhate pratibimba kaluṣitam iva udakam tad nivṛttau syāt etad aikātmye vibhāgasya asatya tvāt tad adhiṣṭhāna śravaṇa ādayaḥ api asatyāḥ katham kasmaicid kāryāya syuḥḷ asatyāt ca satya pratipattiḥ mithyā eva yathā dhūmaḥ iti mithyā gṛhītāt bāṣpāt iti ucyate na ayam niyamaḥ asatyam na kasmaicid kāryāya bhavati iti bhavati hi māyā prīteḥ bhayasya ca nimittam asatyam ca satya pratipatteḥ yathā rekhā gavayaḥ lipi akṣarāṇi ca syāt etad svarūpeṇa idam satyam na śūnyam aikātmya vādinaḥ tu sva rūpeṇa api upāyānām asatya tā ucyate santu sva rūpeṇa satyāḥ yena tu rūpeṇa pratipādakāḥ tad asatyam kārya upayoga rahitā svarūpa satyat vyarthāḥ api ca abheda darśana upāyāḥ api na sva rūpeṇa mithyā yatas brahmā eva eṣām sva rūpam tatra brahma eva avidyā anubaddham brahma prāpti upāyaḥ yathā rekhā ādayaḥ kakāraḥ ayam gavayaḥ ayam aitya vidyamāna rūpeṇa eva varṇa ādīnām bodhakāḥ yaḥ api manyate na rekhā gavayaḥ gavayatvena gavaya antarāṇām pratipatti hetuḥ na rekhā varṇa tvena kim tu sādṛśyāt etad sadṛśaḥ gavayaḥ iti rekhā ca samayāt īdṛśīm rekhām dṛṣṭvā ayam varṇaḥ smartavyaḥ iti tasya loka virodhaḥ tathā hi bālāḥ hi rekhāsu varṇa tvena eva vyutpādyante loke abhedena ca vyapadeśaḥ ayam gavayaḥ aitya ākhyātuḥ pratipattuḥ ca gavayaḥ ayam mayā dṛṣṭaḥ iti tathā asatyāt pratibimbāt ca adṛṣṭasya pratibimba hetoḥ viśiṣṭa deśa avasthasya anumānam na mṛṣā śabdāt ca nityāt asatya dīrgha ādi vibhāga bhājaḥ artha bheda pratipattiḥ na mithyā tathā mithyā ahi daṃśaḥ maraṇa hetuḥ tatas ca maraṇa mūrcchā ādi anumānam na vitatham kāla ādi bheda yuktāt satya ahi daṃśāt iva yasya eva kṣaṇika jñānam ātmā tasya eva tu upaneya apaneyā sambhavān mokṣa śostrāṇām mukti arthānām ca pravṛttīnām vaiyarthyam kṣaṇikasya svarasena eva nirvāṇāt anādheya atiśaya tvāt ca ekasmin kṣaṇe viśeṣa aviśeṣa vibhāga abhāvāt kṣaṇasya abhedya tvāt yadi matam santatau  upaneyam apaneyam ca samasti iti tad asat kartā bhoktā ca saṃsārī na ca santatiḥ avastu tvāt kartrī bhoktrī vā katham vāsataḥ  mukti bandhauḷ atha matam na atyantam asatī santatiḥ na api satī kalpanayā tu satī tad vimokṣāya śāstrāṇi pravṛttayaḥ ca iti kalpitaḥ tarhi saṃsarati vimucyate ca kalpita viṣayau ca saṃsāra vimokṣau  api kalpi tau  eva tad etad asmābhiḥ ucyamānam kim na bhavataḥ abhimatamḷ uktam etad kalpita viṣayau  eva saṃsāra mokṣau na parasmin parama arthe api ca abhyupagamya api kṣaṇikam vijñānam anādinidhanāyāḥ eva santateḥ mukti saṃsārau  abhyupetau tathā hi santateḥ anādi tvāt saṃsārasya avastu tvāt ca na utpādaḥ na ucchedaḥ avastu tvāt antyakṣaṇa anupapatteḥ ca sa hi antyaḥ kṣaṇaḥ kiñcid kāryam ārabheta vā na vā ārambhe na antyaḥ iti tad abhāva at na ucchedaḥ anārambhe sarva śakti virahāt asat lakṣaṇāt tasya asattvam tasmin  asati sarve api anena eva krameṇa asantaḥ santāninaḥ syuḥ tad abhāve santānaḥ eva na asti kasya ucchedaḥḷ atha ārabhate eva kāryam antyaḥ santāna antare sārvajñe sati hetu phala bhāve katham santāna antaramḷ na hetu phala bhāvāt anyat eka santateḥ vyavasthāpakam na hetu phala bhāva mātrāt eka santati vyavasthāḥ api tu upādāna hetu phala bhāvāt na ca sārvajñasya jñānasya cara makṣaṇaḥ upādānam ālambana pratyayaḥ hi saḥ samanantara pratyayaḥ ca upādānam sva santati patita samanantara pratyaya janyam ca sārvajñam jñānam ālambana pratyayaḥ asya cara makṣaṇaḥ yadi tulya jātīyam upādānam na mukta citta sārvajña jñānayoḥ tulya jātīya tā na asti yaḥ api manyate vilakṣaṇa kārye santati ucchedaḥ iti tasya rūpa jñāna prabandhe viṣaya antara vijñānāt nirvāṇa prasaṅgaḥ katham cit tulya tā āyām anirvāṇam iti alam ati prasaṅgena kecid tu vijñāna guṇam avijñāna svabhāvam ātma tattvam icchantaḥ samutkhāta sakala viśeṣa guṇe svarūpe tasya sthitim brahma prāptim āhuḥ sā hi tasya avasthā deha indriya ādi upādhibhiḥ akṛta avacchedāḥ bṛhatī brahma iti gīyate jñāna svabhāva tve ca sarva gatasya deha indriya nirapekṣasya nitya tvāt jñāna svarūpasya sannihita vividha jñeya bhedasya bṛhattaraḥ saṃsāraḥ syāt atha na vijānāti kiñcid na tarhi jñāna svarūpaḥ sa karmakaḥ hi jānātyarthaḥ na asati karma sambandhe yujyate tān pratyāha vijñānam iti kutas ḷ śrūyate hi satyam jñānam anantam brahma ‘vijñānam ānandam ityādi na ca ukta doṣaḥ yathā dāhakaḥ api vahniḥ upanītam dāhyam dahati na anupanītam adāhyam ca yathā ca sphaṭika darpaṇa ādayaḥ su acchāḥ prakāśa svabhāvāḥ api yad eva upanidhīyate yogyam ca tad chāyā āpattyā tad eva darśayanti evam ayam puruṣaḥ  bhoga āyatana śarīra sthaḥ bhoga sādhana indriya upanītān śabda ādīn bhuṅkte tad chāyā āpattyā nitya caitanyaḥ api atas ca na sarvasya sarva darśi tva prasaṅgaḥ na ca muktau bāhya viṣaya upabhogaḥ syāt etad sarva gatasya sarvam eva viṣaya tvena vartate tatra kim upaneyam ḷ ucyate yasya api ajñasya ātmanaḥ jñānam manaḥ saṃyoga ādi janyam tasya api sarva manobhiḥ sarva ātmanām saṃyogāt katham upabhoga vyavasthāḷ manaḥ saṃyoga mukhena sarve hi tad viṣayāḥ viṣaya tve asya vartante atha asya karma nibandhana tvāt upabhogasya karma nimittā vyavasthā sā citi rūpa ātma vādinaḥ api na daṇḍa vāritā api ca asya abheda darśana pariniṣpattyā sarvasmin  ātma bhāvam āpanne dṛśya abhāvāt eva na darśanam dṛś svabhāvasya api dagdhuḥ iva vahneḥ dāhya abhāvāt na dāhaḥ prakāśasya iva ca prakāśya abhāvāt na prakāśaka tā tad uktam na hi draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ vidyate avināśi tvāt na tu tad dvitīyam asti tatas anyat vibhaktam yad paśyet yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt ityādi vijñāna ādi viśeṣa guṇa nivṛtti lakṣaṇā ca muktiḥ uccheda pakṣāt na bhidyate na hi sataḥ api ātyantikaḥ  darśana abhāvaḥ abhāvāt viśiṣyate kaḥ ca sarvatas preyasaḥ ātmanaḥ abhāvam abhikāṅkṣeditya puruṣa arthaḥ mokṣaḥ syāt syāt etad  vividha duḥkha upaśama tvāt ātma ucchedaḥ api puruṣeṇa arthyate dṛśyante hi tīvra pāpa roga grastāḥ sva ucchedāya yatamānāḥ satyam pravṛddha gada unmūlita nikhila sukhāḥ duḥkha mayīm iva mūrtim udvahantaḥ na tu evam saṃsāriṇaḥ vividha vicitra deva ādi ānanda bhāginaḥ tatra yathā vividha duḥkha uparama tvāt puruṣa artha tvam tathā vividha sukha uparama tvāt apuruṣa artha tvam api yasya tu nirmṛṣṭa nikhila duḥkha anuṣaṅgā parama ānanda saṃvedanā avasthā tasya eva aikāntikam puruṣa artha tvam iti alam ati prasaṅgena akṣaram iti śabda ātma tām āha viśeṣeṇa sāmānyasya lakṣaṇāt apariṇāmi tvam vā pariṇāme pūrva dharma nivṛtteḥ kṣaraṇasya bhāvāt tad vyudāsena katham tāvat śabda ātma tāḷ param ca aparam ca brahma yadā uṅkāraḥ aitya ādi śrutibhyaḥ na ca idam abhidheya apekṣam kāra pratyaya antasya śabda svarūpa paratvāt avarṇāt api varṇa samudāyāt paraḥ kāra pratyayaḥ dṛśyate eva kāraḥ kimarthaḥḷ ‘kimarthaḥ cakāraḥḷ iti nanu idam anyathā eva vyācakṣate sarva viśeṣa atigasya brahmaṇaḥ upāsitum aśakyatvāt pratīkā upadeśaḥ ayam asmin  ālambane brahma upāsitavyam yathā devatāyāḥ sākṣāt pūjā sambhavāt tad lāñchane dāruṇī aśmani vā pūjā vidhānam tad buddhyā tathā dhyātā devatā sā prasīdati iti anena vā abhidhānena tad dhyeyam praṇavasya tad abhidhāna tvāt ucyate om iti ātmānam dhyāyatha ‘om iti yuñjīta aiti yatra yoga aṅga tā śrūyate tatra evam darśayitvā vāc rūpa atyāgāt ca rūpa prapañcasya oṅkāraḥ eva idam sarvam aiti upasaṃharati yatra api etena eva param puruṣam abhidhyāyīta iti śravaṇam tad api sarva ātma bhāva pratipādana pūrvakam na ca sarva ātma bhāvaḥ aupacārikaḥ stuti arthaḥ iti yuktam mukhya artha tve api avirodhāt sarvasya hi pratyakṣa ādi anavaseyam śāstra gamyam idam rūpam na viruddhyate na hi pramāṇa antareṇa anavagamaḥ pramāṇa antarasya viṣayam apaharati tasmāt vidvān iti ca sārvātma vidaḥ eva tena dhyāna upadeśaḥ na ca tad anyatas tasmāt anantaram eva vākyam tatra paryavasitam tatas adhigata sārvātmyasya sataḥ puruṣaḥ buddhi pūrvam niyoga sāmarthyāt icchayā vā punar pravartate nivartate vai iha tu tattva pratipatti mātrāt niyoga icchā anapekṣasya hetu abhāvāt eva tasya bhaya nivṛttiḥ na ca bhaya nivṛttau puruṣa artha tvāt svayaṃpravṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ niyojyaḥ na api tad upāye tattva pratipattau rajjuḥ na sarpaḥa iti śabdāt eva tad utpatteḥ śabda artha pratipatti uttara kālasya ca vyāpārasya vidhi nibandhana tvāt  tathā dūra deśa vṛttānta ākhyānāni pṛṣṭavatām kutūhalinām autsukya nivṛtti arthāni bhūta artha paryavasitāni na hānāya upādānāya vā yatra api api ca yatra api edition bhūta artha pratipattau hānam upādānam vā saṃbhavati eṣa pratirodha kavān adhvā nidhimān eṣa bhū bhāgaḥa iti tatra api hāna upādānayoḥ śabdaḥ vyāpriyate bhūta artha upakṣayāt śabdāt bhūtam artham pratipadya tasya pramāṇa antara avagatām upakāra hetu tām apakāra hetu tām vā saṃsmṛtya icchayā pravartate dveṣeṇa nivartate vā nanu prayoktā buddhi pūrva kārī śrotuḥ pravṛtti artham nivṛtti artham vā vacanam prayuṅkte tathā ca pravṛtti nivṛtti paryavasitam eva idam hi tatra prayoktavyam na prayujyate na gantavyam anena adhvanāa tathā ‘gṛhāṇa itaḥ nidhim iti na etad sāram bhūta artha paryavasitasya api vacasaḥ  bhūta artha avagama mukhena pravṛtti nivṛtti aṅga bhāvaḥ yatas na vyāhanyate pratyakṣa ādīnām iva bhūta artha pramā pari samāpta vyāpṛtayaḥ pratyakṣa ādayaḥ mātrayā api agocarīkṛta pravṛtti nivṛttayaḥ na pravṛtti nivṛtti aṅga bhāvam jahati tathā śabdaḥ api iti na kiñcid praduṣyati prayoktṛ abhisaṃhite pravṛtti nivṛttī iti ced na prayoktṛ abhisaṃdhānāt śabda artha tvam api tu sāmarthyāt anyathā nidhi prāpti dvārikā nānāvidha puruṣa artha avāptiḥ api tasya abhisaṃhitā iti śabda arthaḥ syāt yadā ca pravṛttim nivṛttim vā abhisaṃdhāya kiñcid pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ jijñāsyate tadā abhisaṃhite api pravṛtti nivṛttī na pratyakṣa ādi prameye tadā abhisaṃhite api pravṛtti nivṛttī na śabda arthau itas ca etad evam itas ca tad evam edition yad kasyacid upādāna buddhiḥ anyasya upekṣā śabda artha tve hi sarveṣām upādāna buddhiḥ eva syāt na ca pravartaka vākya vyavahārāt eva sambandha avagamaḥ yena pravṛtti para ta eva avagamyeta anyathā api darśanāt devadattaḥ kāṣṭhaiḥ sthālyām odanam pacati aitya vyutpanna kāṣṭha śabda arthaḥ vyutpanna itara padārthaḥ vyutpanna vibhakti arthaḥ ca yad pacati arthe karaṇam paśyati tasya kāṣṭha prātipadikā artha tām pratipadyate tathā harṣa viṣāda āśvāsa prayojanebhyaḥ tattva ākhyānebhyaḥ  harṣa ādi nimitteṣu bhavati vyutpattiḥ yathā eva hi pravṛtti viśeṣa darśanāt viśiṣṭa pravṛtti pratyayaḥ tad nimitta pratyayaḥ vā anumīyate hetu antara abhāvāt śabda anantaryāt śabdasya tatra sāmarthyam kalpyate tathā harṣa ādi upalabdheḥ harṣa ādi nimitta pratyaya anumānam śabda anantaryāt ca śabdasya tatra sāmarthya kalpanā pramāṇa antareṇa ca putra janmanaḥ harṣa nimittasya tasya avagata tvāt anyasya abhāvāt  putraḥ te jātaḥ aiti idam vākyam āptena tatra putra janmani prayuktam iti pratipadyate putra janma eva ca asmāt vākyāt anena pratītam iti avadhārayati tad evam prayoga pratyayābhyām asmin  arthe vākyasya sāmarthyam pratipadyate bhavatu vā loke sarva vacasām pravartaka tā tatas ca sambandha avagamaḥ tathā api idam vicāryam kim vidhāyaka pada vyatirekiṇām padānām sva artha mātra para tā āhosvit kārya artha saṃsarga para tā uta padārtha mātra saṃsarga para tā iti tatra sva artha mātra paryavasāne vākya artha pratyaya abhāvaḥ prayoga vaiyarthyam ca syāt tasmāt anya artha vyatiṣaṅga para tā tāvatā prayoga pratyayayoḥ upapattau na viśeṣa vyatiṣaṅge pramāṇam asti yaḥ  hi viśeṣa vyatiṣaṅgam kalpayati kalpayati asau  artha antara vyatiṣaṅgam tathā ca vinā api kāryeṇa padārthānām paraspara saṃsargāt viśiṣṭa bhūta artha pratyaya siddhiḥ avaśyam ca etad evam vijñeyam anyathā loke vivakṣā para tvāt padārtha anvayasya tad abhāvāt vede veda artha pratītiḥ na syāt api ca sarveṣām kārya anvayitve parasparam padārthānām anabhisambandhaḥ tatra na viśiṣṭa padārtha viṣayaḥ niyogaḥ pratīyeta eka padārtha sādhyaḥ eva syāt atha na viniyoga pratyarthī niyogaḥ viśiṣṭa viṣaya tvāt  pūrvaḥ tarhi viniyogaḥ paścāt niyogaḥ kim atas ḷ asti niyoga atirikta artha anvaye api padasya sāmarthyam niyoga anapekṣam ca paraspara anvitānām iyoga anvayāt na ca niyoga ākāṅkṣā nibandhanaḥ saṃsargaḥ iti pratipādayiṣyate anadhigatam api ramāṇa antareṇa anadhigata sambandham ca sva śabdena śakyam śabdena nirūpayitum viśeṣa pratiṣedha mukhena viśeṣa śabdānām nañaḥ ca yathāyatham arthaiḥ vidita saṅgati tvāt tathā ca ittham eva tad upadiśyate asthūlam aiti sarva viśeṣa atigam etad kathayati bheda prapañca vilaya dvāreṇa iti etad ca vakṣyate iti anyaḥ arthaḥ yad uktam pratyasta mita sakala viśeṣam tattvam pratipatteḥ eva aviṣaya iti tatra ucyate viśeṣa nivṛttyā eva tad śabdena buddhau nidhīyate suvarṇa tattva vat na hi suvarṇa tattvam piṇḍa rucaka ādi saṃsthāna bheda upaplava rahitam dṛśyate na ca te eva suvarṇa tattvam tad parityāge api bhāvāt saṃsthāna antare atha ca adṛṣṭa saṃsthāna bheda upaplava vivekam api buddhyā bheda apoha dvāreṇa svayam pratīyate parasmai ca pratipādyate saḥ eṣa pratipatti kramaḥ śrutyā eva darśitaḥ saḥ eṣa na iti na iti iti tathā anyaiḥ satyam ākṛti saṃhāre yad ante vyavatiṣṭhate tathā aparaiḥ adhyāra karmaṇoḥ sāhityam darśitam pūrvam tāvat prakṛta udgītha viṣayam om iti etad akṣara mudgītham iti upakramāt pareṇa api karma nindayā akṣara jñāna stutiḥ vidyā karmaṇoḥ ca samanvārambhaḥ bhedena vidyāvantam vidyā anvārabhate karmavantam karma iti tasmāt evam api na karma jñānayoḥ eka adhikāra tvam iti ye api virodhāt asambandhaḥ eva karma jñānayoḥ dvaita viṣayam karma advaita viṣayam jñānam aiti manyante teṣām anutpādaḥ eva advaita jñānasya prasajyate pramāṇa ādi vibhāgā dvaita pratipattyoḥ virodhāt atha upāya upeyayoḥ ayaugapadyāt avirodhaḥ pralīyate eva advaita pratipattau sarvaḥ vibhāgaḥ na ca virodhaḥ anupāya tvam vā upāyasya pūrva kāla tvāt tadā ca tasya apralīna tvāt bhedaḥ eva ca abheda pratipattau  upāyaḥ na tarhi karmabhiḥ api virodhaḥ upāya tvāt eva syāt etad asādhya tvāt brahmaṇaḥ na karmaṇām upayogaḥ vidyate śrūyate ca na asti akṛtaḥ kṛtena iti na ca jñāna utpattau  upayogaḥ jñānasya pramāṇa adhīna tvāt na ca jñāna saha kārīṇi karmāṇi jñānasya sādhya antara abhāvāt na tasya mokṣaḥ sādhyaḥ anitya tva prasaṅgāt atha bandha hetu vicchedaḥ sādhyaḥ iti tasmin vicchinne tad abhāvāt mucyate kaḥ punar bandha hetuḥḷ anādya vidyā na tarhi pṛthak ta d vicchedaḥ sādhyaḥ yatas vidyā udayaḥ eva avidyā vyāvṛttiḥ syāt etad  bhavatu agrahaṇa lakṣaṇa avidyā vyāvṛttiḥ vidyā utpādaḥ yatas bhāvaḥ eva abhāva vyāvṛttiḥ na ca vidyā utpādaḥ eva viparyāsa jñāna vyāvṛttiḥ na khalu bhāva antaram bhāva antara vyāvṛttiḥ na ca paraspara abhāva ātmānaḥ bhāvāḥ abhāva tva prasaṅgāt yadi manyeta tattva agrahaṇa nimittaḥ  viparyāsaḥ nimitta nivṛttau svayam eva nivartiṣyate tad ca na na khalva grahaṇam abhāvaḥ kasyacid nimittam mūrcchā ādiṣu prasaṅgāt kim tarhi nimittamḷ anādiḥ aprayojanā ca avidyāa iti uktam tatra ca hetu anuyogaḥ niravakāśaḥ viparyāsa tad saṃskārayoḥ ca paraspara hetu phala bhāvena vyavasthānāt na doṣaḥ atas viparyaya jñānasya nivṛttiḥ vidyayā sādhyeti tatra jñānasya sahakāri apekṣā syāt  etad ca vārtam na khalu śuktikā ādiṣu viparyāsa purassaram samupajāta samyak jñānāḥ tad nivṛttaye pṛthak prayatante sahakāri vā anyat apekṣante yatas virodhi bhāva antara utpādaḥ eva pūrva pradhvaṃsaḥ na śūnyam anyathā na pradhvaṃsaḥ hetumān syāt virodhinī ca vidyā viparyaya jñānasya tad utpattau viparyāsaḥ naṣṭaḥ eva bhavati atha ucyeta karmāṇi bandha hetavaḥ tad kṣayaḥ jñānāt sahakāri savyapekṣāt iti tad ca pramṛṣṭa aśeṣa viśeṣa viśuddha jñāna udaye kutas sambhavaḥḷ tathā ca viparyāsa saṃśayābhyām tulya vat prasaṃkhyātāni karmāṇi abhidyante hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare iti atha vijñāna vaimalyāya ani apekṣā sā api mudhā saṃśaya viparyāsayoḥ jñāna malayoḥ pramāṇa uttha vijñāne asaṃbhavāt atha matam śābda jñānāt anyat api pratyakṣam jñānam iṣyate vigalita vibhāga udgrāham sarva vikalpa atītam tasya hi brahma gocaraḥ na śābdasya vibhakta padārtha saṃsarga udgrāhiṇaḥ tad utpattau karma upāsana ādi apekṣā iti kaḥ punar asya viśeṣaḥ yena tad arthyateḷ spaṣṭa ābha tvam na tasya upayogaḥ jñānam hi jñeya abhivyāptaye śābda jñāne ca utpannaḥ āptam eva jñeyam pramiteḥ pratyakṣa paratvāt tatra ca naiḥ ākāṅkṣyāt tad arthyate iti ced etad adhigate prameye kim anyat ākāṅkṣyetaḷ pramāṇa antaram iti ced na prameya siddhi artha tvāt tad ākāṅkṣāyāḥ punar siddhi artham iti ced na pūrvasmāt api asakṛt tad siddheḥ siddhasya ca siddhi apekṣāyām na hetuḥ asti upāya antara sadbhāvaḥ ced upāya antaram tarhi apekṣeta prameye tu naiḥ ākāṅkṣyam eva prīti viśeṣaḥ ced sa pūrva pramāṇa jāt api darśanāt sidhyati na tad siddhi artham pramāṇa antaram pratyakṣa dṛṣṭam api itaraiḥ tad sambhavāt jijñāsyeta viśeṣa abhāvāt niścāyaka tvam itareṣām api pramāṇa bhāvāt hāna ādi yogya viṣayam pratyakṣam sannikṛṣṭa artha tvāt na itarāṇi iti ced  sannikarṣa hetuḥ tarhi apekṣya tām na pramāṇam siddha tvāt pramāyāḥ prakṛte ca prameye na eṣa viśeṣaḥ asti sāmānya viṣayāḥ śabda ādayaḥ viśeṣa viṣayam pratyakṣam iti ced anadhigataḥ eva tarhi śabdena pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ bāḍham uktam etad na śābdasya jñānasya viṣayaḥ  brahma iti yadi tarhi na śabdena adhigatam brahma katham tasmin  upāsanā pravartatāmḷ na ca anyasmin  upāsyamāne anyat sākṣāt bhavati kasya ca rūpasya sākṣātkaraṇāya yajña ādi vidhānamḷ śabda upadarśita niratiśaya ānanda apahata pāpma ādi rūpa brahma svabhāvasya ātmanaḥ sākṣātkaraṇāya yajña ādi vidhiḥ upapadyate avidita puruṣa artha rūpe tad viparīta rūpe nirvicikitsāt pramāṇāt prakaṭa tām prāpte na aparam apekṣyam asti nanu avagate api tad tvam asi iti śabdāt brahma ātma bhāve prāk iva sāṃsārika dharma darśāt tad nivṛttaye bhavati anya apekṣā na etad sāram katham khalu avagata brahma ātma bhāvaḥ vidita ātma yāthātathyaḥ mithyā darśana nimittaiḥ dharmaiḥ yujyateḷ śrūyate ca brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati iti na ca brahmaṇi apahata pāpmani teṣām avakāśaḥ tathā ātmānam ced vijānīyāt ayam asmi iti pūruṣaḥ kim icchan kasya kāmāya śarīram anusañjvaret tathā aśarīram vāva santam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti mithyā abhimāna nimittaḥ śarīra sambandhaḥ tasmin yāthātathya darśanāt nivṛtte aśarīra tvam tatra priya apriyayoḥ asambandhaḥ ākhyāyate tasmāt na avagata brahma ātma bhāvaḥ prāk iva sāṃsārika dharma bhāj yaḥ tu tathā na asau  avagata brahma ātma bhāvaḥ iti atra ucyate niścite api pramāṇāt tattve sarvatra mithyā avabhāsāḥ nivartante hetu viśeṣāt anuvartante api yathā dvi candra diś viparyāsa ādaya āpta vacana viniścita diś candra tattvānām tathā nirvicikitsā dāmnāyāt avagata ātma tattvasya anādi mithyā darśana abhyāsa upacita bala vat saṃskāra sāmarthyāt mithyā avabhāsa anuvṛttiḥ tad nivṛttaye asti anyat apekṣyam tad ca tattva darśana abhyāsaḥ loka siddhaḥ yajña ādayaḥ ca śabda pramāṇakāḥ abhyāsaḥ hi saṃskāram draḍhayan pūrva saṃskāram pratibadhya sva kāryam santanoti yajña ādayaḥ ca kena api adṛṣṭena prakāreṇa śreyaḥ paripanthi kaluṣa nibarhaṇa dvāreṇa iti anye nityānām karmaṇām durita kṣaya artha tvāt syāt etad anuvartantām mithyā avabhāsāḥ pramāṇāt tu niścayaḥ yathātattvam yathā niścayam ca vyavahāraḥ tasmānāvagata ātma tattvasya kācana śubha aśubhā vā pravṛttiḥ upapadyate ucyate jāte api tattva darśane anāhite ca paṭau saṃskāre draḍhiyasi ca mithyā darśana je saṃskāre niścayāḥ api mithyā arthāḥ bhavanti yathā diś mūḍhasya ananu saṃhita āpta vacasaḥ prāk iva pravṛtti darśanāt tathā pramita rajju bhāvāyāḥ api rajjvāḥ pramāṇa ananu sandhāne sarpa bhrāntyā bhaya darśanam tasmāt jāte api pramāṇāt tattva darśane anādi mithyā darśana abhyāsa pariniṣpannasya draḍhīyasaḥ saṃskārasya abhibhavāya ucchedāya vā tattva darśana abhyāsam manyante tathā ca mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti ucyate śama dama brahmacarya yajña ādi sādhana vidhānam ca anyathā kaḥ tad upadeśa arthaḥḷ syāt etad  brahmacarya ādi sādhana karaṇāt eva āmnāyāt tattva vijñānam tad asat śabda mātrāt pratipatteḥ utpatteḥ na hi prāk  sādhana viśeṣebhyaḥ tattva pratipatti paraḥ āmnāyaḥ avācakaḥ na api aniścāyakaḥ aśeṣa āśaṅkā nirmokṣāt anyathā tad upadiṣṭeṣu sādhaneṣu api durlabhā pratipattiḥ api ca anyathā niścaye api raṅga gatāḥ bharata ādayaḥ mithyā avabhāsena śoka bhaya ādi hetavaḥ niścite api guḍasya mādhurye tatra mithyā tikta avabhāsaḥ avitathaḥ iva duḥkhayati avitathasya iva tasya api dhūtkṛtya tyāgāt tasmāt tad nivṛttaye viniścita brahma ātma bhāvena api sādhanāni apekṣyāṇi yathā eva pramāṇāt tattva abhivyaktau na mukteḥ kārya tā tathā abhivyakti viśeṣe api sādhanebhyaḥ śrutayaḥ tu abhyāsa pariniṣpatti avasthā viṣayāḥ śabda sādhana jñāna apekṣāḥ vā bhavantu tad hetu tvāt uttarasya iti alam ati vistareṇa yad api pṛthakkāryāḥ eva karma vidhayaḥ jñāna adhikāram avatārayanti apākṛta ṛṇa trayasya tatra adhikārāt tad api na niyogataḥ āśrama vikalpasya smaraṇāt tassya āśrama vikalpam eke ‘yam icchet tam avaseda iti ‘yadi vā itarathāḥ brahmacaryāt eva pravrajet iti śravaṇāt etad ha sma vai tad pūrve vidvāṃsaḥ agnihotram na juhavāñcakrire tathā kim prajayā kariṣyāmaḥa tathā ‘kimarthā vayam adhyeṣyāmahe kimarthāḥ vayam yakṣyāmahe iti karma tyāga darśanāt pratipannaga arhasthyasya ātma vidyayā eva kṛtakṛtya tām manvānasya ṛṇa apākaraṇam pratyanādṛtasya vihita akaraṇa nimittasya pāpmanaḥ vidyā udaya pratibandhṛ tvam darśayati ṛṇāni trīṇi apākṛtya iti idam tu yuktam kārya antara nirākāṅkṣāṇām api karmaṇām saṃyoga pṛthaktvāt tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇāḥ vividiṣanti yajñena iti vidyā aṅga bhāvaḥ saḥ api utpatti artha tayā na prayāja ādi vat kāya upayogena vidyāyāḥ kārya antara abhāvāt saṃskāra pakṣaḥ vā smṛteḥ saṃskṛtasya hi vidyā utpatteḥ tad uktam vihita tvāt ca āśrama karmā apia iti nanu dṛṣṭa utpāyaḥ eva vidyā utpādaḥ tatra dṛṣṭā eva iti kartavya tāpekṣyatām śama dama ādi sādhana viśeṣaḥ citta vikṣepasya vihantrī sama hita cittasya ābhasataḥ jñāna prasāda utpatteḥ na tu yajña ādayaḥ taiḥ vinā api abhyāsena tad sambhavāt satyam tathā ca ūrdhvaretasām ca āśramiṇām vinā api taiḥ viśuddha vidyā udayaḥ iṣyate kim tu kāla kṛtaḥ  viśeṣaḥ sādhana viśeṣāt hi sā kṣipram kṣiprataram ca vyajyate tad abhāve cireṇa ciratareṇa ca tad uktam sarva apekṣā ca yajña ādi śruteḥ aśvavat eṣaḥ arthaḥ yajñena dānena aiti śravaṇāt karmāṇi apekṣyante vidyāyām abhyāsa labhyāyām api yathā antareṇa api aśvam grāma prāptau siddyantyām śaighryāya akleśāya vā aśvaḥ apekṣyate nanu vidyā rūpam brahma eva na vidyā brahmaṇaḥ anyā tad ca nityam akāryam tatra katham kiñcid apekṣya itaḷ ucyate yathā upadhāna tirohita rūpa sphaṭika maṇiḥ upadha avakarṣaṇam svarūpa abhivyaktaye apekṣate tathā iha api draṣṭavyam na hi sphaṭika maṇeḥ pūrva rūpam vinaṣṭam upadhāna sannidheḥ tad apagame vā anyat utpannam na hi akasmāt aneka visabhā ga kṣaṇa vyavahitasya pūrva sabhā ga kṣaṇasya utpattiḥ sambhavati na hi agni vigame aṅgārebhyaḥ punar  kāṣṭha santati pravṛttiḥ tasmāt yathā eva akāryam sphaṭika rūpam upadhāna avakarṣaṇam apekṣate tathā ātma rūpam api syat etad jñānam tatra sa apekṣam tad ca sphaṭikāt bhinnam kāryam puruṣa prayatnaḥ hi tatra jñāna arthaḥ kim punar jñānam sva rūpeṇa eva arthitam āhosvit artha svabhāva siddhayeḷ na tāvat svarūpeṇa arthena vyavahārat na vijñāna mātra nibandhanaḥ vyavahāraḥ mithyājñānena api prasaṅgāt atha artha svabhāya jñānam arthyeta tad arthaḥ vyāpāraḥ tena arthitaḥ bhavati na ca jñānāt arthe kaścid vikāraḥ tayoḥ asaṃbandhāt yogya deśa tāyāḥ sarvatra bhāvāt sarva pratipattṛṇām ca vidita tva prasaṅgāt dhvasta anāgateṣu ca tad asaṃbhavāt tasmāt yathā atirohitam api tirohitam iva abhivyajyate iva prayatna apekṣam tathā ātma tattvam api atirohitam tirohitam iva prayatnāt abhivyajyate iva iti puṣkalam yatas ca viśeṣa pratyasta mukhena tad nirūpaṇam atas anyaiḥ brahma vidyā abhiyuktaiḥ sāmānya rūpam brahma nirūpitam saḥ eva mahān ajaḥ ātmā sattā lakṣaṇaḥa tathā ‘sattā eva sarva bheda yoniḥ prakṛtiḥ parāa iti yathā suvarṇa tattvam kaṭaka aṅgulīya ādi viśeṣa upasaṃhāreṇa nirūpyamāṇam tad sāmānyam iti ye vā nirviśeṣam na sāmānyam bhavet śaśa viṣāṇavat aiti abhāvam āhuḥ tān pratyucyate saṃhṛta akhila bheda iti yadi tāvat asāmānya tvam sādhyate siddha sādhanam viśeṣāṇām abhāve keṣām tad sāmanyamḷ sāmanyam tu uktam brahma vādibhiḥ viśeṣa pratyasta mukhena nirūpaṇāt upacārataḥ atha abhāvaḥ eva sādhyaḥ viśeṣaiḥ eva asya nirviśeṣaiḥ vyabhicāraḥ iti [iti śrīmat maṇḍana miśra viracitāyām brahma siddhau brahma kāṇḍaḥ samāptaḥ edition auriginallī bhrahma and tharka kāṇḍaḥ ṭere togetheḥ  Vacaspati doeḥ na ut knoṭ thiḥ division] [tarka kāṇḍaḥ ] nanu pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ vyāvṛttānām bhāva svabhāvānām avagamāt na ekasmin  advaye śabdaḥ pramāṇam pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt grāva plavana ādi arthavacaḥ vat ucyate nanu pramāṇa antara paratantrāṇām puruṣa vacasām tad virodha ādi uktam apramāṇa tvam svatantrasya tvāmnāyasya anapekṣita pramāṇa antara pravṛtteḥ tad virodhe api kasmāt apramāṇa tvamḷ āmnāya virodhāt eva tu pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇa tāyāḥ kim iti na cyavanteḷ tulye anapekṣa tve na viśeṣa hetuḥ asti tatra vṛthā pramāṇa antara virodha parihāra pariśramaḥ iti tatra kecid āhuḥ pratyakṣa ādi virodhe āmnāyasya daurbalyam sa apekṣa tvat tathā hi svarūpa siddhi artham eva tāvat pratyakṣa ādīni āmnāyaḥ apekṣate tathā ca teṣām prāmāṇyam anumantavyam tad apabādhane svarūpasya eva tāvat asiddheḥ na tu evam āmnāye pratyakṣa ādīnām kācid apekṣā dṛṣṭa vyabhicāra tvāt ca śabdasya pratyakṣasya ca adṛṣṭa vyabhicārāt api ca sa avakāśa anavakāśayoḥ anavakāśam balavat anavakāśāḥ ca pratyakṣa ādayaḥ sa avakāśaḥ tu śabdaḥ gauṇena arthena tathā hi śakyam eka tvam abheda śrutīnām upacaritam avakāśaḥ varṇayitum avivakṣita arthānām vā vedāntānām japa upayogaḥ avakāśaḥ upaniṣadaḥ vedāntā iti varṇitam kim ca vyākula tvāt āmnāyasya avyākula tvāt pratyakṣa ādīnām karma vidhayaḥ hi bheda āśrayāḥ abheda āśrayāḥ ca vedāntāḥ paraspara parāhatā asati api pramāṇa antara virodhe durlabha prāmāṇyāḥ kim punar avyāhata pratiṣṭhita prāmāṇya ādi virodhe tasmāt idam avirodhāya prayatyate iti mukhya tvāt ca mukhyāḥ hi pratyakṣa ādayaḥ jātasya jantoḥ apara kāle āmnāyaḥ sa taiḥ pratiṣṭhita arthaiḥ apahṛta viṣayaḥ kalpanīya arthaḥ bādhyate tad anusāreṇa vā artha kalpanām arhati arthataḥ api ca mukhya tā pratyakṣa ādīnām pada padārtha vibhāga adhīnaḥ āmnāya artha paricchedaḥ sa ca pratyakṣa ādiṣu āpatate atas avirodhāya prayatyate iti anye manyante tulya bala tve api pratyakṣa ādīnām āmnāyasya ca vastuni vikalpa anupapatteḥ virodhe saṃśayaḥ syāt tena avirodhaḥ upapādyate iti anyat darśanam āmnāyaḥ eva balavān  tad virodhe paurvāparye pūrva daurbalyam prakṛti vat pūrva ābādhena na utpattiḥ uttarasya hi sidhyati iti tathā hi sarvasya nisarga jaḥ pratyakṣa ādi nibandhanaḥ kila vibhakta vastu paricchedaḥ tad apekṣaḥ tu tad pūrvakaḥ anisarga jaḥ kasyacid eva agantuḥ advaita avagamaḥ sa pūrvam anupamṛdya udetum aśaknuvan  tad apabādha ātmā udīyate itas ca saṃbhavat vicitra vibhrama hetu tvāt pratyakṣa ādīnām vigalita nikhila doṣa āśaṅka tvāt ca āmnāyasya puruṣa āśrayāṇām hi doṣāṇām śabde puruṣa abhāve asaṃbhavāt śakyaḥ hi āmnāyāt eva anādiḥ avidyā saṃskāraḥ vibhrama hetuḥ pratyakṣa ādiṣu saṃbhāvayitum niścetum ca deha ātmā abhimānaḥ iva na tu evam apauruṣeye śabde kācid doṣa āśaṅkā satyām vā pramāṇam eva na syāt pratyakṣa ādīnām tu vyāvahārikam prāmāṇyam avidyā saṃskārsya sthemnā vyavahāra viparyaya abhāvāt yatra ca vyavahāra viparyayaḥ na tatra prāmāṇyam śabde tu saṃbhāvita doṣe na tattva āvedanena prāmāṇyam na vyavahāra aviparyayeṇa adṛṣṭa artha tvāt doṣebhyaḥ vyavahāra visaṃvādi jñāna darśanāt ca pratyakṣa ādīnām tu vyavahāre saṃvādāt na śakyate vyavahāra visaṃvādi jñāna hetuḥ doṣaḥ kalpayitum vyavahāra viparyayāt hi sa kalpyeta tattva darśanasya tu vedānta janmanaḥ pratipakṣa tvāt tattva pratihati mātra hetuḥ eva anādiḥ avidya anubandhaḥ kalpyate tatas doṣa anubandhaḥ prāmāṇyam ca iti na virodhaḥ śabdaḥ tu saṃbhāvita doṣaḥ durlabha prāmāṇyaḥ eva syāt dṛśyate hi doṣebhyaḥ vyavahāra visaṃvādi jñāna utpattiḥ tatra doṣa āśaṅkayā vyavahāra visaṃvādasya śaṅkita tvāt tattva pratighātasya ca na tattva āvedana lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam na vyavahāra avisaṃvāda lakṣaṇam iti tasmāt śabdasya prāmāṇya abhyupagame pramāṇa antara virodhe api tasya eva balavat tvam iti sāṃpratam yad tu pratyakṣa ādi apekṣaṇāt iti tatra ucyate na pramitau  apekṣāvattā śabdasya pratyakṣa ādiṣu kim tu svarūpa siddhau anyathā pramāṇam eva na syāt tathā ca sva kārye apekṣa tvāt na pratyakṣa ādibhyaḥ hīyate pratyakṣa ādayaḥ api svarūpa siddhau na anya anapekṣāḥ kārye hi sa apekṣa tvam sāmarthyam apakarṣati iti yad tu eteṣām prāmāṇyam anumātavyam iti kaḥ vā anyathā ahaḷ vyavahāra avisaṃvādi lakṣaṇam tu tad na tattva āvedana lakṣaṇam vyāvahārika prāmāṇya upetebhyaḥ pratyakṣa ādibhyaḥ siddhāt āmnāyāt tattva darśanam tad virodhāt teṣu tattva darśana aṃśam eva apabādhate na vyavahāra avisaṃvāda aṃśam dṛṣṭam ca hetu tvena apekṣitāyāḥ api pūrvasyāḥ pratipatteḥ parasyāḥ pratipatteḥ balīyaḥ tvam yathā dūra stheṣu vanaspatiṣu hasti pratipattibhyaḥ vanaspati pratipatteḥ apekṣitāḥ hi hasti pratipattayaḥ  vyakta vanaspati pratipattyā hetu tvena na tasyāḥ indriya artha saṃnikarṣa mātrāt janma āpāte abhāvāt na ca deśa viśeṣāt  tad deśa sthasya eva utpatteḥ tasmāt puras vartiṣu vanaspatiṣu praṇihita manasaḥ prācya viparyāsa anugatam ati saṃskāra saciva indriya ādi saṃyoga kāritā sā iti mantavyam evam eka ādi saṃkhyā buddhi apāyāḥ viṃśati ādi buddhayaḥ api udāhāryāḥ evam ca yad eke varṇayanti svayam eva vyāhatā vedānta artha pratipattiḥ nābhedaḥ bhedam antareṇa śakyaḥ avasātum bheda upāyā hi tasya pratipattiḥ tatra abhedaḥ samākṣipta bhedaḥ eva pratāyate iti vyāghātaḥ tad apāstam yatas upāyam ākṣipati pratipattiḥ na upāyasya parama artha tām mithyājñānāt api tattva pratipatteḥ vyāvahārikam ca bhedasya satya tvam iṣṭam eva iti vyabhicāra darśanam ca duṣṭa hetu janmanoḥ śabda pratyakṣayoḥ samānam itarayoḥ api tulyam avyabhicāri tvam tathā anavakāśa tvam api yadi khalu ekam advayam vedānta arthaḥ kaḥ teṣām anyaḥ avakāśaḥḷ atha aupacārika tvam eka tvam tad arthaḥ avivakṣita artha tā vā japa upayoginām tatra virodhaḥ eva na asti iti bala abala cintā na avatarati tad kutas sa avakāśa tvena daurbalyamḷ katham ca mukhyam artham ati laṅghya upacaritaḥ avakāśaḥḷ katham vautpattike śabdasya artham prati śeṣa bhāve dṛṣṭaḥ hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam ‘a viśiṣṭaḥ tu vākya arthaḥ aiti ca avivakṣita artha tāḷ pramāṇa antara virodhāt iti ced vārtam etad na pramāṇasya pramāṇa antara apekṣam prāmāṇyam yena tad virodhe svarasam jahyāt tad apekṣa tve hi tad anuguṇa tayā varteta nirapekṣasya kaḥ pramāṇa antara anusaraṇe hetuḥḷ laukikāḥ tu śabdāḥ pramāṇa antara apekṣam sva artham abhidadhati iti yuktā teṣām tad anusāriṇī vṛttiḥ tulye tu anapekṣa tve kim iti na viparyayaḥ ubhayoḥ vā vyāghātāt aprāmāṇyam paurvāparye pūrva daurbalyam aiti vā rajata jñānasya iva pūrvasya bādhaḥḷ na khalu rajata jñāna virodhāt śukti jñānam anya viṣayam aviṣayam vā katham tarhi vede guṇavādaḥ yatra śrautaiḥ arthaiḥ pramāṇa artha niṣpatteḥ asambhavaḥ tatra dvitīyasyāḥ api vṛtteḥ śabdānām pravṛtti darśanāt tayā pramāṇa viṣaya lābhaḥ yatra tu śabdāḥ svarasena labhante viṣayam tatra na pramāṇa antara virodhāt apāvartante na hi eṣām pramāṇa antara nibandhanaḥ arthaḥ yena tad vaśāt apāvarteran atha matam ubhaya anugrahāt evam kalpyate evam hi śabdaḥ pratyakṣa ādayaḥ ca anugṛhītāḥ bhavanti anyathā pratyakṣa ādayaḥ atyantam apabādhitāḥ ṃ ā @meva bādhitāḥ edition syuḥ na etad sāram pramāṇa sāmarthya anusāreṇa prameye kācid kalpanā syāt pramāṇe tu svarasa siddham parityajya kalpanāyām na nibandhanam asti tasmāt pramāṇa anusāreṇa vikalpa samuccaya vyavasthāḥ kalpyante na ubhaya anugrahāt na ubhayam anugṛhītavyam iti pramāṇam asti te eva pramāṇe iti ced yadi matam na pramāṇasya pramāṇa antarāt anugrāhya tvam api tu svatas eva pramāṇa tvāt eva hi tasya tena artha vyavasthāpanā yathā tarhi tatas arthaḥ avagamyate tathā vyavasthāpanīyaḥ evam tad anugṛhītam bhavati anyathā bādhitam syāt apramāṇikā ca artha vyavasthā tatas svarasena apratīteḥ anyasya ca abhāvāt itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt ca prāmāṇyāt siddhāt artha antare pratītiḥ prāmāṇya ani athā anupapattyā kalpanīyā tad pratīteḥ ca prāmāṇyam svarasalabhye tu arthe pratītitaḥ eva prāmāṇyam iti na itaretarāśraya tā tasmāt virodhe bādhaḥ eva pūrvasya pramāṇa anusārī tathā pratīteḥ na uttarasya viṣaya antara kalpanā na khalu rajata jñāna anugrahāya śukti śakala jñānasya gocaraḥ  aparaḥ kalpyate na ca pratyakṣa ādīnām ananya gati tvāt anavakāśa tvam yā khalu rajata ādi vibhramāṇām gatiḥ sā teṣām api yadi teṣām upacaritaḥ kalpitaḥ vā viṣayaḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām api tathā atha asattvāt tasya āviṣayāḥ avidyamāna arthāḥ pratyakṣa ādayaḥ api evam tasmāt avivakṣita artha tvam upacarita artha tvam vā gatiḥ ubhayoḥ aviśiṣṭāḥ etena idam api parākṛtam yad āhuḥ śabdasya pramāṇa antara virodhe dṛṣṭam upacarita artha tvam avivakṣita artha tvam vā loke tasmāt pratyakṣa ādi virodhe vedāntānām tathā abhāvaḥ iti pratyakṣa ādiṣu api tathā darśanāt iti yad tu mukhya tvāt pratiṣṭhita arthaiḥ apahata viṣayaḥ āmnāyaḥ iti atas eva bādhakaḥ śukti jñāna vat na ca tad anusāreṇa artha kalpanām arhati anapekṣa tvāt na tad adhīnam asya pramāṇa tvam na taiḥ saṃbhūyakāri tvam nāmnā ayasya pratyakṣa ādīnām ca eka vākya bhāvaḥ paraspara anapekṣaḥ hi ubhayatra buddhi utpādaḥ tatra para balīyaḥ tvam nyāyyam yathoktam pūrvāt para balīyaḥ tvam tatra nāma pratīyatām anyonya nirapekṣāṇām yatra janma dhiyām bhavet yatra tu eka vākya tayā saṃbhūyakāri tvam tatra anupajāta virodhitayā sva rasa vṛttyā mukhye sthite prathamayā vṛttyā tad eka vākya tvam pratipattum aśaknuvanti tad apekṣita artha samarpaṇa anupapatteḥ para padāni dvitīyayā vṛttyā pūrva apekṣitam artham samarpayanti eka vākyatā sāmarthyāt iti mukhya balīyaḥ tvam yad tu vyākula tvāt iti tatra ucyate syāt vyākula tvam yadi karma vidhayaḥ bheda pratipādana parāḥ syuḥ te tu siddham bhedam upāśritya idam anena ittham sādhayet iti puruṣa hita anuśāsana pradhānāḥ syāt etad asati bhede aṃśa traya pratyasta mayāt kutas hita anuśāsanamḷ ucyate yathā khalu śyena ādiṣu na hiṃsyāt sarvā bhūtāni iti pratiṣedhāt sādhya aṃśa pratyasta maye api anuśāsanam evam sarvatra sarva aṃśa pratyasta maye api tathā hi niṣiddha anartha udayā katham hiṃsā sādhyā syātḷ atha bhavati kasya cit tīvra krodha ākrānta svānta tayā samuddhata dhvānta tiraskṛta viveka vijñānasya anartham api artha tvena paśyataḥ śāstra upadeśam atikrāmataḥ tathā jyotiṣṭoma ādiṣu nisarga ja avidyā upadarśitāḥ apratibuddhānām trayaḥ api aṃśāḥ tān upāśritya teṣām anuśāsanam pratibuddhāḥ tu karma vidhibhiḥ na anuśiṣyante yathā śyena ādi vidhibhiḥ apajita krodha arātayaḥ tad evam vyavahāra siddha bheda āśrayeṣu karma vidhiṣu yadi api bheda pratītiḥ asti tathā api teṣām atatparatvāt na tatra prāmāṇyam vṛttānteṣu iva arthavāda padānām tathā ca kutas taiḥ veda antānām parāhatiḥ vedāntaiḥ vā teṣāmḷ api ca pratyakṣa ādiṣu eva parāhatiḥ upalabhyate bādhya bādhaka bhāva darśanāt rajata śukti śakala ādi jñāneṣu bheda abheda pratīteḥ ca sarvatra tad evam balavat tve api āmnāyasya yaḥ nāma manda dhīḥ laukika vacasām pratyakṣa ādi virodhaḥ upacarita artha tva darśanāt loka vat vede api śabda vṛttam iti manyate yaḥ vā nirūḍha nibiḍa tayā bheda darśana andhakārasya pratyakṣa ādīnām eva balavat tvam manyate loka vacasām ca taiḥ bādha darśanāt tad pratibodhanāya virodhaḥ nirasyate na hi yaḥ nāma manda viṣeṇa vṛścikena daṣṭaḥ mriyate na asau na cikitsyate iti tatra pratyakṣe trayaḥ kalpāḥ vastu svarūpa vidhiḥ vastu antarasya vyavacchedaḥ ubhayam vetti ubhayasmin  api traividhyam yaugapadyam vyavaccheda pūrvakaḥ vidhiḥ vidhi pūrvakaḥ vyavacchedaḥ iti tatra vastu antara vyavacchede ubhayasmin vā bhedaḥ pratyakṣa gocaraḥ iti bhavati virodhaḥ sva rūpa vidhi mātre tu kasyacid vyavacchedena śūnye na bhedaḥ pramāṇa arthaḥ na hi vyavacchedāt ṛte bheda siddhiḥ vidhi mātra vyāpāram ca pratyakṣam atas na virodhaḥ katham iti ucyate na tāvat vyavaccheda mātram pratyakṣa vyāpāraḥ na yugapad ubhayam na vyavaccheda pūrvakam vidhānam yatas siddhe viṣaye siddha rūpam eva niṣidhyate na idam iha ‘nāya mayam aiti siddhe bhū tale siddhaḥ ghaṭaḥ gavi vā aśvaḥ na pratiṣedhyāt pratiṣedha viṣayāt ca vinā pratiṣedhaḥ avakalpate katham tarhi atyanta asatām pradhāna kha puṣpa ādīnām pratiṣedhaḥḷ na hi tatra kvacid deśe kāle vā niṣedhaḥ ātyantika tvāt na api kutaścid siddhi atyanta asattvāt tatra kecid āhuḥ kha puṣpa ādiṣu tāvat siddheṣu kha ādiṣu tadvidhāḥ puṣpa ādayaḥ niṣidhyante pradhānam na asti aiti jagat kāraṇe sukha duḥkha moha ātma tā vibhakta kārya tva ādīni nivāryante anye tu kutaścid nimittāt buddhau labdha rūpāṇām bahis niṣedhaḥ kriyate iti varṇayanti anyathā daiva niṣiddhe kaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ aprāpta rūpeḷ prāpta rūpe vā katham atyantāya pratiṣedhaḥḷ api ca anapekṣita viṣaya niṣedhye vyavacchede śūnyatā pramāṇa arthaḥ syāt na bhedaḥ sarvasya sarvatra aviśeṣeṇa niṣedhāt yaḥ tu bhedāya vyavacchedaḥ sa bhedyayoḥ siddhim apekṣate na ca sā vidhāna ādṛtaḥ iti prāc vidhānam eṣitavyam vidhi pūrvakaḥ eva ca niṣedhaḥ aṅgīkriyata iti na api vidhi pūvakaḥ vyavacchedaḥ yatas na khalu eka pramāṇa jñāna vyāpārau santau vidhi vyavacchedau kramavantau yujyete kṣaṇika tvāt  kramavatoḥ hi vyāpārayoḥ paścāt tanaḥ na tad vyāpāraḥ syāt vyavadhānāt api ca janma eva buddheḥ vyāpāraḥ artha avagraha rūpāyāḥ sā ced arha vidhāna rūpa udayā vidheḥ eva asyāḥ vyāpāraḥ yaugapadyasya niṣedhāt utpannāyāḥ ca punar anutpatteḥ api ca saṃnihita artha ālambanam pratyakṣam na asaṃnihitam artham avabhāsayitum arhati na ca anavabhāsamāna rūpam vyavacchettum paryāpnoti anavabhāsamāne hi tatra vyavacchedye vyavaccheda mātram syāt na vyavacchedaḥ kasyacid sarvasya vā syāt tasmāt na anavabhāsamāne vyavacchedye vyavacchedaḥ na ca saṃnihita artha avalambane pratyakṣe asaṃnihita avabhāsaḥ yuktaḥ katham idānīm bādhakam pratyakṣamḷ tatra hi pūrva artha niṣedha puraḥsaraḥ anya vidhiḥ eka jñāne abhyupeyate asaṃnihita niṣedhya avabhāsaḥ ca tasmāt na eṣa niyamaḥ yatas pūrvaḥ niṣedhaḥ eka jñāna vyāpāre ca kramaḥ pratyakṣeṇa ca asaṃnihita artha avabhāsaḥ na etad sāram tatra api pūrva vijñāna vihite rajata ādau idam iti ca saṃnihita artha sāmānye niṣedhaḥ vidhi pūrvaḥ eva śuktikā vidhiḥ tu virodhi niṣedha pūrvaḥ ucyate vidhi pūrva tā ca niyamena niṣedhasya ucyate na vidheḥ niṣedha pūrvaka tā niṣidhyate na ca tatra eka jñānasya krama vat vyāpāra tā ubhaya rūpasya utpatteḥ pūrva jñāna prāpita tvāt ca viṣaya vyavacchedyayoḥ na asaṃbhavaḥ pūrva jñāna avabhāsite ca vyavacchedye vyavacchedasya vṛtteḥ na asaṃnihita artha avabhāsa prasaṅgaḥ pūrva apekṣasya tasya utpatteḥ pūrva apekṣayā eva ca tad dvi rūpam udeti anyathā eka rūpam eva udīyāt api ca sarva vyavacchedān apākurvataḥ kaḥ vyavacchedaḥ abhimataḥ yena pratyavasthīyetaḷ siddhaḥ sa lokaḥ iti ced ayam vā kim na loka siddhaḥ na aśvaḥ gauḥ na gauraśvaḥ itiḷ yad tu matam eka vidhiḥ eva anya vyavacchedaḥ tathā hi darśanam yathā eva tad ākāratayā tad rūpam vidadhāti tathā tad eka ākāra pratiniyamāt tad eva na anyat iti anyat vyavacchinatti tad sāmarthya prabhāvitau ca ‘idam na idam aiti vikalpau bhāva abhāva vyavahāram pravartayataḥ na hi eka ākāra pratiniyatāt ananya saṃsargiṇaḥ jñānāt anyaḥ anya vyavacchedaḥ tatra ucyate na eka pratiniyamaḥ anya abhāva niścaya nimittam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpti asya itarasya ca aviśeṣeṇa vyavaccheda prasaṅgāt tad pratiniyamaḥ hi tatas anyasya asaṃsargaḥ tathā ca asaṃsargāt vyavacchede tasya dṛśya adṛśyayoḥ aviśeṣāt ubhayoḥ vyavacchedaḥ syāt atha matam bhavati eva tathā hi yāvantaḥ  asya anātmāna stān aviśeṣeṇa tad ātma niyamāt darśanam apākaroti tathā ca na asya anyaḥ ātmānaḥ tad deśa kālāḥ tu bhaveyuḥ rūpa ādi vat avirodhāt  tatra upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ viśeṣaḥ tad deśa kāla vyavaccheda avadhāraṇāya saṃbhavati hi anupalabhyaḥ tad deśa kālaḥ anātma anupalabhyamānaḥ  api anya upalabdhau itara vat anyathā na tulya upalambha yogyatas syāt satyam asti ayam vibhāgaḥ na tu idānīm darśana pratiniyamasya sāmarthyam tathā hi pratiniyatam api tatra deśe kāle ca rūpe darśanam tayoḥ yathā rūpa vidhi mātra upakṣayāt na rasam vyavacchinatti tathā bhū bhāga darśana niyamaḥ api bhū bhāga vidhi mātra vyāpāra tvāt na ghaṭadṛśyam api vyavacchindyāt vyavacchede vā sarvasya vyavacchedaḥ tasmāt dṛśya vyavacchede api hetu antaram upāsyam na darśana pratiniyama mātram tathā ca ātmā antara vyavacchedaḥ api na tatas  siddhim upāśnute kāmam vidheḥ vidheyā sattva vyavaccheda rūpa tvāt tad abhāvaḥ vyavacchidyeta na ātma antara sat tā tad deśa kālayoḥ iva anupalabhya sattā na ekasya bahavaḥ ātmānaḥ iti ced anyatas tarhi virodhāt vyavacchedaḥ na darśana niyamāt asati ca vyavacchede kutas bahu tvam kutas vā virodhaḥ itaretara āśrayam vāḷ tasmāt na eka vidhiḥ anya vyavacchedaḥ api ca eka niyamāt anya vyavacchede citra ādiṣu nīla ādīnām eka darśana bhājām bhedaḥ na sidhyet eka jñāna saṃsargāt ekatra jñānasya aniyamāt nanu prakṛtyā eva bhinnāḥ bhāvāḥ tān  tadvidhān vidadhat eva darśanam parasparataḥ vyāvartayati na hi vyāvṛttiḥ anyā vyāvṛttimataḥ tatra vyāvṛttimat vidhau sā api vidhīyate eva yad prakṛtiḥ khalu yaḥ padārthaḥ sa tayā eva prakṛtyāḥ vidheyaḥ anyathā na tasya vidhiḥ syāt vyāvṛtta svabhāvāḥ ca bhāvāḥ yathāyatham darśaneṣu nirbhāsante tasmāt tathā eva vidhīyante iti atra api asaṃspṛṣṭa nirbhāsanāt asaṃspṛṣṭa svabhāva tve dṛśyayoḥ aviśeṣeṇa vyavacchedaḥ tad avasthaḥ api ca na vyāvṛttiḥ vastu svabhāvaḥ sā khalu eka aneka adhiṣṭhānā pratijñāyate prajñāyate ca tathā ca tasyāḥ ekasyāḥ aneka vṛtteḥ vastu svabhāva tve vastūnām api bhedaḥ na syāt na ekasmāt abhinna svabhāvam bhinnam yujyate tadvat eva atha mā bhūt eṣa doṣaḥ iti artha antaram eva vyāvṛttiḥ āsthīyate tathā api vyāvṛtteḥ rūpa tvāt svarūpeṇa na bhāvāḥ vyāvṛttāḥ syuḥ aparaḥ kalpaḥ bhedaḥ parasparān ātma svabhāvaḥ sa ced vastunaḥ svabhāvaḥ vastūnām abhāva prasaṅgaḥ abhāva ātmaka tva pratijñānāt aparaḥ prakāraḥ bhedaḥ ced vastunaḥ svabhāvaḥ na ekam kiñcana vastu syāt bhedena ekatvasya virodhāt paramāṇuḥ api bhedāt aneka ātmakaḥ iti na ekaḥ tathā ca tad samuccaya rūpaḥ anekaḥ api asya ātmā na avakalpate tatra ekatva aneka tvayoḥ anupapatteḥ tṛtīya prakāra asaṃbhavāt ca vastunaḥ  niḥsvabhāva tva prasaṅgaḥ anyā vyākhyā dvitīya ardhasya vyatireka avyatireka vikalpe pratyavatiṣṭhate vastu gataḥ eṣa vibhāgaḥ tad svabhāva tvam anya tvam ca iti na avastuni vikalpa viracita śarīre bhede avatāram arhati tathā hi tattva anya tva abhyām anirvacanīyaḥ anādi vikalpa vāsanā upādāna vikalpa paridarśita śarīraḥ ayam asmāt bhinnaḥ ayamanayoḥ bhedaḥ iti vyavahāram pravartayati na bhedaḥ nāma kiñcid vastu yasya tattvam anya tvam vā kiñcid vicāryeta tatra idam punar upatiṣṭhate arūpeṇa ca bhinna tvam vastunaḥ na avakalpate yadi tarhi arūpaḥ niḥsvabhāvaḥ bhedaḥ na hi vastu sthityā asti vikalpaiḥ eva kevalam upadarśyate na tarhi vastunaḥ bhinna tvam paramārtha taḥ  bheda abhāvāt na hi kalpitena svabhāvena pāramārthikī tadvat tā yujyate kalpitā eva syāt tad etad asmābhiḥ ucyamānam kim iti bhavān na anumanyateḷ vayam api etad eva brūmaḥ na bhedaḥ bhāvataḥ asti anādya vidyā vilasitam etad iti yad uktam bheda ātma tve vastuna eka vastu abhāvaḥ tad bhāvāt itarasya api iti vastu abhāvaḥ tatra āhuḥ para apekṣam vastunaḥ bheda svabhāvam brūmaḥ na ātma apekṣam yena virodhāt eka vastu abhāvaḥ syāt sva rūpeṇa tu ekam vastu para apekṣayā bhinnam iti tatra ucyate pauruṣeyīm apekṣām ca na hi vastu anuvartate na apekṣā nāma kaścid vastu dharmaḥ yena vastūni vyavasthāpyeran na khalu sva hetu prāpita udayeṣu svabhāva vyavasthiteṣu vastuṣu svabhāva sthitaye vastu antara apekṣā yujyate tatra puruṣa pratyaya dharmaḥ ayam na ca puruṣa pratyaya anuvidhāyīni vastūni sva hetubhyaḥ sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ atas na tad anusāreṇa vastu rūpam vyavatiṣṭhate vyavasthita vastu svarūpa anusāreṇa eva tasya vyavasthā nyāyyā tad pūrvaka tvāt paraspara apekṣāyām ca vastu svabhāva sthitau  itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt athavā yad uktam ekasmāt bhedāt avyatiredāt vastunaḥ  bheda abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti tatra āhuḥ na bhedaḥ ekaḥ rūpa virodhāt eka tve ca tad nimittam vastūnām eka tvam syāt tasmāt pratibhāvam bhedaḥ  bhidyate katham tarhi aneka āśraya tvamḷ apekṣātaḥ tathā hi pratiyogi apekṣam tasya svarūpam vyavasthitam tathā ca yathāyatham bhedaiḥ pratiyogi apekṣaiḥ ātma bhūtaiḥ bhinnāḥ sarve bhāvāḥ iti tatra ucyate pauruṣeyīm iti puruṣaḥ hi ekam artham gṛhītvā param apekṣate kārya artham sva hetubhyaḥ tu pratilabdha avikala svabhāvānām bhāvānām bhāva antareṣu kim artha apekṣāḷ nanu svabhāva sthitaye nānāvidhāḥ hi bhāva svabhāvāḥ tatra kaścid pratiyogi apekṣayā eva vyavatiṣṭhate vastu tattve yathā ayam eva bhedaḥ na tarhi hetubhyaḥ  bhāvasya avikala ātma lābhaḥ bheda ākhyasya rūpasya pratiyogi apekṣa tvāt hetu antarāt ca pratiyoginaḥ saṃpadyamānaḥ paścāt bhedaḥ na svabhāvaḥ syāt syāt etad avikala rūpaḥ eva bhāvaḥ hetubhyaḥ jāyate tatra bheda ākhyam rūpam pratiyogi apekṣam na anapekṣam kadācid ittasya tadvidha tvāt tena tadvidhena eva saha jāyate iti na vikala rūpa prādurbhāvaḥ tatra ucyate bhavatu tadvidhasya prādurbhāvaḥ apekṣā arthaḥ tu vaktavyaḥ yasya hi yatra kiñcid āyatate tad tat apekṣate iti ucyate na anyaḥ viśeṣaḥ sa apekṣa nirapekṣayoḥ vyapasthāpakaḥ  nirūpyate tatra na tāvat utpattiḥ pratiyoginī āyatate sva hetubhyaḥ avikalasya utpatteḥ na artha kriyā tad asaṃnidhāne api tasya artha kriyā darśanāt pratītiḥ ced tathā hi na anapekṣya pratiyoginam bhedaḥ pratīyate iti na tarhi bheda svabhāvaḥ sa apekṣaḥ tasmin  avasthite vastu sthiti uttara kālā pratītiḥ artha antaram eva pratiyoginam apekṣate yathā vyavasthita anapekṣa svabhāvā rūpa ādayaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi apekṣāyām pratītau na sa apekṣa svabhāvāḥ kathyate itaretara āśrayāt ca na pratītiḥ api paraspara āyattau  akalpate na ca vastu mātrāt anavagṛhīta bhedāt bheda siddhiḥ ekasmin  api tad prasaṅgāt tasmāt pauruṣeyīm apekṣāyām na vastu anuvarttate atas na vastu svabhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ anyā vyākhyā na bhedaḥ vastunaḥ rūpam āpekṣikaḥ hi pratīyate na ca apekṣāyām puruṣa pratyayam vastu anuvartate vyavasthita vastu pūrvaka tvāt iti katham tarthi pitṛ ādayaḥḷ na hi te apekṣayā vinā na ca khapuṣpa gandharvanagara ādi tulyāḥ avisaṃvādi vyavahāra aṅga tayā loka siddha tvāt ucyate bhedaḥ api evam kim na loka siddhaḥḷ api ca vyavasthite eva janya janaka śaktī pitṛ putra śabdayoḥ abhidheye vidyate vyavasthitayoḥ api vastunoḥ bhāva bhede tu ayam vastu tattva gataḥ vicāraḥ na ca apekṣā hetuḥ kaścid upalabhyate hrasva dīrghayoḥ api eka jātīyāyām kriyāyām deśa vyāptau nyūna adhika bhāvāt evam draṣṭavyam yadi tarhi kārya bhedāt api apekṣāḥ hanta  artha kriyā bhedāt eva bhāvānām paraspara apekṣaḥ bhedaḥ setsyati kim ca asatyām api darśanāt bheda siddhau vidhi mātra vyāpāra tvāt kārya bhedāt eva kāraṇa bhedam anumimīmahe na ekatve kārya bhedaḥ kalpate kāraṇa svabhāva apekṣa tvāt kārya bhedasya tad jananaḥ ca id asya tad jananam ced asya edition svabhāvaḥ na anya jananaḥ tasmāt vyapadeśa bheda mātram tu syāt ekasmin  api vahnau dāha pāka ādi kārya bheda dṛṣṭeḥ atha matam rūpa ādi samūhaḥ vahniḥ tatra rūpāt prakāśaḥ sparśāt dāha iti kāmam dāha pākau tu sparśāt eva tau ca loke pratīti bhedau sati api saṃyogi dravya vikriyā sāmānye karma ca ekam saṃyoga vibhāga saṃskārāṇām hetuḥ ātmā ca icchā ādīnām sattva ādayaḥ ca pratyekam abhedāt lāghava prakāśa ādīnām rūpa ādayaḥ jñāna viśeṣāṇām sajātī yakṣaṇānām ca iti utprekṣitavyam nanu na artha kriyā bheda mātrāt bhedam brūmaḥ api tu tatra asaṃbhāvinyāḥ adṛṣṭāyāḥ yathā cakṣuṣi sati api adṛṣṭāyāḥ ca badhire tatra asaṃbhāvinyāḥ śabda buddheḥ indriya bhedaḥ paraspara asaṃbhavi kāryāḥ ca prāyeṇa bhāvāḥ anya kāryasya anyatra adarśanāt atha kārya asaṃbhavaḥ katham pratyetavyaḥḷ nanu uktam tatra adarśanāt na tarhi asaṃbhavaḥ yasya khalva dvayam jagat tasya kārya jātam ekatra eva dṛśyate iti katham adarśanamḷ tatra siddhe bhede tatra adarśanam tatra adarśanāt ca bheda siddhiḥ iti ita retara āśrayāt na bheda anumānam atha matam adṛṣṭasya darśanāt iti tad asat ekasmāt api kramavatām kāryāṇām darśanāt syāt etad ekāntataḥ abhede kārya darśana adarśane na yukte viśeṣa abhāvāt na tarhi kārya bhedaḥ abhedam apabādhate tad anupamardena viśeṣa mātra anumānam syāt tad ca kalpanā viṣayam na eva avajānīmahe vastu sataḥ tasya ayogāt tattva anya tvayoḥ asaṃbhavāt yaḥ tu kṣaṇika vādī tattvam eva viśeṣasya na manyate tasya asati kāraṇa svabhāva abhede katham tulya svabhāva kārya utpādaḥ atha niranvaya vināśānām api kalpanā viṣayāt abhedāt kāryasya tulya tā hanta  tarhi bhedāt eva kalpanā viṣayāt kārya bheda siddheḥ avacchinnāḥ dharmāḥ anavacchinnam anantam artham āśrayantaḥ api na vyaśnuvate atas na ekasmin  api bhāva abhāva virodhaḥ yaḥ tu manyeta artha kriyā bhedaḥ artha kriyā vyavasthā tatas bheda adhigamaḥ eka tve hi na vyavasthā yujyate tathā ca payasaḥ api tailam tilebhyaḥ ca dadhi syāt tathā ekasmin jāyamāne sarvam jāyeta naśyati ca naśyet anyathā bhedaḥ eva śabda antareṇa uktaḥ syāt tad uktam saha utpatti vināśau sarvam ca sarvatra upayujyeta iti tasya āpi idam eva uttaram dāha pāka vibhāgena iti yadi kārya nānā tvam vyavasthā na tayā tilānām payasaḥ ca bhedam pratipadyate atha payasaḥ dadhnaḥ janma na anyatas iti vyavasthā na anya tvam siddhayā vyavasthayā pramitsitam tad lakṣaṇam anupraveṣṭum arhati tasyāḥ asiddhi prasaṅgāt tasmāt dadhi janana śaktiḥ tad abhāvaḥ ca vyavasthā tatas bhedaḥ na hi eka viṣaya ekasya śakti aśaktī yujyete iti sa ca ayam virodhi dharma yogaḥ bheda hetuḥ anantaram eva nirāsi yathā khalu dīrgha kālāḥ padārthā mita kālaiḥ dharmaiḥ saṃbadhyamānāḥ tad dharmāṇaḥ atad dharmāṇaḥ ca na virodha pada bhājaḥ tathā parimita deśaiḥ vipula deśāḥ anantāḥ ca katham anantasya antavān dharmaḥ iti ced vyatireke anivarcanīya tve vā na asti asaṃbhāvanā avakāśaḥ avyatireke api dīrgha kālasya iva mita kālaḥ yaḥ api dīrgha kālam artham na pratipadyate tam prati idam punar paṭhitavyam dāha pāka vibhāgena iti ekaḥ api vahniḥ kiñcid eva dahati pacati ca tathā ca dāhakaḥ ca janakatvam ajanaka tvam iti atha ekasmin  eva janaka śaktiḥ anyam pradhvastam āgāminam vā ekam kim na janayati atha tatra eva eṣām sāmarthyam na anyatra tulya jātīye api kutas ḷ tasya eva utpatteḥ kārya gamya tvāt ca sāmarthyasya tathā ca na śaktiḥ aśaktiḥ ca iti virodhaḥ abhede api tarhi payasaḥ tilānām dadhnaḥ anutpattau na virodhaḥ tathā hi yasya tāvat dadhnaḥ payasaḥ janma na tasya tilebhyaḥ anutpattiḥ yena śakti aśakti virodhāt bhedaḥ syāt kutas ḷ tilānām payasaḥ abhedāt atha dadhi antarasya anutpatteḥ virodhaḥ tad ca na anyatra aśakteḥ tatra eva śakteḥ bīja ādīnām iva na hi samartham iti eva kāraṇam sarvam tulya jātīyam janayati ekasmāt eva sarva tulya jātīya kārya utpatti prasaṅgāt atha matam artha kriyāsu bhedena viniyogāt bheda madhyavasyāmaḥ dadhne hi payaḥ viniyujyate na sikatā iti tad api anaikāntikam eka tve api bhedena viniyoga darśanāt tad eva artha vastu sahakāri sametam viniyujyate na kevalam atha matam bhinnam eva tad sahakāri sannidhāna upādhi bhedāt aupādhikaḥ tarhi pratyaya mātra niveśī bhedaḥ na paramārthataḥ tathābhūtaḥ ca bhāva bhedaḥ hi anujñāyate eva yaḥ api kṣaṇika tvena bhedam āha tasya api bhedasya tulya tvāt sarvam sarvatra viniyujyate na vā kiñcid kvacid adṛṣṭa sāmarthya tvāt atha kalpanā viṣayāt abhedāt tad siddhiḥ parasya api tādṛśāt bhedāt iti na viśeṣaḥ iti uktam yaḥ api ekasya ubhayam pratijānīte bhedam abhedam ca bhedasya upapatteḥ virodhasya ca anaikāntika tvāt asiddha tvāt vā vyavasthāyāḥ ca viniyoga bhedasya ca anaikāntika tvāt abhedāt iva ca kalpitāt bhedāt tad siddheḥ bheda abhedayoḥ ca ekatra samavāye śīrṣā iti ‘yat bhūtam yad ca bhavyam iti pūrvarc dvaya nirdiṣṭa vividha viruddha abhimata dharma kārya vyavahāra āśrayaḥ katham iti atas apratyakṣa abhimatāt ‘puruṣaḥ eva idam sarvam aiti vā adṛṣṭa nirdiṣṭāt uta amṛta tvasya aiti vā deva manuṣya loka bhedena prapañcāt ekā ekasmāt samastāt ca vṛddhataraḥ puruṣaḥ tena asmin parimitānām viruddha abhimatānām api anante na samāveśaḥ na yujyate tad eva jyāyaḥ tvam darśayati pādaḥ asya viśvā iti kṛtsnaḥ api tāvat bhūta prapañcaḥ asya kanīyān bhāgaḥ iti kim punar pratyekam tathā hi tri pāt aiva aparimitam anantam maraṇa ādi bhūta prapañca dharma śūnyam rūpam ‘di vi apradyota avasthāyām vartate pramoda avasthāyām vā sūrya maṇḍale dyusthāne vā tatra hi tad upāsyam tad hi tasya upalabdhi sthānam iti tatra iti ucyate aparaḥ kalpaḥ kalpite api kārya bheda ādi avasthāyāḥ vā kāraṇa bhede kim iti na kārya antaramḷ kim iti vā na saṃkaraḥ viparītāḥ vā vyavasthāḷ bhede api payasaḥ tilebhyaḥ eva tailam na sikatābhyaḥḷ bhinā api ca eka kāryāḥ aviparītam ca kāryam tanmātreṇa tad siddheḥ aprāmāṇikāḥ bhāvānām bhāva kalpanā iti syāt etad  vahneḥ api śakti bheda nibandhanaḥ kārya bhedaḥ tad na ekasmāt anekam kāryam tatra yadi vahniḥ api kāraṇam katham na ekasmāt anekam kāryamḷ atha śaktīnām eva kāraṇa tvam abhipraiti tatra ucyate ekasya aneka kārya yoga virodhāt śakti bhedaḥ kalpyate yadi ca ekasya aneka saṃbandha virodhaḥ katham nānā
