sāmarthyena kāryatvāt niyogasya tad pradhānam iti atra ucyate yadi puruṣaḥ  adhigate viṣaye vacaḥ prayuṅkte iti viniyoga viṣaya tā tasya kalpyate pramāṇa antara apekṣa tvāt tarhi saṃbhavat pramāṇa antaraḥ asya viṣayaḥ na tu saṃbhavat pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvāt puruṣa vacaḥ api sa apekṣam sa apekṣa tva nimitta tvāt tadvidhasya viṣayasya sva upalabdhi khyāpanāya puruṣasya gīḥ tatas tasyām pramāṇa antara saṃbhedaḥ mayā upalabdhaḥ ayam arthaḥ aiti arthaḥ tena tatra upalabdhe saṃbhava asaṃbhavau  eva apekṣyeyātām yatra upalabdheḥ niścayaḥ saṃbhavati asya upalabdhiḥ na ca anupalabhya ayam bravīti iti tatra prāmāṇyam yathā āpta puruṣasya pramāṇa viṣaye yatra tu upalabdheḥ asaṃbhavaḥ eva yathā dṛṣṭa arthe buddha ādi vākye yatra ca anupalabhya api vacana pravṛtti saṃbhāvanā tatra aprāmāṇyāt na tu pramāṇa antara saṃbhavāt puruṣa vacane api tad apekṣāḥ atas eva pauruṣeya tva apauruṣeya tve sa apekṣa tva anapekṣa tva kāraṇe nyāya vidbhiḥ daśite pauruṣeya tva nirākaraṇa prayatnena autpattikaḥ tu śabdasya arthena saṃbandhaḥa iti autpattike śabda artha sambandhe asvātantryāt śabdasya na puruṣa buddhi pūrvakatvam iti na pramāṇa antara saṃbhinnā śabdāt artha avagatiḥ iti nirapekṣa tvam nanu pramāṇa antara asaṃbhave api kṛtaḥ eva yatnaḥ sat saṃprayoge iti satyam codanā eva pramāṇam na anyat  iti avadhāraṇa siddhaye na tu pramāṇam eva iti atha pramāṇa antara saṃbhave api yadi codanā prāmāṇyam na vyāhanyate kaḥ arthaḥ pramāṇa antara nirākaraṇenaḷ dharma tattva jñānam pramāṇa antara saṃbhave hi sarva jña abhimata buddha ādi upadiṣṭaḥ api dharmaḥ pratīyeta tatra na dharma tattvam avadhāritam syāt tad avadhāraṇa arthaḥ ca ayam yatnaḥ codanā prāmāṇyam api tad artham mṛgyate na adṛṣṭāya athavā tad virodhāt codanāyāḥ bādhaḥ syāt saṃśayaḥ vā tulya bala tve tena tasya asaṃbhavaḥ pratipādyate na tu tad saṃbhavāt sa apekṣatā iti nanu tad abhāvaḥ apekṣaṇīyaḥ syāt kāmam na tu śabdaḥ pramāṇa antara apekṣam artham pratipādayati yatas yad arthasya pratipādakam na tu tad apekṣyate yad apekṣyate na tad artham pratipādayati na hi virodhi pramāṇa abhāvaḥ pratipatti hetuḥ virodha saṃbhava mātreṇa ca aprāmāṇye pratyakṣa ādīnām api tad syāt api ca virodhi saṃbhavāt aprāmāṇyam kārya niṣṭha tve api aparihāryam kartavyatā dvāreṇa bhūta artha pratipatteḥ iṣṭa tvāt tatra tu pramāṇa antara virodhi saṃbhāvanāt bhūta arthasya pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvāt tena kārya niṣṭhatā varṇyate pramāṇa antara viṣaya tve kila anuvāda tvāt pramāṇa antara apekṣam artham pratipādayati pramāṇa antareṇa ayam adhigataḥ iti na svātantryeṇa kārya niṣṭha tve tu svātantryeṇa tasya pramāṇa antara agocara tvāt uktena prakāreṇa na sa apekṣa tvam iti bhūta artham api sa apekṣam na atas apuruṣa buddhi jam aiti suṣṭhu uktam yadi matam ākhyāta padārtham antareṇa na nāma padārthānām saṃsargaḥ kriyā hi padārtha saṃśleṣa hetuḥ tad abhāve sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt atas siddhaḥ arthaḥ brahmādiḥ na śabda gocaraḥ padasya avidita saṃgati tvena anavabodhaka tvāt  na vākya arthaḥ tasya saṃsarga ātmaka tvāt kriyā rahitānām ca padārthānām asaṃsargāt evam api kriyā abhyupeyatām tad dvāreṇa ca padārtha saṃsarga siddhiḥ āśāsyatām na vidheḥ kaścid arthaḥ sā api ca kriyā sarvatra sulabhā eva aśrūyamāṇā api astyādiḥ astiḥ bhavantī paraḥ prathama puruṣaḥ aprayujyamānaḥ api gamyate iti tatra brahma svarūpa pratipatti param vākyam asti artha niṣṭham tad nibandhanaḥ tatra padārtha saṃśleṣaḥ sattāyāḥ ca prakṛtyā eva sat pradhāna tvāt tad dvāreṇa viśiṣṭa vastu siddhiḥ iti atra āhuḥ na pramāṇau  agamya tāyāḥ anyā kācana sattā tathā hi yad pramāṇena avagamyate tatra astia iti vyavahāraḥ laukikānām viparyaye ‘nāsti iti na khalu anyaḥ sat asat vibhāga hetuḥ lakṣyate artha kriyā bhāva abhāvau ced na tayoḥ api pramāṇa bhāva abhāva adhīna tvāt tathā hi kārye api sat vyavahāraḥ  yadi kārya antara nibandhanaḥ anavasthā tasmāt ante api pramāṇāt eva sat vyavahāraḥ tad viparyayāt ca asat vyavahāraḥ evam ced ādau  eva pramāṇa abhāva abhāva nibandhanau sat asat vyavahārau stām tathā ca asti artha niṣṭham vākyam pramāṇa antara apekṣam eva artham bodhayati pramāṇa viṣaya tāyāḥ asti artha tvāt atra ucyate na pramāṇau  agamya tvam asti arthaḥ na astia iti buddheḥ tad viṣayaḥ yatas pramāṇāt eva tridhā buddhiḥ bhavati dhūmāt asti atra agniḥ ‘nadī pūra viśeṣāt abhūt vṛṣṭiḥ ‘megha udaya viśeṣāt bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥa iti tatra yadi buddhiḥ pramāṇa viṣaya tām gocarayati pramite hi syāt na pramāṇāt eva na hi prāk pramāṇa utpatteḥ san pramāṇa saṃbandhaḥ pramāṇa saṃbandha nibandhanā ca iyam buddhiḥ atha vaiyātyāt uttara kāla tām eva asyāḥ brūyāt traividhyam anupapannam pramāṇa saṃbandhasya abhedāt bhinna kāleṣu api artheṣu atha matam ātma saṃbandhi tayā eva pramāṇena arthaḥ avagamyate atas na asti aiti buddheḥ uttara kāla tā pramāṇa saṃbandha viṣayāyāḥ api sva ātma saṃbandhi tayā eva arthasya pratīteḥ evam api asti iti eva sarvatra syāt na traividhyam sarvasya pramitau pramāṇa saṃbandhasya vartamāna tvāt na ca ittham pramāṇa antara vyapekṣa tvam asti artha niṣṭhe vacasi tad pramāṇa saṃbandhasya eva asti artha tvāt atha matam pramāṇa antara gamya tā eva liṅgena adhigamyate tena na uttara kālatā tad ca pramāṇam tri kālam iti traividhyam kim punar tatḷ pratyakṣam tathā hi bhūtāyām dṛṣṭau kasyacid bhūtam pratyakṣam bhaviṣyantyām bhaviṣyat  vartamāne agnau vartamānam iti etad ca vārtam nitya anumeye tasya abhāvāt api ca liṅgam api evam pramāṇa antara apekṣa tvāt apramāṇam syāt  atha liṅgāt eva pramāṇa antara sadbhāvasya siddheḥ nirapekṣa tvam tathā hi pramāṇa antara sadbhāvaḥ eva idānīm liṅgam pramāṇam na ca tatra anyat apekṣyate pramāṇa sadbhāva dvārā prameya siddhiḥ iti na ayam vidhiḥ vede daṇḍa vāritaḥ vaidikam api vacaḥ asti artha niṣṭham viśiṣṭa artha pramāṇa sadbhāvaḥ eva pramāṇam tatra nirapekṣam tad pramāṇa dvārā ca viśiṣṭa artha siddhiḥ iti samānam syāt matam yuktam liṅgasya prāmāṇyam evam arthe tasya pramāṇa antarasya saṃbhavāt saṃbhavati hi vṛṣṭi ādiṣu pramāṇa antaram tatas tad dvāra artha gatiḥ na tu sarva viśeṣa atīte brahmaṇi āmnāya eka nibandhane abhyupagamyate tatra yathā eva buddha ādi vākyānām eva m ayam puruṣaḥ vedaḥ iti jñāna niṣṭhānām atīndriya arthe jñānasya asaṃbhavāt na arthe prāmāṇyam atīndriya artha upadeśinām tathā atra api syāt  saṃbhavi pramāṇa viṣaya āpta vacana vat tu liṅgasya pramāṇa niṣṭha tve api yujyate prāmāṇyam tad asat brahmaṇi api sākṣātkaraṇasya abhyupagamāt avidyā saṃhāre avidyāvatām tu tadāmnāya eka nibandhanam ucyate api ca yadi ca liṅgena pramāṇam eva mīyate mīyamāna tā eva ca sattā tatra pramīyamāṇa tvāt pramāṇam sarvam sat eva sat ca vartamānam iti ucyate tatra vartamāna tvāt pramāṇasya sarvatra arthe astia iti eva syāt na pramāṇa traividhyāt arthe traividhyam mīyamānasya sattvāt sataḥ ca vartamāna tvāt iti api ca idam ayam praṣṭavyaḥ kim vartamāna pramāṇa yogaḥ pramāṇa saṃbandhaḥ sattā tad viparyayaḥ asattā āhosvit  pramāṇa yoga mātram anāśrita kāla viśeṣamḷ tatra na smaryamāṇasya vartamāna pramāṇa saṃbandhaḥ nanu smaryamāṇe vināśa saṃbhavāt na eva astia iti vyavahāraḥ satyam na asti iti api na asti yadi vartamāna pramāṇa yogaḥ sattā tad viparyayaḥ asattā na asti iti eva syāt na ca ‘asti iti tasmāt anye sat asat tve anāśrita kāla viśeṣe pramāṇa yoga mātre sattve pramita naṣṭam api vastu sat iti tena artha kriyā prasaṅge anaṣṭena iva sattva aviśeṣāt naṣṭānaṣṭayoḥ viśeṣāt na evam iti ced saḥ eva tarhi viśeṣaḥ sat asat vyavahāra vyavasthāyāḥ hetuḥ kārya vyavasthāyāḥ iva na pramāṇa yogaḥ tad anusāriṇī eva eṣā dṛśyate loke na khalu pramita naṣṭam sat aiti upacarati lokaḥ kim ca pramite arthe sat asat tve jijñāseran na punar laukikāḥ siddha tvāt pramāṇa yoga mātrasya tad lakṣaṇa tvāt ca sattvasya atha matam na vartamāna pramāṇa yogaḥ sattā nānā āśrita kālam tad yoga mātram api tu pramāṇam prati yogyatā sā ca naṣṭāt cyutā iti na tasya sattva prasaṅgaḥ smaryamāṇe tu kutaścid cyutā kutaścid na iti na sarvasya asattvam iti etad api na sundaram abhyupagata hānāt tathā hi ittham artha svabhāvaḥ eva sattā varṇitā bhavati pramāṇa yogyaḥ artha svabhāvaḥ sattā artha svabhāva nibandhanaḥ eva sat asat vyavahāra vibhāgaḥ na pramāṇa tad abhāva upādhiḥ tasya tu eṣa kathana upāyaḥ na pramāṇa saṃsparśaḥ yathā nīla ākāra jñāna yogyaḥ arthaḥ  nīlaḥ aiti ākhyāte api na nīla śabdaḥ nīla jñāna upādhiḥ tathā ca saḥ asti śabdena abhidhīyate iti artha svabhāva niṣṭham asti artha pradhānam vākyam iti kutas sa apekṣa tvamḷ pramāṇasya asaṃsparśāt syāt etad bhinnāḥ eva artha svabhāvāḥ pramāṇam prati yogyāḥ sat śabda vācyāḥ santu na ekā sattā mā bhūt na etad sādhyam sarvathā artha svabhāva abhidhāyyasti śabdaḥ na pramāṇa yoga nimittaḥ iti pramāṇa saṃsparśe hi sa apekṣatā syāt aneka tā tu na kañcid doṣam āvahati api ca yadi tasya anekatvam katham abhinna śabda pravṛttiḥḷ tathā hi bhinneṣu abhinnam viśeṣaṇam upalakṣaṇam vā aśritya ekaḥ śabdaḥ varteta bhinna nimittaḥ vā sādhāraṇa śabdaḥ syāt akṣa ādi vat tatra na tāvat ananta artha svabhāveṣu sādhāraṇa tvam upapadyate saṃbandha grahaṇa sāmarthyāt parimita jāti viṣayāḥ hi akṣa ādi śabdāḥ parimita upalakṣaṇa lakṣitāḥ vā syuḥ syāt etad dravya tva ādi sāmānya traya upalakṣitānām arthānām sat śabdaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ iti tad na yaḥ hi sattām avajānīte sa dravya tva ādīni api avajānītaḥ eva na kila tejaḥ dṛṣṭavataḥ apsu tad avamarśaḥ bhavati api ca sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyā api santaḥ eva na teṣu aupacārikaḥ sat śabdaḥ pratyayasya availakṣaṇyāt na ca sāmānyāt vinā upacāraḥ sati vā sāmānye tad eva sat śabda arthaḥ tad eva ca sattā tulya tvāt pratyayasya atha matam sarva pravādeṣu sarva padārthāḥ parimitaiḥ kaiścid dharmaiḥ upasaṃgṛhītāḥ tad upalakṣaṇānām anantānām api arthānām sat iti sādhāraṇaḥ śabdaḥ tad ayuktam saṃgrahaḥ hi na ekam antareṇa tatra yadi sat śabda artha tayā sat śabda tāyām edition saṃgrahaḥ etāvat prabhedaḥ sat śabda arthaḥ aiti na artha antara nivṛttiḥ syāt tatra na sarva artha saṃgrahaḥ syāt yathā navavidhaḥ gaḥ śabda arthaḥ aiti na anyeṣām abhāvaḥ eva tatra na pravādebhyaḥ kācid artha tattva avagatiḥ syāt nanu na pravādānām arthavat tā sādhyā na brūmaḥ pravādānām arthavat tā sādhyeti kim tu pratipadyante pravādinaḥ kañcid artha svabhāvam ekam yasya ayam pañca ṣaṭ aityādi prabheda saṃgrahaḥ yatas  na ekam antareṇa upasaṃgrāhakam avāntara saṃkhyānām niveśaḥ atha etāvān pramāṇa yogyaḥ artha kriyā sāmarthyaḥ vā iti pramāṇa yogya tve artha kriyā sāmarthye vā saṃgrahaḥ tābhyām eva sat śabda arthaḥ upalakṣyatām vyarthaḥ parimita dharma upanyāsaḥ tatra sāmānya śabda tā eva syāt na sādhāraṇa śabda tā bhinna nimitta tve ca akṣa ādi śabdebhyaḥ iva nimitta bhedāt saṃśayaḥ syāt na viśeṣa pratītiḥ na hi san ghaṭaḥ iti nimitta bhedeṣu pratipattāraḥ saṃśerate yathā eva śuklaḥ paṭaḥ aiti nirākāṅkṣaḥ tathā ‘san ghaṭaḥa iti api yaḥ tu dravyam guṇaḥ karma rūpam vijñānam iti vā saṃśayaḥ na sa laukikānām laukikāḥ tu abhinnam eva nimittam pratipadyante arthāt ca saṃdehaḥ na śabdāt  kutas ḷ viśeṣa pratītim antareṇa api pratipattuḥ naiḥ ākāṅkṣyāt yatra hi artha sāmarthyena saṃśayaḥ yathā vṛkṣaḥ chidyatām iti paraśu kuṭhāra ādiṣu tatra anyatara viśeṣa an avagame api nairākāṅkṣam yasya kasyacid upādānāt anyathā anavasthānāt yatra tu śabdāt tatra viśeṣa avagama hetoḥ vinā sa ākāṅkṣa tvam eva tad evam na nānā nimittaḥ sādhāraṇa śabdaḥ viśeṣaṇam api ekam pramāṇam syāt tad ca prāk api tatas  sat śabda anuviddha buddhi utpādāt anupapannam iti uktam mānāt eva yatas buddhiḥ iti prapañcena api ca kāryāt api vṛttam eva pramāṇam avasīyate tatra kutas tad viśiṣṭa tā na khalu arthaḥ asat nihita viśeṣa guṇaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ bhavati na ca niścite viśeṣaṇa abhāve viśiṣṭa abhidhāna anuviddhaḥ saṃśayaḥ bhavati daṇḍa abhāva niścayaḥ iva daṇḍī na vā iti bhavati ca śūnya nagara ādiṣu cira nikhāta nidhiṣu pramāṇa abhāva niścaye api santi na aiti saṃśayaḥ tasmāt anyaḥ pramāṇa yogāt sad arthaḥ yatra eṣa saṃśayaḥ na api upalakṣaṇam pramāṇam pramita dhvasteṣu sat śabdā prayogāt smaryamāṇe ca sat śabda anuviddhāt saṃdehāt vṛtta pramāṇa saṃbandhasya pramāṇa upalakṣita tvāt sattvam eva syāt na asattvam na saṃśayaḥ yaḥ api artha kriyayā sat śabda artham viśinaṣṭi upalakṣayati vā tasya api prāc kārya darśanāt na sat śabda yogaḥ syāt atha pramāṇa jananam eva artha kriyām brūyāt pramāṇāt eva asti buddhiḥ na syāt atha vaikalpikīyam pramāṇa uttara kālatā iti matam liṅgāt na syāt atha nirjñāta kārya saṃbandham eva liṅgena anugamyate evam tarhi prameya abhāvaḥ tathā hi kāryavat tā hi asti arthaḥ sā ca adhigatā eva kārya vat tayā eva kāryavat tau  agamyate iti acatur asram kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca yaugapadya abhāvāt viśiṣṭa tā anupapattiḥ atha upalakṣaṇam atītasya api sattva prasaṅgaḥ smaryamāṇe ca saṃśayaḥ na syāt iti uktam tasmāt yathā eva nīla ādi śabda arthaḥ artha svabhāvaḥ na kārya lakṣyaḥ na pramāṇa lakṣyaḥ anavasthānāt sva rūpa vyavasthaḥ tu yathāpramāṇam avasīyate tathā sat artha svabhāvaḥ api iti yuktam kārya pramāṇa sat asadbhāva nibandhane hi sat asat vyavahāra vibhāge tasya apravṛttiḥ eva kārya viṣaya tvam na ayam aparicchedaḥ sati eva arthe hetu vaikalya nimittaḥ samagra tvāt tad hetūnām tasmāt artha abhāvāt iti yadi matam yatra bhū bhāga ādau caraṇa nyāsa ādi lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ tasya tatra na tāvat svarūpeṇa miśre api tasya bhāvāt viśeṣaṇa yogena kaivalye prāptā kīṭa kaṇṭaka ādi abhāva viśiṣṭa paricchedāt pada nyāsa ādi lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ yatas na anya abhāvāt viśeṣaṇa m anyādṛśam iti uktam nanu na asti aityayam arthaḥ ‘nedam pramīyate iti na punar abhāvaḥ avagamyate viruddham idam na asti avagamyate ca iti yadi evam pramāṇa abhāvaḥ viṣayaḥ uktaḥ syāt na asti iti dhī śabdayoḥ tatra kaḥ aparādhaḥ syāt prameya abhāvasya yena tam ati laṅghya pramāṇa abhāvaḥ viṣayaḥ ucyateḷ na hi tayoḥ nirupākhya tve kaścid viśeṣaḥ atha matam na eva stām na asti iti buddhi vyavahārau katham paśyāmi aiti vibhramaḥ na hi tamaḥ nāma kiñcid dṛśyam asti na etad sāram yadi khalva darśane viparyaya darśana bhramaḥ bhavati suṣupta ādi avasthāsu viśva abhāva darśana bhramaḥ syāt āloka adarśana tā doṣaḥ pramāṇa antara saṃbhedasya abhāvāt  pramāṇa yogyaḥ aiti etāvat mātra adhigateḥ tathā hi ye api pramāṇa yogya tām sattām āhuḥ na tad vyatirekiṇīm te api na atra antara artha saṃsparśam icchanti tad saṃsparśe hi anyat pramāṇam anveṣyam syāt katham na anveṣyamḷ yadā vacaḥ pramāṇa yogya tāyām paryavasitam na viśiṣṭa artha sattvam bodhayati tatra yasya pramāṇasya yogyaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ arthaḥ tad avaśya apekṣaṇīyam kim artham tad apekṣyateḷ viśiṣṭa vastu sattva adhigamāya kam punar viśiṣṭasya vastunaḥ sattvamḷ pramāṇa yogya tvam adhigatam eva tarhi tad asti artha niṣṭhāt vacanāt pramāṇa yogya tāyāḥ asti artha tvāt pramāṇa antara saṃbheda abhyupagame api na aprāmāṇya prasaṅga doṣaḥ iti darśayati na khalu pramāṇa antara saṃbhinna artham api vacaḥ na pramāṇam pramāṇam eva hi āpta vākyam iti arthe apramāṇam yathā atīndriya arthe buddha vacaḥ puruṣasya darśana asaṃbhavāt yathā uktam puruṣa aśaktitaḥ tatra sa apavāda tva saṃbhavaḥ iti yathā ca vipralambhaka vākyam ayathā dṛṣṭa artha
