etad śravaṇāt pravṛttaḥ iti yathā gāmānaya iti sāsnādi mada ānayana darśanāt tad pratyayam anumāya tatra saṃbandha grahaṇam iti yadi pravṛtti unnīyamāna pratyaya viśeṣaṇa tvena vyavasthitaḥ  anumeyaḥ vidhāyaka arthaḥ saṃbandha jñāna viṣayaḥ na tarhi śabda eka pramāṇakaḥ atha anumānam śabda pūrvakam iti tathā ucyate śābdaḥ api pratyayaḥ anumāna pūrvakaḥ iti anumāna eka gocaraḥ syāt na khalu bīja aṅkurayoḥ iva ānayoḥ ekasya prāthamyam vyavasthāpayitum śakyam śabda avagatasya anumānāt anumitasya vidita saṃgateḥ śabdāt avagamāt api ca sarva pratipattṝṇām anumāna pūrvā śabdāt pratipattiḥ iti teṣām śabdaḥ anuvādakaḥ eva tathā hi śabdāt buddhyamānaḥ anumitam vidita saṃgatim budhyate sarva pratipattā na tu anumimānaḥ śabda avagatam anumimīte nanu śabda avagataḥ eva anumīyate satyam anena tu pratipattrā na ca anyadīyā pratipattiḥ anya pratipattim anuvādīkaroti pravṛtti hetu mātre ca saṃbandha vyutpatteḥ tanmātram śabda arthaḥ syāt na ca ālaukikaḥ kalpayitum api śakyaḥ laukikāt api pravṛtti siddheḥ syāt etad vaidikīṣu pravṛttiṣu tad asaṃbhavāt alaukika kalpanā na etad  loka avagata sāmarthyaḥ hi śabdaḥ vede api pratipādakaḥ tatra laukikīṣu pravṛttiṣu laukike vidita saṃbandhe vede api tad pratipattiḥ eva syāt asaṃbhave vā mithyātvam atha bahuvidha tvāt pravṛtti hetūnām vyabhicārāt aśabda artha tve pravṛtti hetu sāmānyam śabda arthaḥ tatra vede laukikānām viśeṣaṇānām asaṃbhavāt alaukikam viśeṣa antaram pratīyate evam api yaḥ śabda arthaḥ vede sāmānyam sa loka siddhaḥ iti na anuvāda tā vyāvartate padārtha antara vat yaḥ api viśeṣaḥ saḥ anya asaṃbhavena pariśeṣa anumāna gocaraḥ iti na pramāṇa antara aviṣaya tvam na ca pariśeṣa anumānam api śreyaḥ sādhana tāyāḥ saṃbhavāt atha matam loka vyavahāraḥ iva veda vyavahāraḥ api anādiḥ tatra vaidikīṣu pravṛttiṣu laukika pravṛtti hetu abhāvāt alaukike tu pravṛtti hetau vaidikānām vidhāyakānām saṃbandha jñānam na ca anumeya tvam tad pratyayasya pravṛttyā anumānāt tad siddhiḥ tu tad pratyaya sāmarthyena eva sa ca pratyayaḥ śabda utthaḥ iti ananya pramāṇa tā na ca laukikasya eva śreyaḥ sādhana tvasya saṃbhavaḥ iti yuktam laukikī hi pramāṇa antarau  agamyā śreyaḥ sādhana tā tatra prayoga darśanāt liṅā ādeḥ tad anusāreṇa ca śabda artha avadhāraṇāt pramāṇa antara gamya tā api śabda artha anupraveśinī atra ucyate bhavatu nāma veda vyavahārāt eva śabda artha anugamaḥ tathā api na pramāṇa antara gocara tā vyāvartate tathā hi alaukike pravṛtti hetau śabdasya sāmarthya jñāna kāle pramitaḥ vā syāt na vāḷ pramitaḥ ced śabda saṃbandhasya tadā eva jñāyamāna tvāt avaśyam pramāṇa antareṇa iti vācyam atha na pramitaḥ katham tatra saṃbandha jñānamḷ na hi apramitayoḥ saṃbandhinoḥ tad āśrayaḥ saṃbandhaḥ pramātum śakyaḥ yaḥ api manyate śaktiḥ hi śabdasya saṃbandhaḥ sā ca na arthe tasya vyavasthita tvāt pratyayaḥ tu tasya kāryaḥ sa ca pravṛttyā anumitaḥ tatra eva sāmarthya lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ pramīyate iti saḥ idam praṣṭavyaḥ kim pratyaya mātre sāmarthyam gṛhyate atha viśiṣṭe pravṛtti hetu pratyayeḷ yadi pratyaya mātre yad kiñcit tatas pratīyeta atha viśiṣṭe laukika vyatirikta pravṛtti hetu pratyaye pravṛtti pariśeṣābhyām tasya anumita tvāt prāptam pramāṇa antara gocara tvam dvayī hi viśeṣaṇasya gatiḥ smārta ākṛṣṭam viśiṣṭa pramitau  aṅga tvam eti yathā agnimān dhūmāt iti viśiṣṭa grāhi pramāṇa prameyam vā yathā śuklaḥ gauḥ iti ubhayathā ca pramāṇa antara viṣayaḥ śabdasya anadhigata saṃbandha tvāt smārta ākṛṣṭa tve pramāṇa antaram anveṣyam dvitīye api kalpe viśiṣṭa pratyaya anumāna anumita tvāt atha anumānasya pratyayaḥ eva prāmāṇyam pratīti mātram tu tatra viśeṣaṇasya tāvatā ca tad viśiṣṭa pratīti aṅgam viśeṣaṇa pramitiḥ tu anumitāt pratyayāt yathā puruṣa vacanāt viśiṣṭa artha pramāṇe anumite artha siddhiḥ tatas eva pramāṇāt tatra hi arthaḥ pratīti mātreṇa eva vaktṛ jñānasya viśeṣaṇam tad etad apeśalam smṛti pramāṇa saṃśaya viparyāsa vikalpa antargamāt pratīteḥ tatra alaukika viśeṣaṇa pratītiḥ na smṛtiḥ prāc anadhigateḥ na saṃśayaḥ koṭi dvaya saṃsparśa abhāvāt na vikalpaḥ pravṛtti hetu pratyayasya api tathā prasaṅgāt tathā na viparyāsaḥ katham hi tatra yathārtha tve tathābhūta grāhiṇī tad pratītiḥ artha śūnyā syātḷ pariśeṣāt pramāṇam para jñānena ca paraḥ pratipadyate iti subhāṣitam atha matam na para jñānena paraḥ pratipadyate kim tu sva jñānena eva para jñāna sāmarthyāt atha tasya sva jñānam katamat pramāṇam iti vācyam na tāvat chābdam śabda vijñānāt arthe vijñānam iti lakṣaṇāt na ca tad śabda jñānāt kutas tarhiḷ śabda uttha jñānāt anumitāt atha tasya prāmāṇye pravṛtti hetu sadbhāva siddhiḥ prāmāṇyam ca tasya doṣa rahita śabda udbhavāt tena śabdasya tatra prāmāṇyam ucyate tad adhīnaḥ tatra artha niścayaḥ iti tad api asāṃpratam śabdāt artha jñānam śābdam iti lakṣaṇāt puruṣa vacanam api na arthe na pramāṇam kim tu jñāna viśeṣaṇe dvayī ca viśeṣaṇasya gatiḥ uktā tatra smṛti asaṃbhavāt pramīyamāṇaḥ eva sa viśiṣṭa artha pramiti aṅgam anyathā arthe pramāṇa antaram anveṣyam syāt na ca vaktṛ jñānena eva artha siddhiḥ para jñānena na paraḥ pratipadyate iti uktam yad tu uktam vaktṛ jñāna adhīna artha siddhiḥ iti tad tad mithyā tve tad asaṃbhave vā pramāṇa pratīti bādhane artha pratīteḥ api bādhanāt tad abādhe ca ābādhāt  na tu vacasaḥ arthaḥ na viṣayaḥ anyathā pramāṇa antara paratantram puruṣa vacaḥ arthe sa apekṣam iti etad eva na syāt na hi yaḥ yasya aviṣayaḥ sa tatra sa apekṣaḥ anapekṣaḥ vā tathā ca prāmāṇya sthāpanam tu syāt vaktṛ dhīhetu saṃbhavāt iti uktam sthāpanam abādhaḥ na tu prāmāṇyam eva tad ca vaktṛdhī hetu saṃbhavāt vākyasya na tu vaktṛ dhiyaḥ eva śabdasya ca arthena saṃbandhaḥ na tu jñānena evam hi uktam autpattikaḥ tu śabdasya arthena saṃbandhaḥa iti artha grahaṇam atra artha asaṃspaśī śabdaḥ jñānena eva śabdasya saṃbandhaḥ iti paśyatām nirākaraṇāya tasmāt anyonya yogya tā śabda arthayoḥ eva saṃbandhaḥ na ca apramite arthe sa śakyaḥ grahītum pramite pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvam uktam na ca pratīti mātre arthavatyāḥ pratīteḥ smṛti pramāṇayoḥ anyataratra antargamāt ānarthakye kena saṃbandhaḷ yadi ca śābda pratīti vyatirekiṇyā api pratītyā sa viṣayīkriyate apramāṇa ātmikayā api bhavati ayam aśābdasya api jñānasya gocara iti pramāṇa antara āśaṅkā kena vāryateḷ na ca pramāṇa antara avagamyatā śabda artham anupraviśati yatas na anvaya mātreṇa vyatireka mātreṇa vā śabda arthaḥ sati hi anyasmin prayojake arthe yasya abhāve na prayogaḥ saḥ api tasya śabdasya prayojakaḥ iti gamyate yathā satsu hetu antareṣu yasya abhāve na kāryam saḥ api hetuḥ gamyate iha ca śreyaḥ hetu vivakṣāyām liṅga ādeḥ darśanāt tad abhāve sati api pramāṇa antara gamya tve adarśanāt śreyaḥ hetu tvam tāvat śabda arthaḥ pramāṇa antara gamya tve yadi api darśanam tad abhāve ca yadi api adarśanam na tu śreyaḥ hetu tve sati pramāṇa antara gamya tāyāḥ abhāvāt tatra saṃdigdhaḥ vyatirekaḥ ubhaya abhāve aprayogāt  kiṃnibandhanaḥ aprayogaḥ iti tatra śreyaḥ sādhana tāyāḥ prayojaka tvasya avadhārita tvāt tad abhāve tad nibandhanaḥ iti gamyate tanmātreṇa anvaya vyatireka upapattau na anyasya śabda artha tve pramāṇam anyathā śiṃśapā śabda arthe sattva ādayaḥ api anupraviśeyuḥ teṣu satsu prayogāt tad abhāve ca aprayogāt atha śiṃśapātu asya śabda artha tvāt tad abhāva nibandhanaḥ eva sattā ādya bhāve aprayogaḥ tad sadbhāvāt ca prayogaḥ upapadyate iti na teṣu sāmarthya kalpanā samānam etad atra api atha śreyaḥ hetutvasya pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvāt tasya ca vede asaṃbhavāt aprāmāṇyam tad asat na hi yaḥ ekatra yasya pramāṇasya gocaraḥ saḥ anyatra api mithyā samīpe hi bahis indriya viṣayaḥ dūre tu āgama anumāna gamyaḥ tathā yāga ādiṣu viprakṛṣṭa kāla phaleṣu vedau  agamyam śreyaḥ sādhana tvam bhaviṣyati na ca pramāṇa antara anupalabdhyā pramāṇa antara gamyaḥ bādhyate viṣaya vyavasthayā api pramāṇa pravṛtteḥ atha pramāṇa antara viṣaya tve tad virodhāt aprāmāṇyam anantara phala anupalabdheḥ tad aviṣaye tu śabda arthe na tad virodhaḥ iti syāt yadi virodhaḥ syāt na ca asau ānantaryam hi acoditam iti uktam atha mā bhūt ānantarya codanā mā ca bhūt pramāṇa antara avagamyatā śabda arthaḥ sarvathā pramāṇa antara siddhaḥ ced padārthaḥ āśrīyate sa yathā siddhi āśrayaṇīyaḥ anyathā na tad siddhaḥ syāt anantara śreyaḥ hetu tā ca tad siddhā tad na na tāvat anantara phala sādhana tā niyogataḥ karmaṇām kṛṣi auṣadha pāna ādiṣu anyathā api darśanāt avāntara kāryasya yāga ādau  api pramāṇa sāmarthyena siddheḥ api ca viśiṣṭa siddhau viśeṣaṇam api śreyaḥ hetutva mātram siddham tāvat ca śabda arthaḥ na ca tāvati pramāṇa virodhaḥ tad evam laukike api pravṛtti hetau doṣa abhāvāt vyarthāḥ alaukika kalpanā sukha ādi vat ca asya anumeya tvāt tathā hi mukha prasāda ādi unneya saṃvedanāḥ sukha ādayaḥ tena eva sahonnīyante na evam sattve pṛthak pramāṇam arthyate yadā api idam darśanam vaktṛ jñānam eva puruṣa vacana arthaḥ tatra jñānam na artham antareṇa saṃbhavati iti artha āpattyā anumānena vā artha siddhiḥ tadā api pravṛtti pramitaḥ tadhetu pratyayaḥ na tam antareṇa iti āpta vacana artha vat anumeya tā na vyāvartate atha anumāna hrtoḥ pratyayasya śabda sādhana tvāt śabda pramāṇaka tvam tad asat  na āpta vacana artha jñānasya akṣa sādhana tvāt tad arthaḥ śrotuḥ pratyakṣa pramāṇakaḥ bhavati tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate tasya evam anumeya tve katham śabda eka gocaraḥ tathā na sa kalpayitum śakyaḥ tad siddheḥ laukika dapi iti atha ucyate na brūmaḥ vidhiḥ anyathā vṛthā syāt iti tad adhīnaḥ saṃsargaḥ kim tu pramāṇān tmanā eva sa sva śabdena pratipādyate tathā ca pramāṇa tvāt prameyasya ākṣeptā pūrvasya pramāṇa antara anapekṣaḥ ca na hi asau śabdavat saṃbandha apekṣa tvāt pūrva siddhim apekṣate iti evam api avyutpanna pravṛtti pada dharma vyatikramau pramāṇa ātmā api sa yadi na pramāṇa antara siddhaḥ atha siddhaḥ  yathā avagata anuvāda at na apūrva artha ākṣepaḥ api ca yatra asya prāmāṇyam iṣyate śabdasya eva tatra astu kim anenaḷ nanu uktam śabda saṃgati jñāna apekṣa tvāt anuvādakaḥ na apūrva artha avagamāya prabhavati na etad sāram śabdaḥ ced anuvādakaḥ tad prakāśyam pramāṇam api anūdyamānam yathā adhigatam katham apūrva artham bodhayetḷ na prameya saṃsparśa rahitā pramāṇa avagatiḥ atas  yathā adhigata prameyam eva tad pratīyate na ca niyogasya prameyam nirūpyate na tāvat yāga ādayaḥ prameyāḥ teṣām yajati ādi śabda viṣaya tvāt na api teṣām pramāṇa antarasya agocaraḥ saṃsargaḥ tathā hi avidhiṣu api laukikeṣu vākyeṣu śrotuḥ anadhigataḥ  apūrvaḥ saṃsargaḥ pratīyate brāhmaṇa putraḥ te jātaḥ aityādiṣu atha phala sādhana sāmarthyam prameyam ucyate na kila kāminaḥ niyogaḥ  akāma upāye dhātu arthe avakalpate anupāya tve hi tasya na sa kāminyā kṛtaḥ syāt iti tad api asaṃpratam na hi śabdasya tatra kaścid aparādhaḥ yena tam atikramya anyat pramāṇam mṛgyate pramāṇa antara apekṣa tā pratyuktāḥ anantara phala adarśanena tu virodhaḥ  niyoga gamye api tasmin  aviśiṣṭaḥ ānantaryasya apramāṇa artha tvena tad abhāvaḥ śabde api tulyaḥ atha vā śabdaḥ tatra na duṣyati phala sādhana sāmarthye niyogaḥ tu duṣyati eva na hi tatas puruṣartha sādhana avabodhaḥ saṃbhavati tad ca idam vidhi viveka bhāvanā vivekābhyām avagantavyam tasmāt saṃbandha jñāna apekṣa tvena padārtha antaraiḥ samāna tvāt vidhāyaka arthasya na śakyam viśeṣeṇa vaktum tad nibandhanaḥ padārtha saṃsargaḥ iti sarve eva tu padārthāḥ saṃbandha yogyaiḥ kāraka ādi bhāvaiḥ sva padebhyaḥ pratītāḥ sannikarṣeṇa saṃsṛjyante yatas lokāt śabda vyāpāra avagamaḥ loke ca padaiḥ sva arthānām pratipādanam sannikarṣeṇa viśiṣṭa artha para tayā na sva artha mātra pratipatti para tayā tathā ca sarva padārtha ākāṅkṣā nibandhanaḥ eva saṃsargaḥ sarve hi te padaiḥ aparyavasita rūpāḥ sva rūpa mātre prakāśyante evam padārtha antaraiḥ tulya tvāt vidheḥ na viśeṣeṇa tad nibandhanaḥ saṃsargaḥ sarva padārtha nibandhane ca saṃsarge na vidhi abhāvena saṃsargaḥ na upapadyate tad evam na saṃsarga artham api vidhiḥ upāsanīyaḥ katham na upāsanīyaḥ yadā niyoga para tayā eva padānām sva artheṣu saṃsarga jñānamḷ pravartaka vacana antara pravṛtti darśanena hi tad hetu pratyayam anumāya tatra tasya sāmarthyam gamyate na etad apravartake api vākye svarūpa niṣṭhe saṃbandha grahaṇāt  sannidhāpita agni vyatirikta pākya upakaraṇam agni arthinam prati yadā ucyate caitra gṛhe kṛśānuḥa iti tadā tatas tena ānayanam dṛṣṭvā gamyate iha anena agni sattā pratītā sā ca asmāt vākyāt na ca śakyam vaktum tatas ānaya ‘gaccha vā tatra iti vākyāt pratyayaḥ agni sattā mātra pratyayena vākyāt pravṛtti siddheḥ na vākyasya niyojane api sāmarthyam śakyate kalpayitum artha antara anvaye ca prayoga pratyaya upapattau na viśeṣa anvaye pramāṇam anyathā veda arthaḥ niṣpramāṇakaḥ eva syāt iti uktam atha manyate vastu svarūpa mātra jñānam kartavya tā jñāna rahitam pravṛtti nivṛtti śūnyam anarthakam pravṛtti nivṛtti prayuktā hi vākya pravṛttiḥ athaḥ arthavat tvāya vidhiḥ anyathā ānarthakyam tatra ucyate pratipatti vidhau  api tulyam ānarthakyam tathā hi evaṃvidhaḥ pratipattavyaḥ aiti api na tad svarūpa jñāna atiriktā kācana pravṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ vā atha svarūpa jñānam eva prayojanam tad svarūpa mātra niṣṭhe api tulyam atha pratipatti vidhiḥ prajñām kurvīta ‘sa kratum kurvīta ‘a ātmā iti eva upāsita aiti adhikāra vidhi vyapekṣita prajñā upāsanā viṣaya samarpaṇena arthavān na avagata viṣaya svarūpā prajñā śakya iti svarūpa niṣṭham api vacaḥ tathā artha vat tasya samarpaṇe sutarām sāmarthyam nanu evam asya svarūpa niṣṭhā hīyate niyoga anupraveśinaḥ sva gata niyoga niṣṭham api tarhi tad na niyoga antara anupraveśāt atha matam sva artha paryavasitam eva vākyam vākya antareṇa eka vākya tām upaiti saḥ ayam prākaraṇikaḥ saṃbandhaḥ ucyate anyathā vākya lakṣaṇaḥ eva syāt etad api samānam niyoga anupraveśe api na sva rūpa niṣṭhatā hīyate nanu asti niyoga anupraveśaḥ anyathā ānarthakyāt kāmam tattva pratipatti vidhiḥ tu tāvat ānarthakyāt nirākṛtaḥ vidheḥ vinā api tasmāt śabdāt tatva avabodha siddheḥ yad api codyate yathā utpatti vidheḥ karma rūpa pratipatti mātram arthaḥ āgneyaḥ aṣṭa kapālaḥa iti na tatas pravṛttiḥ adhikāra vidhi nibandhana tvāt tasyāḥ tathā tattva avabodha vidheḥ tattva avabodha mātram arthaḥ pravṛttiḥ adhikāra vidheḥ prajñām kurvīta aityādeḥ yatas ca pravṛtti pratipatti prayojana bhedaḥ vidheḥ atas asya lakṣaṇa dvayam āhuḥ ajñāta jñāpanam apravṛtta pravartanam iti etad api asāram yatas na utpatti gatasya vidhāyakasya svarūpa avagama mātram iṣyate phalam api tu adhikāra vākya saṃbandhaḥ tathā hi vidheḥ puruṣa artha mātra sādhana tve avabuddhe tad viśeṣa ākāṅkṣāyām adhikāra saṃbandhaḥ labhyate na ca tattva pratipatti vidheḥ api tad eva phalam yatas yasya adhikāra saṃbandhaḥ upāsana ādi viṣayasya ātma tattvasya tad akriyā ātmat tvāt na vidhi viṣayaḥ yad tu tad viṣayaḥ tattva jñānam tasya na adhikāra saṃbandhaḥ vrīhi ādi pratyakṣa vat na hi vrīhi ādi svarūpa grāhi pramāṇam prayoga eka deśa tām bhajate pramitānām adhikāra saṃbandhāt niṣpannānām iva anaḥ vāsaḥ prabhṛtīnām vānatakṣaṇa ādiḥ hi tad kriyā na adhikāram anupraviśati iti idānīm tṛtīya pratipatti gocaraḥ vidhiḥ parāsyate tattva avabodha viṣaya tvena saṃbandhāt  dvitīya pratipatti viṣayaḥ hi na tattva avabodha viṣayaḥ kim tu tad abhyāsa viṣayaḥ na brūmaḥ śabda utthaḥ tattva bodhaḥ vidhīyate iti kim tu pratyasta mita buddhi bodhya bheda avagrahaḥ atas ca advayaḥ dvitīya tadvidha bodha abhāvāt vā pramātṛ prameya dvaya virahāt vā tatas anyaḥ tasya ca ālaukikasya pramāṇa antarāt utpatti upāyasya anavagamāt saha upāyaiḥ śama dama manana dhyāna brahmacarya ādibhiḥ vidhānam yatas na śābda jñāna viṣayaḥ ātma tattvam vākya lakṣaṇaḥ hi śabdaḥ pramāṇam tasya ca viṣayaḥ nānā padārtha saṃsarga ātmā tad anugamena pratīteḥ tad jñānasya ca vividha artha mātra saṃbheda avabhāsasya ātma tattvam niṣprapañcam dvaita leśena api anavamṛṣṭam katham gocaraḥ syāt iti etad api asāram yatas yaḥ asau  advayaḥ dvaita leśa saṃsparśa vikalaḥ ātma tattva bodhaḥ saḥ avaccheda vibhrānti virahāt tasya svarūpa avasthānam avaccheda kaluṣa tayā hi tad anātma rūpeṇa prakāśate na tu tatas anyaḥ tattva bodhaḥ satyam jñānam anantam iti śruteḥ ātma tattvam ca praśānta śoka ādi viśvāśivam apahata pāpma ādi śruteḥ prakāśamānān atiśaya ānandam vijñānam ānandam brahma ‘eṣaḥ asya paramaḥ ānandaḥ etasya eva ānandasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvanti iti śrutibhyaḥ tathā ca tad svarūpa sthitiḥ viśva aśiva upaśamāt niratiśaya āhlāda avāpteḥ ca suṣṭhu praśānta aparaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ phalam uktam ca ātma lābhāt na param vidyate iti na ca puruṣa arthe api ajñāta upāye na pravartate iti yuktam yatas pravṛtteḥ pūrvarūpam icchā tathā ca tad vāreṇa pravṛtti upadeśa kvacid atha atas dharma jijñāsā tathā yaḥ hi yad icchati sa tad karoti iti uktam api ca ajñāta upāye ced na pravartate avaśyam upāya jñāpanayā tatra pravartyaḥ phalam uddiśya tāvatā ca tatra api pravṛtti siddheḥ na vidhāyakasya tatra vyāpāraḥ āśrayitavyaḥ tad uktam tasya lipsā artha lakṣaṇāa iti tasmāt phala sādhanaḥ eva vidhi vyāpāraḥ nanu phalavatī api artha lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ kva tarhi vidhi vyāpāraḥḷ itthaṃbhāve na etad sāram yatas yathā eva sādhana sāmānye arthāt pravṛttiḥ tathā itthaṃbhāva sāmānye api yatas  na ananugrahakam sādhanam samartham atha tad viśeṣe pravartyaḥ sādhana viśeṣe api tathā astu api ca apekṣita upāya tā eva vidhiḥ tasyāḥ  apravṛtta pravartanā lakṣaṇa tvāt pravṛtti hetoḥ ca dharmasya pravartanā śabda abhidheya tvāt iṣṭa tāyāḥ tad sādhana tāyāḥ ca anyasya pravṛtti hetoḥ abhāvāt iṣṭatāyāḥ ca pramāṇa antara avaseya tvāt svayam pravṛtteḥ jānāti eva asau mayā etad kartavyam iti na iṣṭatāyāma pravṛtta pravartanātvam iṣṭa sādhana tāyām tu pramāṇa antara avagama abhāvāt śabda eka gamyāyām na śabdam antareṇa apravṛtta puruṣa pravṛtti hetu tvam atas sā śabda pramāṇikā satī vidhiḥ iti gīyate anutiṣṭhataḥ ca sādhanam anuṣṭheyam pravṛtti hetuḥ na svabhāva siddham tena anutiṣṭhataḥ sādhana tā vidhiḥ atas anuṣṭhānam sādhana viṣayam eva vidhāyakāt śabdāt gamyate nanu adhyavasāyaḥ ākūtam ādyā pravṛttiḥ kāla traya viyuktam pravṛtti mātram ajñāta kriyā kartṛ saṃbandhaḥ iti vidhi vidaḥ vidhim vyācakṣate na etad sāram yatas adhyavasāya ādīnām eva hetuḥ atra mṛgyate sa ca na anyaḥ apekṣita upāya tāyāḥ na ca te nirasta hetavaḥ syāt etad  abhidhānam eṣām hetuḥ tad ca vārtam abhidhānāt hi pratītiḥ eṣām syāt na utpattiḥ na hi pratīti mātreṇa ghaṭa ādayaḥ pravṛtti hetava ityādi varṇitam vidhi viveke athavā na abhidhānataḥ na ca śabdāt adhi avasāya ādiḥ jñāpaka tvāt avyutpanna pravṛtti prasaṅgāt ityādi tatra eva uktam athavā yaḥ manyate mayā idam kartavyam iti yatas adhyavasāyaḥ ‘niyuktaḥ asmiaiti yatas buddhiḥ sa niyogaḥ  vidhi śabda paryāyaḥ iti tam pratyucyate tatas eva apekṣita upāya tvāt kartavyam aiti dhyavasāyaḥ tathā hi kartuḥ iṣṭa abhyupāye kartavyam aiti loke buddhiḥ tad abhāve tu akartavyam iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām te ca tad viṣaye gamyete tathā niyuktaḥ asmia iti ‘pravartitaḥ asmiaiti sva ātma pravṛtti hetu pratītiḥ na ca saḥ anyaḥ iṣṭa abhyupāya tāyāḥ na khalu dṛṣṭa sāmarthye akasmāt vinā hetunā hetuḥ iti yuktimat na hi tam parityajya laukikam alaukika kalpane pramāṇam asti kutas caḷ na abhidhānataḥ na khalva laukikasya abhidhānam saṃbhavati saṃbandha agrahāt iti uktam atha vā tatas hi adhyavasāya prārambha anuṣṭhāna parisamāpanāḥ apekṣita upāya tvāt tad sadbhāvaḥ eva niyukta pravṛtteḥ yasya kasyacid niyogāt apravṛtteḥ syāt etad kartavyam iti pratyayāt pravartate anyathā kartavyam na kṛtam syāt tad ca na na akasmāt kartavya pratyaya utpādaḥ sa hi sva artha avāpti nimittaḥ syāt etad śabdāt eva kartavyatā buddhiḥ tatra ucyate na abhidhānataḥ na śabdāt kartavya tā buddhiḥ niyogaḥ hi śabda arthaḥ sa hi niyoktṛ dharmaḥ svatantraḥ vā syāt kartavyatā tu viṣaya dharmaḥ atha viṣaya dharmam niyogam brūyāt prāptam apekṣita upāya tvam atha niyogāt kartavya tā syāt evam api na tasyām śabdaḥ pramāṇam sākṣāt tasya niyoga abhidhāyi tvāt na api arthāt akartavye api anāpta niyoga darśanāt atha niyogasya kārya tā gamyate tad niṣpatti adhīnā iti viṣaye kartavyatā avagamaḥ tad asat viṣaye kārya tā pratīteḥ loke tathā hi gauḥ duhyatām tvayāa iti niyoge anyena dugdhāyām na punar doham ārabhate viṣayasya kārya tā pratīteḥ tasya niṣpādita tvāt na ca anyena eva niyogaḥ niṣpāditaḥ tasya aniyukta tvāt tatra niyoga siddhaye punar doha ārambhaḥ syāt vistareṇa ca ayam arthaḥ vidhi viveke vicāritaḥ iti alam ati prasaṅgena syāt etad asya jñānasya mokṣa sādhana tvāt vidhānam vidyā sādhyaḥ hi mokṣaḥ śrūyate vidyayā tadā ārohanti ‘vidyayā amṛtam aśnute ayaḥ tam ātmānam anuvidya vijānāti sa sarvān  ca kāmān tathā ‘sa yadi pitṛ loka kāmaḥ bhavati saṃkalpāt eva asya pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhanti ityādi na ca sādhya tve api antavat tvam śabda gamya tvāt anāvṛtteḥ na ca punar āvartate iti na hi eṣa tarka gamyaḥ yena tarkeṇa asya tattvam vyavasthāpyeta śabda gamyasya tu śabdāt eva tattva vyavasthā ananta vidyā asādhya tvāt vā ananta tvam kṣaṇika tve api ca vijñānasya saṃtati rūpeṇa ananta tvam tatra āhuḥ kaḥ punar eṣa mokṣaḥḷ yadi anāgata deha indriya buddhi anutpādaḥ aśarīram vāvasantam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti darśanāt sa prāgabhāvaḥ na sādhyaḥ atha brahma prāptiḥ sā caitra grāmayoḥ iva vā syāt jīva brahmaṇoḥ mārga śrutibhyaḥ aśatam ca ekā ca hṛdayasya nāḍyaḥ tāsām mūrdhānam abhi nissṛtā ekā tayā ūrdhvamāyan  amṛta tvam eti sa yāvat kṣipyet manaḥ tāvat ādityam gacchati etad vai khalu loka dvāram tathā ‘te arciṣam abhisaṃbhavati arciṣaḥ ahaḥ aityādi yathā vā madhuni nānā kusuma rasānām samudre ca nadīnām prāptiḥ avibhāga lakṣaṇā tathā syāt yathā loke madhukṛtaḥ madhu kurvanti iti ‘yathā somya imāḥ nadyaḥ iti darśanāt kāryasya vā kāraṇa bhāva āpattiḥ tathā vidvān puṇya pāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti aiti śruteḥ tad rūpa pariṇāma lakṣaṇāḥ vā yoga vyāghra vat sa yaḥ ha vai tad paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati iti darśanāt ‘brahma saṃpadyata iti ca sphaṭikasya iva rāga apakarṣaṇena sva rūpa prāpti lakṣaṇā param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti śravaṇāt tatra na tāvat prathamaḥ kalpaḥ sarva gata tvāt tad antarasya sarvasya ‘nityam vibhum sarva gatam iti ananya tvāt ca tad vijñānena sarva vijñāna upadeśāt tad tvam asi iti sākṣāt pratipādanāt pratyagātma vṛttinā ca sarvatra ātma śabdena nirdeśāt ‘atha yaḥ  anyāma iti bheda darśana apavādāt atas eva ca na dvitīyaḥ niravayava tvāt ca niṣkalam niṣkriyam aiti paraspara avayava saṃbheda lakṣaṇasya avibhāgasya anupapatteḥ na api tṛtīyaḥ kāryasya sarvadā kāraṇa tvāt atha kārya rūpa nāśaḥ uccheda ātma tā prasaṅgaḥ mokṣasya tatra vidyayā amṛtam aśnute iti virodhaḥ vidyayā eva uccheda prasaṅgāt ātma ucchedasya ca aniṣṭa tvāt aphala tvam pratiṣiddhaḥ ca akṣaram aityatra mukhyaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ‘vāca ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ nāmadheyam aiti vikāra anṛta tva pratipādanāt śrutyāḥ na caturthaḥ ananya tvāt eva caitanyasya ca brahma rūpasya aviśeṣāt atha vijñāna ātmanām śoka moha ādi abhāvaḥ viśiṣyate iti ced tatra api śoka ādayaḥ ced ātmānaḥ vijñāna ātmanām anucchedyāḥ atha guṇāḥ artha antaram āgama apāyinaḥ kṣaṇikāḥ kṣaṇika tvāt eva ca ucchidyante iti na tad sādhanam apekṣyam na ca āgāminām anutpattaye apekṣyate iti uktam atha aiśvarya viśeṣaḥ  brahmaṇi tad prāptiḥ tad rūpa pariṇāmaḥ mokṣaḥ sa svarāj bhavati iti śruteḥ tad asat aneka īśvara anupapatteḥ brahmaṇaḥ nyūnam samam vā vijñāna ātmanām aiśvaryam syātḷ nyūna tvena brahma rūpāpattiḥ na svārājyam tathā hi brahma śabda vācyaḥ parameśvaraḥ teṣām adhipatiḥ syāt  tathā ca anya rāja tā tatra ca antava tvam śrūyate atha ye anyathā atas viduḥ anya rājānaḥ te kṣayya lokāḥ bhavanti iti upapadyate ca parameśvara icchayā nyūna aiśvaryāṇām aiśvarya pracyuti darśanāt loke samatvasya tu anapapattiḥ eva yugapad ekaḥ ced sarva adhipatiḥ sarvasya praśāsitā paraḥ kim kurvan  īśaḥ syātḷ virodhāt ca na khalu eṣām ekam ati tve hetuḥ asti tatra ekasmin vastuni viruddha abhiprāyayoḥ eka abhiprāya anuvidhāyi tve tasya itarasya anīśvara tvam ubhaya anuprāya anuvidhānam na virodhāt ubhayoḥ ananuvidhāne anīśvara tvam ubhayoḥ kārya asiddhaḥ ceda ekamatye hetuḥ pariṣadvat anyathā tasya āsiddheḥ iti ced pratyekam anīśvara tvam atha paryāyeṇa aiśvaryam avirodhāya ucyate antavat tā jagat sargasya ca asaṃbhavāt na brahma tulyam aiśvaryam yatas paraḥ eva jagat sarge śrūyate tad upāsanena sarga uttara kālaḥ apavargaḥ iti tasmāt sphaṭikasya iva rāga ādi apakarṣaṇena svarūpa āvirbhāvaḥ brahma prāptiḥ brahma rūpa tvāt vijñāna ātmanaḥ tathā ca param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate aiti uktam anya rūpa niṣpattau sva śabda anupapatteḥ niṣpadyamānasya abhedāt saṃbandhāt vopapattiḥ iti ced na viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyāt sarvasya tasya niṣpadyamānasya sva tvāt  tatra yathā mala apagame śuklam eva sat vastram śuklam jātam aiti ucyate tathā moha āvaraṇa vigame svarūpa āvirbhāve ‘svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti ucyate tathā brahma eva san brahmā apyetia iti tad evam sva rūpa sthiti lakṣaṇa tvāt mohasya na kārya tā prāk api svarūpasya bhāvāt āgantukasya asva rūpa tvāt na ca anya tvam yatas avidyā apagamaḥ eva uktena prakāreṇa muktiḥ avidyā saṃsāraḥ vidyā eva ca avidyā nivṛttiḥ yadi agrahaṇam avidyā yatas bhāvaḥ eva abhāva vyāvṛttiḥ atha viparyāsaḥ tathā api virodhita tattva jñāna udayaḥ eva tad nivṛttiḥ na hi śuktikā jñāna utpādāt anyā rajata jñāna nivṛttiḥ tad sādhyā prayatna antara sādhyāḥ vā tayoḥ yaugapadyāt prayatna antara anapekṣaṇāt ca tathā ca vidyā brahma prāptyoḥ tulya kālatā śrūyate brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati iti tathā ‘a ānandam brahmaṇaḥ vidvān na bibheti ‘tadā ātmānam eva avedaham brahma asmi iti tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat tatra kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śoka eka tvam anupaśyataḥ veda bhavati vidvān na bibheti kaḥ mohaḥ paśyate iti paurvāparya aśravaṇāt yad tu kvacid paurvāparyam tad vyādāya svapiti aiti yathā nanu eka tve tulya kāla tāpi anupapannāḥ na ekasya api vastunaḥ bhāva abhāva rūpeṇa vyapadeśāt tathā yadā ghaṭaḥ naśyati tadā kapālāni jāyante iti katham tarhi mārga avibhāga sarga apyayā aiśvarya śrutayaḥḷ tatra āhuḥ na mārgaśrutayaḥ nirupādhi viśuddha brahma vidyā viṣayāḥ yatra hi sarva upādhi viśuddham asthūla ādikam brahma upāsyam tatra brahma eva san brahma api eti ‘na tasmāt prāṇāḥ utkrāmanti atra eva samavanīyante iti prāṇān utkramaṇena vijñāna ātmanaḥ eva āgatiḥ ucyate na hi tad agamane tad upādheḥ tasya brahmaṇaḥ bhedena vijñāna ātma tvam yatra tu manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ bhā rūpaḥ iti sa upādhi upāsyam tad viṣayāḥ tāḥ yatra etad śrūyate araḥ ca ha vai ṇyaḥ ca arṇavau brahma loke tṛtīyasya amitas divi tadaiḥ aṃmadīyam saraḥ tad aśvatthaḥ soma savanaḥ tad aparājitā pūrbrahmaṇaḥ prabhu vimitam hiraṇmayam veśma iti tathā ca abrahma vidām api tad gati śravaṇam ye ca amī araṇye śraddhām satyam tapaḥ iti upāsate iti para brahma prāptiḥ tu na abrahma vidām yujyate vidyayā tad ā ārohanti yatra kāmāḥ parāgatāḥ na tatra dakṣiṇāḥ yānti na avidvāṃsaḥ tapasvinaḥa iti tathā tam eva viditvā ati mṛtyum etia iti vacanāt apunarāvṛtti śrutiḥ tarhi kathamḷ atra kecid manyate krama mukti āśrayaṇāt tad prāpya tatra utpanna nirupādhi tattva jñānāḥ param padam aśnuvate yathā uktam vedānta vijñāna su niścita arthāḥ saṃnyāsa yogāt yatayaḥ śuddha sattvāḥ te brahma lokeṣu para anta kāle para amṛtāḥ parimucyanti sarve brahma lokeṣu iti kārya brahma loka nirdeśaḥ bahuvacanāt tatra avayava dvāreṇa bahu tva upapatteḥ para anta kālaḥ mahāpralayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sva adhikāra paryavasānam tasmin para amṛtāḥ para brahma rūpeṇa amṛtāḥ santaḥ saṃnyāsa yogāt bhedena parameśvare sva kṛtānām karmaṇām phalānām ca saṃnyāsāt yogāt ca sarvam idam kartṛ ādi brahma iti upāsanāt tathā ca smṛtiḥ brahmaṇā saha te sarve saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare parasya ante kṛtātmānaḥ praviśanti param padam anye tu manyate yathā candra loke yāvat saṃpātam uṣitvā sthitaḥ eva tasmin bhukta bhogāḥ āvartante na evam sthitaḥ eva brahma loke tatas āvṛttiḥ kim tu tad pralaya paryavasānā tatra sthitiḥ tad pralaye hi na tatas āvṛttaḥ bhavati tatas ca anāvṛttiḥ śrūyate tathā ca imam mānavam āvartam na āvartante iti ‘imam ḷ im edition iha aiti viśeṣaṇam ‘amṛta tvam eti aiti amṛta tvam āpekṣikam yathā amṛtā devāḥa iti tathā ca paurāṇika smaraṇam ābhūtasaṃplavam sthānam amṛta tvam hi bhāṣyate iti yad tu manyate sarva gata tve api brahmaṇaḥ vikṛta avikṛta bhedaḥ tatas ca deśa bhedaḥ tathā ca avikṛtasya brahmaṇaḥ  deśa bhedaḥ śrūyate atha yad atas paraḥ divaḥ jyotiḥ dīpyate iti atas avikṛtasya niyata deśasya brahmaṇaḥ prāptaye yujyate mārga viśeṣaḥ tad saṃpradhāryam na tāvat anutpannā dvaya viśuddha vidyasya ayam mārgaḥ brahma vidaḥ śravaṇāt na api vidyāvataḥ vidyā udaye nikhila bheda ucchedāt iti madhunadī nidarśana avibhāga śrutiḥ api viveka jñāna abhāva parā na tu tadvidhaḥ eva avibhāgaḥ sarga śrutayaḥ api na sarga parāḥ kim tarhiḷ eka ātma tattva pratipatti pradhānāḥ tatas tad anuguṇa tayā eva tāsām artha vyavasthānam na tu tad virodhena tathā hi kasmin nu bhagavaḥ vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavatiḷ sat eva somya idam agre āsīt ekam eva advitīyam iti eka tvena upakramāt  ‘a etad ātmyam idam sarvam tad satyam saḥ ātmā tattvam asi aiti upasaṃhārāt eka tvena eva aikātmya tattva pratipatti param ekam idam vākyam gamyate tatra yadi aparaḥ tejaḥ prabhṛti tattva sargaḥ satyatayā vidhīyeta vākya bhedaḥ syāt atas yathā upāṃśu yāja vākye ajāmi tva upakrama upasaṃhāre viṣṇuḥ upāṃśu yaṣṭavyaḥ aitya ādīni vacāṃsi vākya bheda doṣāt pṛthagvidhi tvam alabhamānāni tādarthyāt tad ānukūlyena stuti artha tayā vyavatiṣṭhante tathā sarga śrutayaḥ api ekatva upāya tayā na ca viparītam śakyam vaktum ekatva śrutiḥ eva bheda pratipatti artha iti sarvatra eka tvena upakramāt upasaṃhārāt ca yena upakramyate yena ca upasaṃhriyate sa vākya arthaḥ bheda pratipatteḥ ca aphala tvāt eka tva pratipatteḥ tu dṛṣṭam śrutam ca phalam śoka ādi nivṛttaḥ viśuddha aikātmya darśanena tad avagamāt tatra kaḥ mohaḥ kaḥ śokaḥ eka tvam anupaśyataḥ iti śravaṇāt phalavat aṅga tā ca aphalasya upāya tvam ca na ca idam jagat asat mūlam kim tarhiḷ advitīya ekasat mūlam kāraṇa avyatirekāt ca kāryasya sat ekam eva idam ghaṭa ādi vat mṛd rūpeṇa hi ghaṭa ādayaḥ na eka tvam atikrāmanti nanu evam mukhyaḥ eva kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ uktaḥ syāt na etad ekatva avatāra upāya mātra tvāt na khalu atra kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva pratipādyaḥ yena asau yathāśabdam mukhyaḥ eva gṛhyeta ekatva upāyattvāt iti uktam eka tvam ca anena upāyena avatāryate puruṣaḥ sa ca mukhyaḥ pradhāna virodhī ekam eva advitīyam aiti punar punar śruteḥ sarva bheda nirāsa paratvāt na śakyam vaktum kāraṇa ātmanā ekatvam kārya ātmanā nānātvam tad satyam saḥ ātmā iti ca kāraṇasya eva satya tva avadhāraṇāt anyatra ca indraḥ māyābhiḥa iti bhedasya māyā gamya tva śruteḥ sākṣāt ca bheda abhāvasya śravaṇāt na iha nānā asti kiñcana iti bheda abhedayoḥ ca virodhāt prāc anupapatteḥ varṇita tvāt tad avirodhena varṇyate tad upādāna mātra tayā bheda vikalpasya bimba pratibimba vat varṇa pada vākya ādi vat ca yathā hi na bimbāt pratibimbānām utpattiḥ nānā rūpāṇām bimba upādāna mātra tayā pratibimba bheda vikalpasya na hi bimbāt para sparataḥ vā vyāvṛttāni kānicid vastūni pratibimbāni bimba upādānam tu tad nānā nirbhāsa mātram tathā na varṇebhyaḥ pada vākya prakaraṇa ādīni kānicid vastūni santi tad upādāna mātra tvāt tad kalpanāyāḥ varṇebhyaḥ padāni niṣpadyante padebhyaḥ vākyam iti ucyate api ca svapne api sṛṣṭiḥ śrūyate na tatra rathāḥ na ratha yogāḥ na panthānaḥ bhavanti atha rathān ratha yogān pathaḥ sṛjate aiti tadvat eṣā syāt anya paratvāt svayam eva vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ nāmadheyam iti vikāra asatya tayā na pāramārthikī iti uktam aiśvarya śrutiṣu api sva guṇa vidyā vipākaḥ ayam śrūyate saḥ ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati ‘sarvān  ca kāmān āpnoti ‘sa svarāj bhavati iti na tu mokṣaḥ sa hi nirupādhi brahma vidyā nimitta eva yad api kvacid apunarāvṛtti śravaṇam tasya api dvayī gatiḥ vyākhyātā iti ekam darśanam anye tu manyante āvirbhūta brahma rūpaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sarva ātma tvāt sarva īśitṛ tvāt ca sarva upabhogānām ca bhoktṛ tvāt tad ānanda mātrā rūpa tvāt deva ādi ānandānām sa sarvān  ca lokān āpnoti sarvān  ca kāmān ‘sa svarāj bhavati aiti tasya tad saṃkīrtanam brahma rūpa āvirbhāva lakṣaṇa mokṣa praśaṃsā artham nanu sarva ātma tvena sarva kāma avāptau sarva śoka moha ādi āptiḥ api syāt na teṣām abrahma rūpa tvāt avidyā adhyasta tvāt jñāna aiśvarya ānanda bhogāḥ tu brahmaṇaḥ rūpam vijñānam ānandam brahma ‘na anyaḥ atas asti draṣṭā ‘etasya eva ānandasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvanti ‘sarvasya īśānaḥ ‘etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi aiti ādi śrutibhyaḥ tathā ca yad kiñcid īśvara tvam yad ca vijñānam yaḥ ca ānandaḥ brahma ādiṣu sthāvara anteṣu bhūteṣu brahmaṇi tāni tāni āvirbhūta brahma svarūpaḥ samaśnutaḥ iti yuktam loka ādayaḥ tu avidyā adhyaḥ tāḥ na brahma rūpam te katham āvirbhūta brahma svarūpam āskandeyuḥḷ nanu prapañca śūnyasya advaitasya brahma rūpasya jñeya abhāvāt īśita vyābhāvāt ca vijñānam aiśvaryam ca anupapannam tatra sarvajñaḥ ‘sarveśvaraḥa iti api śrutī samādheye eva na etad sāram yatas  na īśitavya kṛtam īśvara tvam jñeya kṛtam vā jñātṛ tvam kim tu siddhena jñāna rūpeṇa siddhayā ca īśana śaktyā jñeyam avāpnoti īśitavyam ca viniyuṅkte praśāsti ca prakāśa dāha vat siddhena hi prakāśa rūpeṇa prakāśyam prakāśayati vivasvān na tu prakāśya adhīnam tasya prakāśa rūpam dāhya adhīnā vā agneḥ dāha śaktiḥ tathā ca tad caitanyena eva kṛtsnasya prapañcasya avabhāsanāt tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti ‘na anyaḥ atas asti draṣṭā aitya ādi śruteḥ sarvajña tvam sarveśvara tvam api tad aiśvaryeṇa yathāyatham īśvaraiḥ īśitavyānām īśanāt  evam ca eṣa bhūta adhipatiḥ ‘eṣa lokapālaḥ aiti brahma indra yama ādīnām ca aiśvaryam uktam sarva kāma avāptiḥ ca tadīya tvāt deva ādi ānandasya kāmeṣu ānanda prāptyā kāmāḥ āptāḥ bhavanti na sva rūpeṇa evam sa tatra paryeti jakṣan krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ strībhiḥ vā iti varṇanīyam tad viṣaya ānanda bhogāt na tu strī ādi yogaḥ yathā ātma ratiḥ ātma krīḍaḥ ātma mithunaḥ iti na hi mukhyam ātma krīḍa tvam ātma mithuna tvam vā saṃbhavati yatas ca anavacchinnāni tadīyāni eva sarva bhūteṣu jñāna ādīni kalpita avacchedāni atas yatra yatra na atyantam avacchedaḥ samutkarṣāt teṣām tāni tāni pratyāsatteḥ bhūtāni ātma tvena bhagavān uktvā munīnām api aham vyāsaḥ aityādi upasaṃjahāra yad yat vibhūtimat sattvam iti tathā adṛṣṭam draṣṭṛ aśrutam śrotṛ aityādi sarva bhūta darśana ādīnām tad caitanya nibandhana tvāt anye tu āhuḥ yāvān kaścid parasminnāma rūpa āśrayaḥ vyapadeśaḥ sarvaḥ asau  ādhyānāya yathā yaḥ asau  āditye puruṣaḥ ‘hiraṇya śmaśruḥa ityādi na hi sva mahima pratiṣṭhasya parasya deśa viśeṣa avarodhaḥ sarva viśeṣa atigasya ca rūpa viśeṣa yogaḥ paraḥ ca eṣaḥ sarva pāpma udaya śruteḥ uditaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhyaḥ iti ādhyānam tu tathā vidhīyate tathā sarvajña tvāt api draṣṭavyam iti tad evam brahma ātmanaḥ tad rūpa āvirbhāvaḥ tad prāptiḥ sa mokṣaḥ sā ca vidyā eva tasmāt na sādhyaḥ mokṣaḥ na ca vidyayā anyaḥ iti puṣkalam atha matam mā bhūt mokṣaḥ sādhyaḥ bandha hetu kṣayaḥ tu sādhyate tad sādhanam ātma darśanam syāt śrūyate ca tasya phalam bandha hetūnām karmaṇām kṣayaḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare tathā tad yathā iṣīkātūlam agnau protam pradūyeta evam ha asya sarve pāpmānaḥ pradūyante ‘pāpma śabdena puṇyam api saṃgṛhītam sāvadya phala tvāt anyatra ca na etam setum ahorātre tarataḥ na jarā na mṛtyuḥ na śokaḥ na sukṛtam na duṣkṛtam iti upakramya ‘sarve pāpmānaḥ atas nivartante aiti upasaṃhārāt na ca tad kṣayam antareṇa kṣema prāptiḥ atas avaśya kartavyaḥ na ca adatta phalasya karmaṇaḥ na kṣayaḥ prāyaścittānām doṣa saṃyogena codyamānānām tad kṣaya phala tvāt tasmāt prāyaścittaiḥ iva vidyayā bandha hetu kṣayaḥ sādhyate sā eva ca muktiḥ bandhana viśleṣa artha tvāt muceḥ evam ca na antava tu doṣaḥ pradhvaṃsasya kāryasya api avināśāt tatra ucyate bandha hetu dhvaṃsaḥ api na ātma darśana sādhyaḥ tad hi vidadhadeva nikhila avidyā vyavahāra pravilayam udīyate karma phala bhoga vibhāgaḥ ca avidyā upādānaḥ tatra anavayavena unmūlitāyām avidyāyām na cchettavyam asti avidyādhyastāni hi karmāṇi tad samucchede vidyayā samucchinnāni eva bhavanti tad vipākasya avakāśaḥ eva na asti advaitam ātma tattvam paśyataḥ bheda darśana āśraya tvāt tasya yatas ca avidyā ucchedena eva karma ucchedaḥ atas tulya vat saṃśaya viparyāsābhyām prasaṃkhyātāni karmāṇi bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare nanu evam karma kṣayāmi upagame tattva darśana samanantaram eva muktiḥ syāt na dehapāta pratīkṣā tasya tāvat eva ciram yāvat na vimokṣe atha saṃpatsye iti deha pāta pratīkṣā śrutiḥ bādhyeta yasya tu vidyā tad kṣaya sādhanam śāstrāt gamyate tasya tad anusāreṇa keṣāñcid kṣayaḥ vidyayā keṣāñcid upabhogena tatra kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi aiti aviśeṣāt sarva kṣaya prasaṅge ‘tasya tāvat eva ciram iti deha pāta  adhi śravaṇāt mukteḥ ārabdha kāryāṇām pravṛtta bhogānām na tatas kṣayaḥ bhogena eva kṣayaḥ iti gamyate na hi sarva kṣaye dehapāta pratīkṣā upapadyate tad uktam anārabdha kārye eva tu pūrve tad avadheḥ ‘bhogena tu itare kṣapayitvā saṃpadyate iti vidyayā tu avidyā uccheda karma vipāka vyavahāra ucchittau  aviśeṣāt sarva ucchedaḥ iti sapadyeva mucyeta na eva doṣaḥ na hi iyam śrutiḥ cira kālatā viśiṣṭam dehapāta vadhim mukteḥ āha kim tu kṣipra tām yathā kaścid kṣepīyaḥ tam pratipādayan bravīti kvacid kārye etāvat me ciram yad snātaḥ bhuñjānasya ca evam iyam api anyathā tāvat eva aiti na vācyam syāt ciram iti eva brūyāt tāvat eva aiti tu vacanāt kṣaiprya para tā gamyate atas kṣiprā eva muktiḥ na pratīkṣaṇīyam asti dehapāta pratīkṣā tu tatra na antarīyaka tvāt bhavati eva atha vā cira tvam anūdya dehapāta avadhi tvam atra ucyate anyathā cira tve avadhi viśeṣe ca ucyamāne vākyam bhidyeta tatra ayam arthaḥ yadi kasyacid ciram tāvat eva yāvat na vimokṣye iti nanu pūrvasmin pakṣe tattva jñāna anantara tvāt dehapātasya sthita prajña lakṣaṇa abhidhānam na yujyate sthita prajñasya kā bhāṣāa ityādi dvitīyaḥ api sarva kṣaye cira tva anupapatteḥ tatra avadhi viśeṣa vidhāna ayogāt anupapannaḥ ucyate sthita prajñaḥ tāvat na vigalita nikhila avidyaḥ siddhaḥ kim tu sādhakaḥ eva avasthā viśeṣam prāptaḥ syāt na ca brūmaḥ brahma vedanā anantaraḥ eva deha viyogaḥ kim tu ārabdha kārya karma kṣayam bhogena pratīkṣate iti tatra kasyacid tad kālaḥ apavargaḥ kasyacid kiyān  citkṣepaḥ yathā rajjvām sarpa samāropa samuttha bhaya janmānaḥ vepathu prabhṛtayaḥ tattva darśanāt apāvṛte bhaye kasyacid tadā eva nivartante kasyacid kiyantañcitkālam anuvartante tad saṃskārāt tathā sarva karma kṣaye api bhujyamāna vipāka saṃskāra anuvṛtti nibandhanā śarīra sthitiḥ kulāla vyāpāra vigamaḥ iva cakra bhrāntiḥ nanu evam brahma vidaḥ api ced bhokra ādi vibhāga darśanam anuvartate deha pātāt uttara kālam api anuvarteta tatra viduṣaḥ api na avaśyaṃbhāvi kaivalyam syāt tathā ca tāvat eva ciram iti śrutyā virodhaḥ atha ucchedāt avidyāyāḥ na anuvṛttiḥ kṣaṇam api na syāt iti saḥ eva virodhaḥ sā eṣā ubhayataḥpāśāḥ rajjuḥ ucyate yathā bhaya vigame labdha āśvāsasya api saṃskāra mātrāt kampā ādi anuvṛttiḥ na ca bhaya vigame api anuvṛttiḥ iti etāvatā cira kālā bhavati na ca mūla kāraṇa tulya phalaḥ saṃskāraḥ na ca sthāyī anyathā kampa ādīnām nivṛttiḥ eva na syāt na ca bhaya vigama hetoḥ tattva darśanāt tad nivṛttaye hetu antaram apekṣate tatas eva hi sa krameṇa nivartate svayam eva vā kulāla cakra bhrānti saṃskāra vat tathā nivṛttāyām avidyāyām karmasu ca aviśeṣeṇa ārabdha kāryeṣu anārabdha kāryeṣu ca nivṛtteṣu ārabdha vipāka saṃskārāt śarīriṇam bhoktāram iva ca ayam ātmānam pratyetya ābhāsa mātreṇa vidvān api na tu avidvān iva ārūḍha abhiniveśaḥ sa ca ayam īdṛśaḥ sthita prajñaḥ varṇitaḥ vīta kāmaḥ ātma rūpa saṃtuṣṭaḥ duḥkheṣu cchāyā mātra rūpeṣu tattva darśanāt abhiniveśāt kṛtrimebhyaḥ iva vyāghra ādibhyaḥ anudvigna manāḥ sukheṣu ca kṛtrima ramaṇīyeṣu iva vigata spṛhaḥ yathā khalva viduṣaḥ mṛd dāru racite strī ādau viṣaye chāyā mātra darśanam abhiniveśa vikalam tathā viduṣaḥ kṣīṇa karma avidyasya tad saṃskāra mātrāt darśanam chāyā mātreṇa eva viṣayeṣu tathā ca tad yathā ahi nirlvayanī valmīke mṛtā pratyastā śayīta evam eva idam śarīram aiti viduṣaḥ śarīre anāsthām darśayati yatas na mūla kāraṇa tulya phalaḥ saṃskāraḥ kampa ādi vat eva na ca cira kāla anuvṛttiḥ alpa kāla sthāyi tvāt saṃskārasya tadvat eva ca na tad nivṛttaye hetu antaram apekṣyate tattva darśanāt eva krameṇa tasya api nivṛtteḥ svayam eva vā sā ca iyam avasthā jīvanmuktiḥ iti gīyate ārabdha kārya karma saṃskāra kṣayaḥ ca dehapātāt eva gamyate tad anuvṛttau dehapāta eva na syāt iti na dehapāta uttara kāle tad vipākasya chāyā mātreṇa api darśanam śakyate yena hi karmaṇā yad śarīram ārabdham tatra eva tad vipāka śeṣa ābhāsaḥ anārabdha kāryāṇām tu alabdha vṛttīnām eva nivṛtta tvāt na asti tad saṃskāraḥ labdha vṛtti kāraṇa saṃskārāt hi kārya leśa anuvṛttiḥ na khalu bhaye apratilabdha vṛttau  anupajanita kampa ādau tad saṃskārāt kampa ādi anuvṛttiḥ tasmāt anārabdha kāryāṇām anālabdha vṛtti tvāt ārabdha kārya saṃskāra kṣayasya ca deha pātāt avagamāt viduṣaḥ patite asmin śarīre kaivalyam avaśyaṃbhāvi atra ca labdha vṛtti kāraṇa saṃskārāt vā kārya śeṣaḥ kārya saṃskārāt eva vā tathā ubhaya saṃskārāt eva vā kampa ādi anuvṛttiḥ bhaya saṃskārāt vā bhayam tatas kampa ādayaḥ kampa ādi saṃskārāt vā kampa ādi anuvṛttiḥ sarvathā bhavati kāraṇa vigame api kārya śeṣa anuvṛttiḥ saṃskārāt atas labdha vṛtti karma saṃskārāt tad vipākāt vā viduṣaḥ api śarīra sthitiḥ tad uktam tantra antare api tiṣṭhati saṃskāra vaśāt cakra bhrama vat dhṛta śarīraḥ iti ye tu manyante pravṛtta bhogānām karmaṇām pravṛtta vegasya iṣoḥ iva cakrasya iva vā na śakyaḥ pratibandhaḥ atas bhogena kṣaya pratīkṣā iti tad asat śakyaḥ hi iṣuḥ pratibandhum kuḍya ādibhiḥ nāśayitum ca ccheda ādibhiḥ svapna ādi sūcita upasthita vipāka vartamāna deha bhogya karma kṣaya arthāni ca śāntikāni karmāṇi tasmāt saṃskārāt eva sthitiḥ nanu saṃskāra kāryaśeṣau  avidyā eva tatra katham sarva avidyā pravilayaḥ katham vā na cchedyam avaśiṣyateḷ ucyate viśuddha aikātmya darśana pratipakṣa grastau vilīnau  eva tāvat uditau akiñcitkara tvāt abandha tvāt tad nivṛttaye hetu antarasya anapekṣaṇāt  viśuddham khalvātmānam sākṣāt anubhavataḥ vipāka ābhāsaḥ tamaspṛśan  akiñcitkaraḥ bandha ātmā pralīnaḥ eva yathā citra ādau citra ādi tattvam anubhavataḥ strī ādi ābhāsaḥ rāga ādīnām animitta tvāt tathā avadātam ātmānam jānataḥ viparītam vā khaḍga ādiṣu śyāma ādi ābhāsa utpannaḥ api tattva darśanāt avakāśam alabhamānaḥ pravilīnaḥ eva tathā ca na tad nibandhanena malina tvena śocati ātmānam na tejasvitayā abhinandati avabhāsamānayoḥ api tayoḥ ātmani tattva darśana pratihata avabhāsa tvāt evam ca yad ucyate karmaṇaḥ vā śarīra sthitiḥ syāt saṃskārāt vā kaḥ viśeṣaḥḷ kaḥ ca karmaṇaḥ kṣayaḥ kārya anuvṛttauḷ tad nivṛttyā hi tad kṣayaḥ gamyate tasmāt bhogena tu itare kṣapayitvā saṃpadyate iti eva yuktam tad api apāstam karma vipākaḥ hi ātma saṃsparśī śoka abhinandana vān aviduṣaḥ viduṣaḥ tu tad asaṃsparśāt ābhāsa mātram maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa ādi nibandhana viśeṣa vat na vipākaḥ anabhinandyamāna tvāt at viṣyamāṇa tvāt ca tathā ca tad tat prāpya śubha aśubham na abhinandati na dveṣṭi iti darśitam tathā yasyām jāgrati bhūtāni sā niśā paśyataḥ muneḥ paśyate eva śarīra ādi prapañcaḥ niśā tad asaṃsparśāt adṛśyamāna sama tvāt nanu tattva jñāna pratihataḥ ced utpannaḥ api prapañca avabhāsaḥ na ātma saṃsparśī na kiñcitkaraḥ na bandhaḥ śabdāt eva tasya utpatteḥ kim artham upāsana ādiḷ ucyate parokṣa rūpam śābda jñānam pratyakṣa rūpaḥ prapañca avabhāsaḥ tena tayoḥ avirodhena prapañca avabhāsaḥ na ātma asaṃsparśī na akiñcitkaraḥ na na bandhaḥ yathā pramāṇa antarāt avasīyamāna mādhurye api dravye pratyakṣa sarūpaḥ indriya dvāraḥ tiktā avabhāsaḥ adravya saṃsparśī na ābhāsa mātra tayā avatiṣṭhate tathā ca tad dravyam parama artha tiktam iva anavasita mādhuryam iva duḥkhāya bhavati upāsana ādinā sākṣātkṛtātma tattvasya tu virodhāt san  api prapañca avabhāsaḥ na ātma saṃsparśī devadattaḥ iva siṃha avabhāsaḥ siṃhaḥ devadattaḥ iti samārope avabhāsamānaḥ api tad asaṃsparśī akiñcitkaraḥ na bhaya hetuḥ nityaḥ ca ātma tattva prakāśaḥ tatra na punar vipayarya avakāśaḥ asti śābdam tu pramāṇa adhīnam kṣaṇikam jñānam tatra punar api viparyaya avakāśaḥ dṛṣṭam hi pramāṇa an anusandhāne punar sarpa bhrāntyā rajjoḥ bhayam atha atra api satatam śābdam jñānam anusaṃdadhīta kim anyat upāsanam asmātḷ tasmāt bandha hetu  chedaḥ api vidyā eva na tayā sādhyaḥ evam uttara agha āśleṣe api vācyam yathā puṣkara palāśaḥ āpaḥ na śliṣyante evam evaṃvidi pāpam karma na śliṣyate aiti kartṛ karma pravibhāgasya vidyayā pravilayāt evam na vidyāyāḥ aneka phala kalpanā bhaviṣyati vartamāna apadeśānām ca phala vidhi tvena na vipariṇatiḥ iti yad uktam na śābda jñāna viṣayaḥ brahma iti tatra ucyate na khalu jñāna mātram vidhīyate jñāna viśeṣa vastu na ca aprasiddhe anirūpite tatra niyogaḥ na hi aprasiddhe viṣaye niyoktum śakyate jñānasya ca viśeṣaḥ artha dvāraḥ na ca aprasiddhaḥ  arthaḥ tad viśeṣa nirūpaṇāya prabhuḥ na ca ātma rūpasya śabdāt anyatas siddhiḥ śabdāt api ced na siddhiḥ tad dvāra jñāna viśeṣa asiddhau viṣaya anupapatteḥ niyoga anupapattiḥ api ca jñāna viśeṣa vidhi vādinaḥ ātma tattve prāmāṇyam eva hīyate iti darśayati yadi tāvat niyogasya eva kārya tā pratīyeta tadā sa sva niṣpattau paryavasitaḥ saha śabdena atha viniyogāt viṣaye kartavyatā avagamaḥ tathā api viṣaya siddhau ubhayathā na vastu tattvam saṃspṛśati tatra advaita ātma tattva pratipattiḥ apramāṇikā syāt syāt etad ya ātma apahata pāpmā vijaraḥa iti padānām sāmānādhikaraṇyena sambandhāt anyathā vā vastu tattva pratipattiḥ iti tad ca na anya paratvāt sā hi naḥ evam idam aiti paryavasitā kim tu ‘evam idam pratipattavyam aiti kartavyatā niṣṭhā na vastu tattve pramāṇam vṛttānteṣu iva artha vāda uttha jñānam anya paratvāt na ca ātma tattvam eva vidheḥ viṣayaḥ tasya anuṣṭheya viṣaya tvāt kriyāyāḥ ca tathā abhāvāt siddha vatsva śabda upādāne ananuṣṭheye dravye vyāpāra ayogāt pratyuta avidheya kāla traya anyatama saṃspṛṣṭa satta anugamena dravya svarūpa siddhiḥ īdṛśam vastu abhūt asti bhaviṣyati vā iti tasmāt svarūpa siddhau duṣyati na hi vidheyasya kāla traye api sattā avagamaḥ na hi yajeta aiti ukte yāgasya bhūtakālā vartamāna kālā bhaviṣyat kālā vā sattā pratīyate nanu bhaviṣyat kāla avagamyate bhaviṣyat kāla viṣaya tvāt vidheḥ na etad na hi vihitam niyogataḥ anuṣṭhāsyate vihita akaraṇa doṣa abhāva prasaṃgāt nanu viśiṣṭa kriyā abhidhānam viśeṣaṇe api pramāṇam iṣyate yathā somena yajeta tathā aṅgadī kuṇḍalī vyūḍha uraskaḥ devadattasya putraḥ  adhīte aiti adhyayana kriyā vat sarvaḥ viśeṣaṇa kalāpaḥ pratīyate satyam viśiṣṭa kriyā pramāṇam viśeṣaṇe api pramāṇam anyatra pratipatteḥ pratipattiḥ hi viṣaya viṣeśa viśiṣṭā pramīyamāṇāḥ na viṣaya viśeṣasya sadbhāvam gamayati anyathā bhūte tathā ābhāsa samāropeṇa api saṃbhavāt asau vāva lokaḥ gautama agniḥ aiti yathā dyu prabhṛtiṣu anagni dṛṣṭeḥ atra āha na khalu anyat anyathā pratīyate iti yuktam pratīti virodhāt katham anyasmin pratibhāsamāne anyaḥ viṣayaḥḷ anāśvāsāt ca viṣaya rūpa vyabhicāriṇi jñāne na tatas viṣaya niścayaḥ syāt  api ca viṣaya rūpam ananukurvat aviṣayam anālambanam jñānam agrāhyam eva syāt jñāna hetu mātrasya anālambana tvāt cakṣuḥ ādi vat tathā ca āvedaka tvāt na anya apekṣāt api tatas artha siddhiḥ kim tarhi idam śukti saṃnikṛṣṭe cakṣuṣi rajatam itiḷ smṛtiḥ sāmānya grahaṇāt bhrāntiḥ tarhi kathamḷ pratyakṣa smaryamāṇayoḥ viveka agrahaṇāt saḥ ayam bheda agrahaṇe abheda grahaṇa abhimānaḥ viveka rahitānām yathā dūrāt antarāla agrahaṇe vṛkṣa ādiṣu saṃśleṣa grahaṇa abhimānaḥ tasmāt smarāmi aiti viveka śūnyā rajata smṛtiḥ eṣā atra ucyate yadi cakṣuṣā saṃprayuktam śukti śakalam na rajatam iti pratīyāt rajatam vā tathā na śuktikā śakalaḥ āditsayā pravarteta rajata arthī tasya ‘rajatam iti anavagateḥ loṣṭa ādi vat na ca smaryamāṇe rajate sā pravṛttiḥ tad deśa asaṃnidheḥ na hi pratītim upagate api vastuni yatra tasya asaṃnidhiḥ tatra tena arthī pravartate syāt etad rajatasya pratīteḥ asaṃnidheḥ ca apratīteḥ tatra pravṛttiḥ tad na śuktikā śakalaḥ eva pravṛtteḥ tatra eva tu pravṛttiḥ tad saṃnidhi nibandhanā rajata mātra pratīteḥ smṛti viveka śūnya tvāt ca pravṛttiḥ anyatra api syāt  asaṃnidhāna agrahaṇasya tatra api aviśeṣāt atha matam anya deśeṣu vastuṣu sa viśeṣa pratyakṣa avagateṣu rajatāt viveka grahaṇāt apravṛttiḥ śuktikā śakale tu rajata sādhāraṇa śukla bhāsvara rūpa mātra pratīteḥ viśeṣāt pratyayāt ca smṛti viparivartinaḥ  rajatāt viveka grahaṇāt pravṛttiḥ evam api adṛṣṭeṣu loka ādiṣu tatas anya tā anavadhāraṇāt pravṛttiḥ syāt atha na teṣu rajata avagamaḥ itaratra api na bhāve vā viparītā khyātiḥ abhyupagatā syāt atha adṛṣṭa tvāt eva adṛṣṭeṣu na pravartate śuktau  api na pravarteta nanu yad tu tathā rajata rūpam na tena avagamaḥ sa yathā cakṣuṣā saṃprayuktasya na asti tathā saṃprayuktāyāḥ api śukteḥ yadi manyeta dṛśyamāna smaryamāṇa yoga vivekāt cakṣuḥ saṃprayuktaḥ eva pravartate na itarasmin tatra api idam vicāryam viveka grahaṇasya viveka kṛtaḥ  abhāvāt saṃnidhi pratīteḥ abheda bodhaḥ tatas vā pravṛttiḥ bheda avabodha abhāva mātrāt vāḷ pūrvasmin viparyayaḥ uttarasmin dṛśyamānādṛśyamānayoḥ saṃprayuktā saṃprayuktayoḥ vā na viśeṣaḥ bheda agrahaṇasya tulya tvāt na hi indriya saṃyogasya darśanasya vā kaścid agrahaḥ upayogaḥ abhūta samārope tu asti na kathañcid agṛhīte asaṃprayukte vā aindriyakaḥ samāropaḥ upapadyate api ca idam tatra bhavān vyācaṣṭām smaryamāṇam dṛśyamānāt sva jñānāt eva vivicyate na vā smṛti jñānasya svarūpam eva tādṛśam yad pramātavyāt bhedena avabhāsayati sva rūpa mātra niṣṭham vā tatra pūrvasmin smaraṇa gocarayoḥ avivekaḥ kutas sva jñānāt eva vivikta tvāt ḷ itarasmin  api sadā smṛtau viparyayaḥ syāt sāmānya darśane ca anya smṛtau  avivekāt na ca tad tathā saṃśayasya api darśanāt atha matam eka smṛtau viparyayaḥ tatas avivekāt aneka smṛtau tu saṃśayaḥ na ekasmāt avivekāt tad asat aneka smaraṇe api hi dṛśyate viparyayaḥ yadi ca pratyakṣe arthe viśeṣa jñānāt smaryamāṇam vivicyate na sva jñānāt asati tatra viśeṣa jñāne ca dvayoḥ smṛtau saṃśayaḥ eva syāt  na eka avabhāsaḥ viparyayaḥ atha tu sva jñānāt smṛtam vivicyate smṛti viparyaya bhedaḥ ca abhyupagamyate tadā aneka smaraṇe api indriya doṣa viśeṣāt i uktaḥ viparyayaḥ darśitam ca idam sāmānya darśane api kadācid ekām koṭim smarataḥ na saṃśayaḥ na viparyayaḥ doṣāṇām apuṣṭeḥ atas sva jñānāt eva tadā smṛtam vivicyate na dṛśya viśeṣa paricchedāt evam ced kutas dṛśyamāna smaryamāṇā vivekaḥḷ api ca anyat eva smarataḥ pūrvarūpam eka tvam śaśini dvi tva vibhramaḥ na smaryamāṇā viveka jaḥ na ca jñāna indriya vṛtti bheda avivekāt tayoḥ apratyakṣa tvāt smaryamāṇa tvāt ca śuktikā hita cetasaḥ ca salilam pipāsataḥ na syāt viparyayaḥ salila ābhāsaḥ vā smaryamāṇasya sva jñāna vivekāt yadi ca sadṛśa darśanāt sadṛśa smṛteḥ bhramaḥ katham śvete pīta bhramaḥ madhure vā tikta bhrāntiḥḷ āntara pitta saṃvedane avyāpārayataḥ api bahis indriyam syāt añjana vat ca akṣi gatasya tad gata kṛṣṇim ādi vat ca adṛśya tvāt kiñcid sādṛśye sarva prakāra bhrama prasaṃgaḥ tasmāt indriya doṣa sāmarthya bhedāt niyatā viparyaya utpattiḥ agraha mātre tu doṣa vyāpāre kāmila ādi doṣāt bhrānti niyamaḥ na syāt na hi sādṛśya nimittaḥ asadṛśe api bhrānti darśanāt atha matam sva jñānāt eva smṛtam vivicyate kadācid tu tatra pratyakṣaḥ iva viśeṣa āgrahaḥ tataḥ avivekaḥ sataḥ tu viśeṣa grahaṇaḥ indriya saṃyukte sāmānya darśane api na avivekaḥ tata ubhaya koṭi smaraṇe na saṃśayaḥ eka smṛtau na saṃśayaḥ na viparyayaḥ evam api dvayoḥ smaraṇe na viparyayaḥ syāt na ca smṛtau viśeṣa grahaṇam viśeṣa smaraṇāt atha deśa kāla viśeṣāt smaryamāṇam vivicyate tatra deśa kāla bheda āgrahaḥ iti tad na ananta deśa kāla bheda avagatam tad deśa avagatam ca dṛśyāt smaryamāṇam viviktam gamyate na ca deśa kāla bheda grahaṇāt ananta smaraṇa anupapatteḥ tad deśa avagate ca deśa bheda abhāvāt atha smaryamāṇa tayā agrahaṇāt avivekaḥ smaryamāṇa tā jñānāt ca vivekaḥ tasmāt smarāmi iti jñāna śūnyāni rajata ādi jñānāni bhrānti hetavaḥ paripūrṇā eva tarhi smṛtiḥ na tayā sva viṣayasya kiñcid na gṛhītam svayam eva sā sva viṣayam dṛśyāt vivinakti iti na asti dṛśyamāna smaryamāṇayoḥ avivekaḥ yatas smarāmi iti jñānam anyat eva darśana smaraṇa viveka kāri smṛteḥ tatra idam vicāryam smṛtiḥ sva viṣayam vivinakti vā na vāḷ yadi vivinakti tadā viparyaya abhāvaḥ atha na smṛtiḥ sva viṣayam vivinakti tadā sāmānya darśane ca anya smṛtau viparyayaḥ syāt iti uktam na smarāmi aiti vivekāt ced saḥ eva smṛteḥ svayam avivecaka tvena syāt kārya gamyasya hi jñānasya bhedaḥ kārya viśeṣa unneyaḥ na ced smṛteḥ pramāṇa kāryāt kāryam viviktam syāt kena sā viviktā gamyetaḷ sati api smṛti viveke dṛṣṭaḥ pratyabhijñā bhramaḥ saḥ eva iti na ca pratyakṣasya āvivekaḥ eka vivekena ubhayoḥ vikārāt smṛtāt avivekāt ca smṛti vibhramaḥ syāt na pratyakṣa bhramaḥ tasmāt na smarāmi aiti pramoṣāt avivekaḥ atha asaṃnihitasya saṃnihita ātmanā pratītiḥ avivekaḥ smṛteḥ viparīta artha tva prasaṃgaḥ atha asaṃnidhya grahaṇāt bhavatu sa svapna jñāne natu indriya jāyām bhrāntau manasaḥ anupaghātāt upaghāta hetu tvāt ca agrahaṇasya na ca ittham pravṛtti niyamaḥ syāt iti uktam sati ca vastu grahe kasyacid aṃśasya agrahāt bhrāntau sarva jñāna bhrama tvam na hi kasyacid jñānasya sarva ātmanā vastu viṣayaḥ iti sati api ca viveka jñāne pramāṇa antarāt dvi candra diś moha ādi anugatiḥ dṛṣṭā iti na agrahaṇa mātram viparyayaḥ na idam rajatam aiti prasakta pratiṣedha rūpā pratītiḥ na agrahaṇe avakalpate prasaṅga abhāvāt na khalva grahaṇam kasyacid prasañjakam abhāvaḥ hi saḥ viparītā tu khyātiḥ saṃnihitasya rajata tām abhūtām rajatasya vā saṃnihita tām ādarśayantī prasañjayati nanu ca rajata nayana ghaṭita vastunoḥ khyātī staḥ te eva prasañjike satyam na tu tad upanītayoḥ iyam niṣedha avagatiḥ na hi na idam rajatam aiti rajata mātram cakṣuḥ saṃyukta vastu mātram vā nirasyamānam avasyāmaḥ kim tu cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya tu rajata tām rajatasya vā cakṣu saṃyuktām na ca etayoḥ agrahaṇam prāpakam agrahaṇa tvāt eva tasmāt avaśyam pratiṣedhya prāptaye viparīta khyātiḥ upāsanīyā na ca na idam aitya grahaṇam eva vāryate sarva jñāneṣu tādrūpya prasaṃgāt sarva jñānānām agraha bādhena utpattau ca viveka jñāna mātram idam na prasakta pratiṣedha rūpam iti prati iti anusāriṇaḥ  anurūpam na hi rajata śukti kāśa kalayoḥ yugapad viviktayoḥ grahaṇe īdṛśī pratītiḥ na krameṇa aviviktayoḥ grahaṇaḥ īdṛśī syāt iti ced  yuktāḥ viviktayoḥ grahaṇe aviveka pratiṣedha rūpa tvāt viviktayoḥ grahaṇe prāpti abhāva yuktāḥ api ca bhavati kadācid yaḥ smarati ca rajatasya cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya vastunaḥ sāmānya mātra darśī na rajatāt vivekam gṛhṇāti punar cakṣuḥ prasādāt pratyeti na ca tadā tathā pratītiḥ aviveka grahaṇa abhāvāt nanu sāmānya darśane na ced viparyayaḥ saṃśayaḥ syāt tad apanodi ca nirṇaya jñānam īdṛśam eva na etad sāram na hi asati koṭi dvaya smaraṇe sāmānya darśane api saṃśayaḥ na ca viparyayaḥ bhavati hi puras avasthite bhāsvara rūpa mātra pratītiḥ rajate ca smṛtiḥ na ca tayoḥ anya tvam pratipadyate na ekatvam ca tatra na viveka jñānam evaṃrūpam ekatva apratipatteḥ atha matam viveka agrahaṇāt kāla saṃnidhi pratīteḥ ca rajatam vā cakṣuḥ saṃprayukta vat avabhāsate cakṣuḥ saṃyuktam vā rajata vat atas prāptiḥ iti pratiṣedha upapattiḥ abhyupetā tarhi viparīta khyātiḥ na hi anyā sā atada ātmanaḥ tathā avabhāsanāt kāmam tattva ajñāna nimittā syāt na hi sā tattva jñāne sati udeti virodhāt iti tatra api saṃnidhi khyātiḥ eva nibandhanam tasyāḥ tu viveka grahaḥ apavādaḥ agrahaṇe nirapavādā sā eva kāraṇam na abhāvaḥ viparīta khyāti anabhyugame ca agrahaṇa nibandhanaḥ bhramaḥ iti agrahaṇam agrahaṇa nibandhanam iti su vyāhṛtam svapne ca dvitīya abhāvāt kutas avivekaḥ smṛta tvena aviviktasya tathā viveke dharmiṇi pratipanne dharma antara pratipanne dharma antara pratipatteḥ bādhaka tvam pūrvasyāḥ ca bhrānti tvam syātām iti aidam śuklam rajatam aiti sāmānādhikaraṇyena pratīteḥ ātma upālambhaḥ parasmin  āsajyate pratīti virodhaḥ jñāna bheda kalpanāyāḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt yaḥ hi jñāyamāne arthe anyathā api syāt iti anāśvāsaḥ tasya tena eva jñānena tathā tva paricchedinā utpattiḥ nirudhyate tathā hi anāśvāsa nivṛttaye tadvidham jñānam eva apekṣyate tad ca asti eva na ca vyabhicāra doṣāt asamartha pramāṇam jñānam iti yujyate pramāṇa kāryasya paricchedasya jñāna rūpāt eva siddha tvāt paricchedataḥ hi prāmāṇyam atantra tā tu vyabhicāra avi abhicārayoḥ asati tasmin dhūma ādeḥ avyabhicārasya api apramāṇa tvāt vyabhicāravataḥ api ca sita asita ādiṣu cakṣuṣaḥ sati tasmin prāmāṇyāt na ca vyabhicāraḥ  bādha hetuḥ doṣa vat prāmāṇya upaghātī kvacid dṛṣṭaḥ cakṣuḥ ādau vyabhicāravati pramāṇa tvāt nanu dṛṣṭaḥ vyabhicāraḥ prāmāṇya upaghātī prameya tva ūrdhva tva ādau na etad sāram na tatra vyabhicārāt aprāmāṇyam api tu pariccheda kārya abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ ca hetu abhāvāt  avyabhicārāt hi liṅgāt liṅgi paricchedaḥ yatra tu avyabhicāraḥ na kāraṇam tatra vyabhicāre api sati paricchede prāmāṇyam avivādam akṣeṣu tadvat eva ca jñānam pariccheda nimittam na liṅga vat na ca saṃśaya utpattyā vyabhicāraḥ prāmāṇyam upahanti samyak paricchinne dvaividhi asya asaṃśaya hetu tvāt na niścite sthāṇau  ūrdhva tvena saṃśerate utpattyā eva jñānam artham avadhārayati anavadhārakam tu na eva iha adhikṛtam evam ca avadhāraṇā deva anavadhāraṇam iti vipratiṣiddham yaḥ eva tu avyabhicāram arthayate jñānasya āśvāsa artham tasya eva anāśvāsaḥ avyabhicāra jñāne api anāśvāsāt na hi tad asiddha vyabhicāram ātmani jñāna antareṣu ca āśvāsa kāraṇam jñāna antarāt siddhau  anavasthāḥ api ca jñāna rūpāt ced na artha āśvāsaḥ tasya asiddhau kena saha avyabhicāraḥ jñānasya gṛhya itaḷ kim ca jñāna rūpāt eva avyabhicāraḥ api kathyate viparīta khyātau tad virodhāt tathā sati tad eva viṣayasya sādhakam vyarthaḥ avyabhicāraḥ na ca vyabhicāraḥ prāmāṇyam upahanti iti uktam viveka upāyaḥ ca doṣa abhāva bhāvau grahaṇa agrahaṇayoḥ na daṇḍa vāritau viparyaye viparyaya hetavaḥ  abhyupaghātakāḥ sutarām iṣṭa kārya uparodhāt viparīta udayāt ca na ca aduṣṭeṣu api indriya ādiṣu agraha āśaṅkā nivṛttiḥ yatas hetu bhāve api na niyogataḥ kāryam viparyayaḥ ca syāt pratyakṣā saṃvittiḥ hetunā anumīyeta phalāt tu hetoḥ hetu bhāva anumānam doṣa abhāvāt tu viparyaya kārya asattvam yukta anumānam hetu abhāve kārya anutpādāt ālambana tvahānam ca yathā ākāra antara avabhāse cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya tathāgrahaṇe api sva rūpa ānarpaṇasya tulya tvāt atha kasyacid sāmānya rūpasya su ākāra tvāt atha kānicid cakṣuḥ saṃyuktāni vastūni svena rūpeṇa gṛhyante iti kasyacid agrahaṇe api nānā ālambana tvam tulyam ākāra antara avabhāse api keṣāñcid sva ākārāṇām avabhāsanāt atha agrahaṇe na eva cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya ālambana tvam iṣyate paraḥ api na eva viparyayaḥ icchati evam hi uktam atasmāt yad anyathā santam anyathā pratipadyate tad nirālambanam jñānam abhāva ālambanam ca tad atha viparyaye cakṣuḥ saṃyuktasya ālambana tvāt anyatra api anālambana tā śaṅkā agrahaṇe api tulyā yathā khalu viparyaya jñāne cakṣuḥ saṃprayukta vastu svabhāva nirapekṣa tā dṛṣṭā samyak jñāne api śaṅkyate jñāna tva sāmānyāt tathā cakṣuḥ saṃprayuktam api vastu na avikala rūpam gṛhyate tena anālambanam bhavati sadṛśa smṛti hetu tām ca pratipadyate iti agrahaṇe dṛṣṭa anālambana tā grahaṇeṣu api kasmāt na śaṅkyateḷ doṣa abhāvāt iti ced viparyaye api tulyam na ca anyathā ālambane nirālambana tvam cakṣuḥ tu anyathā api na ālambyate ālambana arthaḥ ca rajata vyavahāra yogya tā śukteḥ tathā hi rajata arthī tām ādatte ghaṭasya api hi na eva anyat sva jñāna ālambana tvam anyatra vyavahāra yogya tāyāḥ yatas na viṣaya ākāram jñānam tatra śuktiḥ sva rūpeṇa na ālambitāḥ rajata jñānena tad nibandhana vyavahāra bhāvāt rajata rūpeṇa tu tad nibandhanasya upādāna vyavahārasya tatra bhāvāt iti kriyā niṣṭhe api vidhau vastu svarūpa siddhaye kaścid āha yathā avaghāta prokṣaṇa ādayaḥ sva rūpeṇa eva dravya arthāḥ dvitīyayā ca dravyasya karma tvena nirdeśāt tathā jñānam api svarūpeṇa para artham karma tvena ca ātmanaḥ nirdeśāt tad artham atas jñāna viṣayaḥ api vidhiḥ ātma rūpam saṃspṛśati na jñāna mātre paryavasyati jñānasya ātma rūpa artha tvena kartavyatā avagamāt jñāna niyogena eva ātma rūpasya ākṣepāt  syāt etad bhavatu jñānasya ātma arthatā abhipretāḥ apahata pāpma ādi rūpa ātma pratītau tu pramāṇam vācyam śabdaḥ tāvat evaṃvidha ātma jñāna kartavyatāyām paryavasitaḥ evaṃvidhātma uddeśena jñānam kuryāt na tu ‘evaṃvidhaḥ ātmā iti tatra ucyate na hi tatra akiñcitkarasya tādarthyena kartavyatā yujyate jñānasya ca karmaṇi na anyat phalam tad rūpa saṃvitteḥ na hi tasyām dṛṣṭāyām anyasya adṛṣṭasya kalpanā tatra yathā vrīhīn prokṣati aiti prokṣaṇa vidheḥ eva vrīhiṣu adṛṣṭa saṃskāra avagamaḥ prokṣaṇa viṣayāt api na anyathā vrīhi arthe prokṣaṇe kartavyatā yujyate na hi tatra kiñcid akurvat prokṣaṇam tad artham kṛtam syāt iti evam vidheḥ eva adṛṣṭa saṃskāra sadbhāva siddhiḥ yathā svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti na anyathā svarga kāmasya yāga kartavya tā pratītiḥ yujyate yadi na svarga upāyaḥ yāgaḥ anupāye ced niyujyate na svarga kāmaḥ niyuktaḥ bhavati anuṣṭhitaḥ api na svarga kāmena anuṣṭhitaḥ bhavati iti kriyā viṣayāt api vidheḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva avagamaḥ śābdaḥ tathā jñāna viṣayāt api vidheḥ ātma rūpa bodhaḥ na hi tadvidham ātmānam uddiśya jñāna niyogaḥ yujyate atadvidhaḥ ced ātmā tena jñānena pratīyate iti ātma artha jñāna vidheḥ etāvat gamyate jñānena saḥ avabhāsyate ālambyate vyavahāra yogya tām āpadyate tad ca avabhāsanam sva rūpeṇa ca dṛṣṭam para rūpeṇa ca rajata ātmanā śuktikāyāḥ pratipāditam etad na agraha mātram etad anyathā khyātiḥ tu tatra ubhayathā saṃbhave kutas etad  tattva pratipattiḥ avaśya abhyupeyāḥ na atasmin  tad khyātiḥḷ anyathā na ātma jñāna vidhiḥ phalavān syāt sa khalu ana ātma rūpa pravilaya arthaḥ anātma rūpa vilayena hi vastunaḥ avagatiḥ dṛṣṭā iti yadi ca na ātmanaḥ nāma rūpa prapañca rūpeṇa prakāśanam kim pravilāpya itaḷ atha matam dvi prakārā iyam avidyā prakāśasya acchādikā vikṣepikā ca svapna jāgaritayoḥ vikṣepikā suṣuptaḥ ācchādikā laya lakṣaṇā tatra ācchādaka avidyā nivṛttiḥ jñāna vidheḥ phalam tad ca asat yatas na acchādikāyāḥ avidyāyāḥ nivṛttiḥ puruṣeṇa arthyate tathā yathā vikṣepasya sa hi vividha duḥkha ātmakaḥ layaḥ tu vividha duḥkha nivṛtteḥ asakṛt ānanda tvena śrutau gītaḥ pratyuta arthanīyaḥ syāt api ca viparyāsam anicchataḥ avidyā bhedaḥ eva na syāt avasthā traye api agrahaṇa mātra tvāt tasmāt agrahaṇa viparyaya grahaṇe dve avidye kārya kāraṇa bhāvena avasthite svapna jāgaritayoḥ ubhe kāraṇa bhūta agrahaṇa lakṣaṇā suṣuptaḥ iti avidyā pravibhāgaḥ upapadyate tad uktam kārya kāraṇa baddhau tāviṣyete viśva taijasau prājñaḥ kāraṇa baddhaḥ tu dvau tu turye na sidhyataḥ nanu anyathā ayam bhedaḥ agrahaṇa samyak grahaṇābhyām agrahaṇa lakṣaṇa ācchādikā suṣupte asamyak grahaṇam itarayoḥ tathā hi abhinnasya vastunaḥ apradeśasya grahaṇe tathā abhāvasya ca agrahaṇāt pṛthaktvena pratyavabhāsaḥ na etad sāram yadi tāvat asamyak grahaṇa mātram tad apaṭu tvam vā jñānasya kenacid drūpeṇa vā grahaṇam na sarva ātmanā tatra dūra sthe sūkṣme ca bhavati apaṭu jñānam sāmānya jñānam na ca tad avidyā na ca kiñcid jñānam sarva ātmanā arthasya grāhakam iti sarva jñāna mithyātva āpātaḥ abhedasya agrahaṇe api bhedasya āvartane api bhedasya asaṃvitteḥ na nivartanīyam asti vidyayā na khalva bheda agrahaṇam nivartanīyam na hi tad kiñcid aparādhyati bhedaḥ tu vividha duḥkha āyatanam atha asamyak grahaṇam pṛthak pratyavabhāsaḥ apṛthak ātmanaḥ abhyupetā tarhi viparyaya khyātiḥ apṛthak pṛthak prakāśate iti atha ucyeta na brūmaḥ pṛthak prakāśate kim tu pṛthak iva prakāśate iti kaḥ iva arthaḥḷ yadi yathā pṛthak bhūtam aprakāśamāna ekatvam prakāśate tathā ekam api ātma tattvam agṛhyamāṇā eka tvam prakāśate iti kenacid aṃśena grahaṇam sarva ātmanā ca agrahaṇam uktam bhavati tatra ca uktam atha prakāśataḥ iva na tu prakāśate prakāśane kaḥ upamā arthaḥḷ tad nibandhana vyavahāra pravṛttiḥ tad nibandhanaḥ ced vyavahāraḥ prāptam prakāśanam na asati kāraṇe kāryam bhavati iti atha abheda āgrahaḥ eva pṛthaktva c raha abhimānaḥ tad asat agrahaṇasya abhāvasya sva rūpeṇa para rūpeṇa vā grahaṇa anabhyupagamāt aprakāśamāne ca pṛthaktve kutas tad avagrahaḥḷ abhinne ca bheda abhimānam parityajya abheda agrahaṇe bheda graha abhimānam ūrīkurvatā kim parihṛtam syātḷ tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate laya vikṣepa bhedaḥ ca na syāt agraha mātrake iti nanu anātma rūpeṇa pratipatteḥ na dṛśyate kiñcit phalam tatra adṛṣṭa kalpanā syāt ātma rūpa pratipatteḥ tu dṛṣṭam phalam tad svarūpa siddhiḥ ucyate na yasya kasyacid darśanāt dṛṣṭa artha tā kim tu puruṣa artha saṃsparśinaḥ tena hi tad vidhiḥ nirākāṅkṣā bhavati na ca puruṣa arrha bhedaḥ tattva atattva pratipattyoḥ yathā hi viśuddham advaitam ātmānam pratipadyamānaḥ tathābhūtaḥ na śokena saṃspṛśyate śocanīya abhāvāt na karma āśayam upacinoti kartavyā abhāvāt na kvacid drajyati kiñcid dveṣṭi vā viṣaya abhāvāt evam jīvan  eva vidvān vimuktaḥ bhavati tathā atathābhūtam api tathā bhāvanā puraḥsaram sākṣāt iva pratipadyamānaḥ abhūtaḥ api arthaḥ paribhāvanā atiśayāt bhūta vyavahāra hetuḥ bhavati idam eva ca atra yujyate pratyakṣa ādīnām avirodhāt karma vidhīnām ca bhūta artha tvāt parama arthe hi prapañca śūnya tve pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni bādhyeran karma vidhayaḥ ca ābhūta kalpanā upādāna vyavahāra siddhārtha gocarāḥ syuḥ tasmāt aparama arthena eva advaita ātma jñāna vidhiḥ yujyate yadi matam sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ iti jānātiḥ tattva paricchedaḥ eva vartate tena na abhūta samāropeṇa jñāna vidhiḥ syāt iti tad na mithyātva ādibhiḥ jñānam viśeṣyate mithyājñānam samyak jñānam saṃśaya jñānam iti tad eka niyame na upapadyeta paunaruktyāt virodhāt ca syāt etad asvarūpeṇa pratipattau na tad ātma jñānam anya jñānam eva bhavati tattva jñānam ca vidhīyate tasmāt tattva siddhiḥ iti tad ca na na khalu etāvat eva tad ātmā jñātavyaḥ iti yadi syāt tad rūpa jñāna vidhiḥ tad ca na ubhayathā anupapatteḥ pramāṇa antara siddham ced ātma rūpam na tad jñānam vidheyam atha asiddham aśakyam eva tad syāt etad  apahata pāpmā vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ ‘idam sarvam yad ayam ātmā aiti śabda samarpita rūpasya tasya jñānam vidhīyate tena ca tattvena api tad saṃbhavati samāropitena api tena na niyogataḥ tathābhūta jñāna vidheḥ tathā abhāvaḥ asya pratīyate yadi ca jñānasya dṛṣṭam phalam tata eva pravṛtti siddhe vyarthaḥ vidhiḥ yaḥ hi ātma rūpam anubhavitu kāmaḥ sa tasya jñāne svayam eva yatate yaḥ tu na tathā tasya tad vyartham iti vidhi śatena api sa na pravartyate atha upāya ajñānāt dṛṣṭa phale api na pravartate svayam atas vidhīyate iti tad ca vārtam yatas saḥ eva upāyaḥ vidhīyatām yatra ayam ajñānāt na pravṛttaḥ jñāne tu dṛṣṭa phala tvāt pravartate eva syāt etad avaghāta ādiṣu dṛṣṭa phaleṣu api dṛṣṭaḥ vidhiḥ satyam na tu adṛṣṭa saṃsparśa rahitaḥ tatra api hi niyama adṛṣṭam phalam taṇḍuleṣu tad praṇāḍyā vā pradhāna pūrva siddhiḥ adṛṣṭā eva atha matam advaita ātma jñānam adṛṣṭa pūrvam alaukikam atas anantara phalam api vidhīyate iti tatra ucyate kimartham vidhīyate pramāṇa antara agocarasya svarūpa pratipatti artham āhosvit anuṣṭhāna arthamḷ tatra na svarūpa siddhi artham anuṣṭhāna phalaḥ hi vidhiḥ na anuṣṭhānāya dṛṣṭa artha tvāt eva tad siddheḥ tasmāt alaukike apahata pāpma ādi rūpaḥ ātma tattve śabdāt pratipanne tasya sākṣāt jñānam prati tad anubhava upāya tvāt svayam eva puruṣasya abhimukhyam bhavati iti vyartham tad vidhānam yathā āścarya bhūte kasmiṃścid arthe āgamāt pratipanne tasya sākṣātkaraṇe svayam eva unmukha tvam bhavati tad upāyeṣu tu ajñāteṣu upāya tva jñāpanāya vidhānam yujyate tad evam jñāne niyoga anupapatteḥ niyoge ca vastu rūpa avagame prāmāṇya ayogāt vyavasthita ātma tattva pratipattim icchatā śabdān na tasya niyoga anupraveśaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ iti idānīm dvitīya pratipatti vidhi nirāsāya āha yad api matam sa kratum kurvīta aprajñām kurvīta ‘nididhya asitavyaḥ iti yatra api svarūpa niṣṭhatā eva lakṣyate ‘tattvam asi iti tatra api ‘sat asmi iti cetaḥ dhārayet aiti vivakṣita tvāt śravaṇāt anyat anucintanam dhyānam pratyaya pravāhaḥ vidhīyate karma vat eva amṛta tva phalam tad api atas eva na yujyate pūrva uktāt tattva avagati pramāṇa abhāva prasaṅgāt anya niṣṭha tvāt vākyasya atha tu vākya antarāt tattva niṣṭhāt adhigate tad viṣaya pratyaya pravāha vidhānam iṣyate bhavatu na kaścid doṣaḥ tathā ca vijñāya prajñām kurvīta aiti ātma tattva vijñānasya siddha tām darśayati tad api vā vyartham eva prāpta artha tvāt sākṣātkaraṇa phalam hi tad tad anucintanam dṛṣṭa artham na tatas anyat phalam ākāṅkṣyate amṛta tvam hi na svarūpa āvirbhāvāt anyat iti prāk varṇitam dṛṣṭā ca jñāna abhyāsasya samyak jñāna prasāda hetu tāḥ loke bhāvanā viśeṣāt hi abhūtam api anubhavam āpadyate kim punar bhūtam sa kratum kurvīta iti tu na sakala viśeṣa atigātma tattva anucintanam vidhīyate tad bhāva phalam api tu nāma rūpa upādhi manaḥ maya prāṇa śarīra ādi rūpa anudhyānam aiśvarya phalam krameṇa vā sākṣātkaraṇa phalam tam eva dhīraḥ  vijñāya iti na prajñā karaṇa vidhiḥ tam eva aiti anya nivṛtteḥ śrutattvāt nivṛttau tātparyam gamyate ‘raktaḥ paṭaḥ bhavati aiti tayā rakta para tvam vākyasya atra ākāśa ādi tattva bheda pūrvam avibhāgaḥ pratipāditaḥ tatra tathā eva prajñā karaṇa prasaṅge tam eva iti vidhīyate tathā ca pūrva ardhe virajaḥ paraḥ ākāśāt ajaḥ ātmā mahān dhruvaḥ iti ākāśa ādibhyaḥ paratvena ātma tattvam darśitam tasya tathā eva prajñā karaṇa prasaṅge tad nivṛttaye tam eva iti ucyate anyathā naḥ eva śabdasya phalam na ca nivartyam vijñāyeta tathā ca tad eva uttareṇa prapañcyate na anudhyāyāt bahūn śabdān iti eka vākyatā anyathā vākyam bhidyeta śabda mātre ca anudhyāna aprasaṅgāt  śabda pūrvat tvāt tasya śabda artha viṣayam eva idam iti evam ātmā iti eva upāsīta aiti evakāra śruteḥ tad artha vidhiḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti api ‘a ātmanaḥ tu kāmāya iti upakramāt ‘idam sarvam yad ayam ātmā aiti upasaṃhārāt ātma svarūpa param ekam vākyam tad antargatāḥ draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti na pṛthagvidhayaḥ kṛtya pratyaya yoge api kṛtya pratyayasya artha antare api smaraṇāt arha ādau stuti arthāḥ yathā upāṃśu yāja vākya antargatāḥ viṣṇuḥ upāṃśu yaṣṭavyaḥ aiti evamādayaḥ aitat ātmyam idam sarvam tad satyam saḥ ātmā tad tvam asi aiti bhūta eva paryavasitam vākyam tatra sat asmi iti dhārayet iti kalpanā iyam tasmāt trividhasya api jñānasya vidheya tva ayogāt vinā ca vidheḥ vākya artha pratipatteḥ apauruṣeya tvena nirapekṣa tvāt bhūte api arthe vedāntānām prāmāṇya siddhiḥ tathā ca tad tu samanvayāt aiti codanā lakṣaṇāt dharmāt tu śabdena viśeṣyam brahma samanvaya gamyam uktam samanvayaḥ hi padārthānām saṃsargaḥ viniyogaḥ tatas brahma gamyate na ca udanātaḥ iti arthaḥ nanu aviśeṣeṇa kārye arthe vedasya prāmāṇyam varṇitam codanā lakṣaṇaḥ arthaḥ dharmaḥa iti codanā lakṣaṇaḥ veda arthaḥ iti arthaḥ na etad sāram evam hi siddha prāmāṇya veda artha vicāraḥ ayam syāt tad uttara lakṣaṇa vat tatra anantaram prāmāṇya pratipādanam na yujyeta vṛttam pramāṇa lakṣaṇam iti ca mantra artha vādeṣu ca kārya artha tvena vipratipattiḥ na syāt sā ca upariṣṭāt eva nirasiṣyate bahu ca atra vaktavyam iti alam prasaṅgena iti niyoga kāṇḍaḥ tṛtīyaḥ caturthaḥ siddhi kāṇḍaḥ evam tāvat pratipatti kartavya tā prāmāṇya vyājena yaiḥ aprāmāṇyam uktam tad pratibodhanāya kṛtaḥ prayatnaḥ idānīm tu aprāmāṇyam eva āhuḥ ye tad bodhanāya prayatyate tatra pūrva pakṣaḥ na tāvat brahma antaryāmya ādi padam pramāṇam saṃbandha jñāna apekṣayā pūrva siddhe pratyaya hetu tvena na api vākyam na hi tad sākṣāt vācakam padārtha dvārā tu tad pratipattiḥ apadārthe jñānasya abhāvāt te hi saṃsargāt guṇa pradhāna bhāvena itara padārtha viśiṣṭam ekam padārtham gamayanti tatra padārthaḥ eva viśiṣṭaḥ vākya arthaḥ bhavati na ca anadhigateṣu pramāṇa antareṇa padārtha tvam sambandha jñāna apekṣaṇāt iti uktam tatra āpadārtha tve na vākya viṣaya tvam anavabodhakam teṣām vākyam padārtha tve pramāṇa antara adhigateḥ anuvādakam tatra atyanta aparidṛṣṭa brahma ādi artha pramāṇa abhimateṣu vākyeṣu tad vācīni padāni syuḥ na vā yadi na santi na te itaraiḥ saṃsṛjyeran na bhidyeran  iti na teṣām prameyāḥ loṣṭa ādi vat atha tu santi tathā api taiḥ adhigata saṃbandhaiḥ na pratipādyeran apratipannāḥ ca na viśiṣṭa vākya artha pratipatti hetavaḥ tatra yathā avanāt pikaḥ ānīyatam iti pika padārtha jñāne avabodhaka tvam tathā teṣām api tasmāt na ca udanātaḥ apūrva padārtha avagamaḥ sā hi vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām kriyāsu puruṣam adhikaroti traividhya vṛddha parigrahaḥ tu japa upayogāt upaniṣadaḥ vedāntāḥ iti tatra viniyogāt tatra ucyate yathā loke dvīpa viśeṣe evaṃnāmānaḥ marataka maya pādāḥ padmarāga maya cañcavaḥ sauvarṇa rājata pakṣāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ aiti pakṣi sāmānyam pramāṇa antaradhigatam ananyasādhāraṇena dharma kalāpena saṃsṛjyamānam pramāṇa antara anadhigatam viśeṣa rūpam āsādayati vākyena ca pramīyate pramāṇa antara anadhigatena viśeṣa rūpeṇa sarvasya eva hi vākyasya anadhigataḥ viśeṣaḥ eva prameyaḥ tathā kāraṇa sāmānyam vā sat sāmānyam vā yatas vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante iti ‘a sthūlam anaṇva hrasvam aitya ādi padārthaiḥ saṃsargāt bhedāt ca pramāṇa antara anadhigatam viśeṣa rūpam āsādayati vākyasya ca prameyam bhavati tad evam loka siddha padārtha anvayena eva apūrva artha pratipatteḥ na anavabodhaka tvam anuvādaka tvam vā athavā na loke atyantam aprasiddham brahma sarva pratyaya vedya tvāt brahmaṇaḥ vyatirekeṇa pratyetavyasya abhāvāt viśeṣa pratyayānām ca sāmānya rūpa anugamāt bheda upasaṃhāra avaśiṣṭam ca satyam brahma iti pratipādanāt vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ nāmadheyam mṛttikā iti eva satyam iti dṛṣṭāntāt kim tarhi śabdena pratipādyateḷ prapañca abhāvaḥ tatra prapañca padārthaḥ api siddhaḥ niṣedhaḥ api siddhaḥ tayoḥ saṃsargāt tad abhāva pratipattiḥ āmnāya eka nibandhana tvam tu tasya ucyate pratyakṣa ādīnām avidyā saṃbhinna tvāt pratyastamita nikhila bhedena rūpeṇa aviṣayīkaraṇāt bheda pratyasta mayasya āmnāyau  agamya tvāt iti paraḥ punar pratyavatiṣṭhate yad khalu vākyam na puruṣam kvacid hita sādhane pravartayati ahita sādhanāt ca nivartayati kevalam siddham artham anvācaṣṭe tad apuruṣa artham apuruṣa artha tvāt ca unmatta pralāpa vadapramāṇam tathā ca prāyeṇa vedāntāḥ ucyate upekṣām api hi phalam pramāṇasya pracakṣate anena śloka ardhena atra bhavitavyam iti abhyūhaḥ param tu mātṛkāsu na dṛśyate na tāvat niyogataḥ pramāṇasya puruṣa artha phala tā na khalu hita upāda ana ahita hāne eva pramāṇa phale upekṣām api hi pramāṇa phalam pramāṇa vidaḥ ācakṣate na ca puruṣa artha tā pramāṇa lakṣaṇam pramāhetu tvam tu tasmāt na puruṣa artha abhāvena aprāmāṇyam api ca śokī aham aduḥkhī aham adhana ādīni mama naṣṭāni aiti viśuddha brahma ātmanaḥ  jīvasya mithyājñānam etad nivṛtti rūpam ca viśuddha ānanda prakāśa brahma ātmata tva jñānam tad sva rūpeṇa eva puruṣa arthaḥ aniṣṭa nivṛtti rūpa tva āt iṣṭa āvirbhāvāt ca yadi api ca saṃskārāt tasya anuvṛttiḥ tathā api śābda jñānam anusaṃtanvataḥ viduṣaḥ na pūrvavat bhavati nivartate ca atyantāya dṛṣṭā ca jñāna utpatteḥ eva puruṣa artha tā kvacid kutūhala ākulitānām ajñāte arthe na hi tad jñānāt  param anyadarthyate na ca pravṛtti nivṛtti viṣayasya eva puruṣa artha tā iti niyamaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni hi pramāṇāni na ca tāvat pravṛtti nivṛtti parāṇi siddha vastu viṣayāṇi na ca puruṣa artha tām jahati yadi matam pratyakṣa ādi jñeyam hi siddham vastu puruṣa arthaḥ salila ādiḥ tad upakārāt tatas pratyakṣa ādīnām puruṣa artha tā bhūta niṣṭhānām api atra api ca śabda prameyam svayam eva brahma puruṣa arthaḥ jarā ādi vividha aśiva upaśamāt parama ānanda prakāśa tvāt ca su prasannam atas eva atat tvam asi aiti śvetaketu mukhena āśāsanīyāya puruṣāya śrutyā abhinnam upadiśyate abhinnam hi tad anuśāsanīyāt bhedena ca pratīyamānam na puruṣa arthaḥ tattve tādātmya jñāne ca tathā abhāvāt viśvāśivā upaśamāt parama śiva bhāvāt ca paripūrṇaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ āptaḥ bhavati yadi matam pratyakṣa ādīni api pravṛti aṅgāni eva pramite arthe hāna upādāna ādi lakṣaṇāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ tad mūla tvāt īdṛśam pravṛti aṅga tvam atra api asti eva śabdāt pramite brahmaṇi sākṣātkaraṇāya pravṛtteḥ iṣṭa tvāt iti
